February 07, 2026

Think Proprioceptively: Embodied Visual Reasoning for VLA Manipulation

Abstract (English): Vision-language-action (VLA) models typically inject proprioception only as a late conditioning signal, which prevents robot state from shaping instruction understanding and from influencing which visual tokens are attended throughout the policy. We introduce ThinkProprio, which converts proprioception into a sequence of text tokens in the VLM embedding space and fuses them with the task instruction at the input. This early fusion lets embodied state participate in subsequent visual reasoning and token selection, biasing computation toward action-critical evidence while suppressing redundant visual tokens. In a systematic ablation over proprioception encoding, state entry point, and action-head conditioning, we find that text tokenization is more effective than learned projectors, and that retaining roughly 15% of visual tokens can match the performance of using the full token set. Across CALVIN, LIBERO, and real-world manipulation, ThinkProprio matches or improves over strong baselines while reducing end-to-end inference latency over 50%.

摘要（中文）: 视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型通常仅在后期将本体感受作为条件信号注入，这阻碍了机器人状态影响指令理解以及影响整个策略过程中所关注的视觉标记。我们引入了ThinkProprio，它将本体感受转换为VLM嵌入空间中的文本标记序列，并在输入端将其与任务指令融合。这种早期融合使具身状态能够参与后续的视觉推理和标记选择，从而偏向于对动作至关重要的证据进行计算，同时抑制冗余的视觉标记。通过对本体感受编码、状态入口点和动作头条件化的系统性消融实验，我们发现文本标记化比学习的投影器更有效，并且保留大约15%的视觉标记可以匹配使用完整标记集时的性能。在CALVIN、LIBERO和真实世界操作任务中，ThinkProprio在匹配或改进强大基线性能的同时，将端到端推理延迟降低了50%以上。

TLDR: The paper introduces ThinkProprio, a method that converts robot proprioception into text tokens and fuses them with task instructions early in VLA models. This approach improves performance and reduces inference latency by enabling embodied state to influence visual reasoning and token selection.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了ThinkProprio，一种将机器人本体感受转换为文本标记并将它们与VLA模型中的任务指令早期融合的方法。这种方法通过使具身状态能够影响视觉推理和标记选择，提高了性能并降低了推理延迟。

Authors: Fangyuan Wang, Peng Zhou, Jiaming Qi, Shipeng Lyu, David Navarro-Alarcon, Guodong Guo

DriveWorld-VLA: Unified Latent-Space World Modeling with Vision-Language-Action for Autonomous Driving

Abstract (English): End-to-end (E2E) autonomous driving has recently attracted increasing interest in unifying Vision-Language-Action (VLA) with World Models to enhance decision-making and forward-looking imagination. However, existing methods fail to effectively unify future scene evolution and action planning within a single architecture due to inadequate sharing of latent states, limiting the impact of visual imagination on action decisions. To address this limitation, we propose DriveWorld-VLA, a novel framework that unifies world modeling and planning within a latent space by tightly integrating VLA and world models at the representation level, which enables the VLA planner to benefit directly from holistic scene-evolution modeling and reducing reliance on dense annotated supervision. Additionally, DriveWorld-VLA incorporates the latent states of the world model as core decision-making states for the VLA planner, facilitating the planner to assess how candidate actions impact future scene evolution. By conducting world modeling entirely in the latent space, DriveWorld-VLA supports controllable, action-conditioned imagination at the feature level, avoiding expensive pixel-level rollouts. Extensive open-loop and closed-loop evaluations demonstrate the effectiveness of DriveWorld-VLA, which achieves state-of-the-art performance with 91.3 PDMS on NAVSIMv1, 86.8 EPDMS on NAVSIMv2, and 0.16 3-second average collision rate on nuScenes. Code and models will be released in https://github.com/liulin815/DriveWorld-VLA.git.

摘要（中文）: 端到端(E2E)自动驾驶最近因其将视觉-语言-动作(VLA)与世界模型统一以增强决策能力和前瞻性想象力而备受关注。然而，由于潜在状态共享不足，现有方法未能在一个单一架构内有效统一未来场景演化和动作规划，从而限制了视觉想象对动作决策的影响。为了解决这个局限性，我们提出DriveWorld-VLA，一种新颖的框架，通过在表征层面上紧密集成VLA和世界模型，在潜在空间内统一世界建模和规划，这使得VLA规划器能够直接受益于整体场景演化建模，并减少对密集标注监督的依赖。此外，DriveWorld-VLA将世界模型的潜在状态作为VLA规划器的核心决策状态，从而帮助规划器评估候选动作如何影响未来场景演化。通过完全在潜在空间中进行世界建模，DriveWorld-VLA支持在特征层面的可控的、动作条件下的想象，避免了昂贵的像素级展开。大量的开环和闭环评估证明了DriveWorld-VLA的有效性，它在NAVSIMv1上实现了91.3的PDMS，在NAVSIMv2上实现了86.8的EPDMS，在nuScenes上实现了0.16的3秒平均碰撞率，达到了最先进的性能。代码和模型将在https://github.com/liulin815/DriveWorld-VLA.git上发布。

TLDR: This paper introduces DriveWorld-VLA, a novel framework unifying vision-language-action with world models in a latent space for improved autonomous driving, demonstrating state-of-the-art performance on multiple benchmarks.

简要说明: 本文介绍了 DriveWorld-VLA，一种新的框架，它在潜在空间中统一了视觉-语言-动作和世界模型，以改进自动驾驶，并在多个基准测试中展示了最先进的性能。

Authors: Feiyang jia, Lin Liu, Ziying Song, Caiyan Jia, Hangjun Ye, Xiaoshuai Hao, Long Chen

World-VLA-Loop: Closed-Loop Learning of Video World Model and VLA Policy

Abstract (English): Recent progress in robotic world models has leveraged video diffusion transformers to predict future observations conditioned on historical states and actions. While these models can simulate realistic visual outcomes, they often exhibit poor action-following precision, hindering their utility for downstream robotic learning. In this work, we introduce World-VLA-Loop, a closed-loop framework for the joint refinement of world models and Vision-Language-Action (VLA) policies. We propose a state-aware video world model that functions as a high-fidelity interactive simulator by jointly predicting future observations and reward signals. To enhance reliability, we introduce the SANS dataset, which incorporates near-success trajectories to improve action-outcome alignment within the world model. This framework enables a closed-loop for reinforcement learning (RL) post-training of VLA policies entirely within a virtual environment. Crucially, our approach facilitates a co-evolving cycle: failure rollouts generated by the VLA policy are iteratively fed back to refine the world model precision, which in turn enhances subsequent RL optimization. Evaluations across simulation and real-world tasks demonstrate that our framework significantly boosts VLA performance with minimal physical interaction, establishing a mutually beneficial relationship between world modeling and policy learning for general-purpose robotics. Project page: https://showlab.github.io/World-VLA-Loop/.

摘要（中文）: 机器人世界模型的最新进展利用视频扩散Transformer来预测未来观测，条件是历史状态和动作。 尽管这些模型可以模拟逼真的视觉结果，但它们通常表现出较差的动作执行精度，从而阻碍了它们在下游机器人学习中的应用。 在这项工作中，我们引入了 World-VLA-Loop，这是一个用于联合优化世界模型和视觉-语言-动作 (VLA) 策略的闭环框架。 我们提出了一种状态感知的视频世界模型，它通过联合预测未来的观测和奖励信号来作为一个高保真的交互式模拟器。 为了提高可靠性，我们引入了 SANS 数据集，该数据集结合了近成功轨迹，以改善世界模型中的动作-结果对齐。 该框架实现了VLA策略的强化学习 (RL) 后训练的闭环，完全在虚拟环境中进行。 至关重要的是，我们的方法促进了一个共同进化的循环：VLA策略生成的失败轨迹被迭代地反馈，以提高世界模型的精度，进而增强后续的RL优化。 在仿真和现实世界任务中的评估表明，我们的框架以最少的物理交互显著提高了 VLA 的性能，从而在通用机器人技术的世界建模和策略学习之间建立了一种互利的联系。 项目主页：https://showlab.github.io/World-VLA-Loop/。

TLDR: The paper introduces World-VLA-Loop, a closed-loop framework for joint refinement of video world models and Vision-Language-Action policies using a state-aware video world model and the SANS dataset, demonstrating improved VLA performance with minimal real-world interaction.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了World-VLA-Loop，一种用于联合改进视频世界模型和视觉-语言-动作策略的闭环框架，它使用状态感知的视频世界模型和SANS数据集，并通过最少的真实世界互动，展示了改进的VLA性能。

Authors: Xiaokang Liu, Zechen Bai, Hai Ci, Kevin Yuchen Ma, Mike Zheng Shou

Consensus-based optimization (CBO): Towards Global Optimality in Robotics

Abstract (English): Zero-order optimization has recently received significant attention for designing optimal trajectories and policies for robotic systems. However, most existing methods (e.g., MPPI, CEM, and CMA-ES) are local in nature, as they rely on gradient estimation. In this paper, we introduce consensus-based optimization (CBO) to robotics, which is guaranteed to converge to a global optimum under mild assumptions. We provide theoretical analysis and illustrative examples that give intuition into the fundamental differences between CBO and existing methods. To demonstrate the scalability of CBO for robotics problems, we consider three challenging trajectory optimization scenarios: (1) a long-horizon problem for a simple system, (2) a dynamic balance problem for a highly underactuated system, and (3) a high-dimensional problem with only a terminal cost. Our results show that CBO is able to achieve lower costs with respect to existing methods on all three challenging settings. This opens a new framework to study global trajectory optimization in robotics.

摘要（中文）: 零阶优化最近在设计机器人系统的最优轨迹和策略方面受到了广泛关注。然而，大多数现有方法（例如，MPPI、CEM 和 CMA-ES）本质上都是局部的，因为它们依赖于梯度估计。在本文中，我们将基于共识的优化（CBO）引入机器人领域，该方法在温和的假设下保证收敛到全局最优。我们提供了理论分析和说明性示例，以深入了解 CBO 与现有方法之间的根本区别。为了证明 CBO 在机器人问题中的可扩展性，我们考虑了三个具有挑战性的轨迹优化场景：（1）一个简单系统的长时程问题，（2）一个高度欠驱动系统的动态平衡问题，以及（3）一个仅包含终端代价的高维问题。我们的结果表明，在所有三个具有挑战性的设置中，CBO 都能够实现比现有方法更低的代价。这为研究机器人领域的全局轨迹优化开辟了一个新的框架。

TLDR: This paper introduces Consensus-Based Optimization (CBO) to robotics, claiming global convergence for trajectory optimization problems where existing zero-order methods struggle, demonstrated through challenging robotics scenarios.

简要说明: 本文将基于共识的优化方法（CBO）引入机器人领域，声称该方法能为轨迹优化问题实现全局收敛，解决了现有零阶方法难以解决的问题，并通过具有挑战性的机器人场景进行了演示。

Authors: Xudong Sun, Armand Jordana, Massimo Fornasier, Jalal Etesami, Majid Khadiv

DynaRetarget: Dynamically-Feasible Retargeting using Sampling-Based Trajectory Optimization

Abstract (English): In this paper, we introduce DynaRetarget, a complete pipeline for retargeting human motions to humanoid control policies. The core component of DynaRetarget is a novel Sampling-Based Trajectory Optimization (SBTO) framework that refines imperfect kinematic trajectories into dynamically feasible motions. SBTO incrementally advances the optimization horizon, enabling optimization over the entire trajectory for long-horizon tasks. We validate DynaRetarget by successfully retargeting hundreds of humanoid-object demonstrations and achieving higher success rates than the state of the art. The framework also generalizes across varying object properties, such as mass, size, and geometry, using the same tracking objective. This ability to robustly retarget diverse demonstrations opens the door to generating large-scale synthetic datasets of humanoid loco-manipulation trajectories, addressing a major bottleneck in real-world data collection.

摘要（中文）: 本文介绍了一种完整的运动重定向流程DynaRetarget，用于将人体运动重定向到人形机器人控制策略。DynaRetarget的核心组件是一个新颖的基于采样的轨迹优化(SBTO)框架，该框架将不完美的运动学轨迹细化为动态可行的运动。 SBTO 增量式地推进优化范围，从而能够针对长时程任务对整个轨迹进行优化。我们通过成功地将数百个人形机器人-物体交互演示进行重定向，并实现了比现有技术更高的成功率来验证DynaRetarget的效果。该框架还可以使用相同的跟踪目标，推广应用到不同的物体属性，例如质量，尺寸和几何形状。这种能够稳健地重定向各种演示的能力，为生成大规模人形机器人定位操作轨迹的合成数据集打开了大门，解决了现实世界数据收集中的一个主要瓶颈。

TLDR: The paper introduces DynaRetarget, a pipeline using Sampling-Based Trajectory Optimization (SBTO) to convert kinematic human motions into dynamically feasible humanoid control policies, demonstrating improved success in retargeting and generalization across object properties.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 DynaRetarget，一种利用基于采样的轨迹优化 (SBTO) 的流程，将人类运动学动作转换为动态可行的人形控制策略，展示了在重定向方面的改进成功率和跨对象属性的泛化能力。

Authors: Victor Dhedin, Ilyass Taouil, Shafeef Omar, Dian Yu, Kun Tao, Angela Dai, Majid Khadiv

Zero-Shot UAV Navigation in Forests via Relightable 3D Gaussian Splatting

Abstract (English): UAV navigation in unstructured outdoor environments using passive monocular vision is hindered by the substantial visual domain gap between simulation and reality. While 3D Gaussian Splatting enables photorealistic scene reconstruction from real-world data, existing methods inherently couple static lighting with geometry, severely limiting policy generalization to dynamic real-world illumination. In this paper, we propose a novel end-to-end reinforcement learning framework designed for effective zero-shot transfer to unstructured outdoors. Within a high-fidelity simulation grounded in real-world data, our policy is trained to map raw monocular RGB observations directly to continuous control commands. To overcome photometric limitations, we introduce Relightable 3D Gaussian Splatting, which decomposes scene components to enable explicit, physically grounded editing of environmental lighting within the neural representation. By augmenting training with diverse synthesized lighting conditions ranging from strong directional sunlight to diffuse overcast skies, we compel the policy to learn robust, illumination-invariant visual features. Extensive real-world experiments demonstrate that a lightweight quadrotor achieves robust, collision-free navigation in complex forest environments at speeds up to 10 m/s, exhibiting significant resilience to drastic lighting variations without fine-tuning.

摘要（中文）: 利用被动单目视觉在非结构化户外环境中进行无人机导航，受到仿真与现实之间显著的视觉领域差异阻碍。虽然3D高斯溅射能够通过真实世界数据实现照片级真实感场景重建，但现有方法固有地将静态光照与几何结构耦合在一起，严重限制了策略对动态真实世界光照的泛化能力。在本文中，我们提出了一种新颖的端到端强化学习框架，旨在实现对非结构化户外环境的有效零样本迁移。在一个基于真实世界数据构建的高保真仿真环境中，我们的策略被训练成将原始单目RGB观测直接映射到连续控制指令。为了克服光度限制，我们引入了可重新光照的3D高斯溅射，该方法分解场景组件以支持在神经表示中对环境光照进行显式、基于物理的光照编辑。通过使用从强烈的定向阳光到漫射阴天的各种合成光照条件来扩充训练，我们迫使策略学习鲁棒且光照不变的视觉特征。大量的真实世界实验表明，一个轻量级四旋翼飞行器能够在复杂的森林环境中实现高达10米/秒的速度下的鲁棒、无碰撞导航，并在没有微调的情况下表现出对剧烈光照变化的显著适应能力。

TLDR: This paper introduces Relightable 3D Gaussian Splatting to train a reinforcement learning policy for zero-shot UAV navigation in forests, achieving robust performance under varying lighting conditions without fine-tuning.

简要说明: 本文提出了可重光照3D高斯溅射方法，以训练强化学习策略，用于在森林中进行零样本无人机导航，在各种光照条件下无需微调即可实现稳健的性能。

Authors: Zinan Lv, Yeqian Qian, Chen Sang, Hao Liu, Danping Zou, Ming Yang

LIBERO-X: Robustness Litmus for Vision-Language-Action Models

Abstract (English): Reliable benchmarking is critical for advancing Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models, as it reveals their generalization, robustness, and alignment of perception with language-driven manipulation tasks. However, existing benchmarks often provide limited or misleading assessments due to insufficient evaluation protocols that inadequately capture real-world distribution shifts. This work systematically rethinks VLA benchmarking from both evaluation and data perspectives, introducing LIBERO-X, a benchmark featuring: 1) A hierarchical evaluation protocol with progressive difficulty levels targeting three core capabilities: spatial generalization, object recognition, and task instruction understanding. This design enables fine-grained analysis of performance degradation under increasing environmental and task complexity; 2) A high-diversity training dataset collected via human teleoperation, where each scene supports multiple fine-grained manipulation objectives to bridge the train-evaluation distribution gap. Experiments with representative VLA models reveal significant performance drops under cumulative perturbations, exposing persistent limitations in scene comprehension and instruction grounding. By integrating hierarchical evaluation with diverse training data, LIBERO-X offers a more reliable foundation for assessing and advancing VLA development.

摘要（中文）: 可靠的基准测试对于推进视觉-语言-动作 (VLA) 模型至关重要，因为它能够揭示模型在泛化性、鲁棒性以及感知与语言驱动操作任务对齐方面的能力。然而，由于现有基准测试的评估协议不足以捕捉真实世界中的分布偏移，它们往往提供有限的、甚至具有误导性的评估结果。本研究从评估和数据的角度系统性地重新思考VLA基准测试，并推出LIBERO-X基准，其特点在于：1) 一个具有渐进难度级别的分层评估协议，针对三个核心能力：空间泛化、物体识别和任务指令理解。这种设计能够对在不断增加的环境和任务复杂度下的性能下降进行细粒度分析；2) 一个通过人工遥操作收集的高多样性训练数据集，其中每个场景支持多个细粒度的操作目标，以缩小训练-评估分布的差距。代表性VLA模型的实验表明，在累积扰动下性能显著下降，暴露了模型在场景理解和指令对齐方面的长期局限性。通过整合分层评估与多样化训练数据，LIBERO-X 为评估和推进VLA发展提供了一个更可靠的基础。

TLDR: The paper introduces LIBERO-X, a new benchmark for Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models that features a hierarchical evaluation protocol and a high-diversity training dataset, aiming to provide more reliable assessments in real-world scenarios.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了LIBERO-X，一个用于视觉-语言-动作 (VLA) 模型的新基准，它具有分层评估协议和高多样性的训练数据集，旨在在真实场景中提供更可靠的评估。

Authors: Guodong Wang, Chenkai Zhang, Qingjie Liu, Jinjin Zhang, Jiancheng Cai, Junjie Liu, Xinmin Liu

Beyond the Majority: Long-tail Imitation Learning for Robotic Manipulation

Abstract (English): While generalist robot policies hold significant promise for learning diverse manipulation skills through imitation, their performance is often hindered by the long-tail distribution of training demonstrations. Policies learned on such data, which is heavily skewed towards a few data-rich head tasks, frequently exhibit poor generalization when confronted with the vast number of data-scarce tail tasks. In this work, we conduct a comprehensive analysis of the pervasive long-tail challenge inherent in policy learning. Our analysis begins by demonstrating the inefficacy of conventional long-tail learning strategies (e.g., re-sampling) for improving the policy's performance on tail tasks. We then uncover the underlying mechanism for this failure, revealing that data scarcity on tail tasks directly impairs the policy's spatial reasoning capability. To overcome this, we introduce Approaching-Phase Augmentation (APA), a simple yet effective scheme that transfers knowledge from data-rich head tasks to data-scarce tail tasks without requiring external demonstrations. Extensive experiments in both simulation and real-world manipulation tasks demonstrate the effectiveness of APA. Our code and demos are publicly available at: https://mldxy.github.io/Project-VLA-long-tail/.

摘要（中文）: 通用机器人策略在通过模仿学习多样化操控技能方面前景广阔，但其性能往往受到训练演示数据长尾分布的限制。基于此类数据（高度偏向少数数据丰富的头部任务）学习到的策略，在面对大量数据匮乏的尾部任务时，常常表现出较差的泛化能力。在这项工作中，我们对策略学习中普遍存在的长尾挑战进行了全面分析。我们的分析首先证明了传统的长尾学习策略（例如，重采样）在改善策略在尾部任务上的性能方面的无效性。然后，我们揭示了这种失败的潜在机制，发现尾部任务上的数据稀缺直接损害了策略的空间推理能力。为了克服这个问题，我们引入了接近阶段增强（APA）——一种简单而有效的方案，可以在不需要外部演示的情况下，将知识从数据丰富的头部任务转移到数据匮乏的尾部任务。在模拟和真实世界操控任务中的大量实验证明了APA的有效性。我们的代码和演示可在以下网址公开获取：https://mldxy.github.io/Project-VLA-long-tail/。

TLDR: This paper addresses the long-tail problem in robot imitation learning, showing the ineffectiveness of common techniques and proposing Approaching-Phase Augmentation (APA) to improve performance on data-scarce tail tasks by knowledge transfer from head tasks.

简要说明: 该论文解决了机器人模仿学习中的长尾问题，指出常用技术效果不佳，并提出了逼近阶段增强（APA），通过从头部任务迁移知识来提高数据稀缺尾部任务的性能。

Authors: Junhong Zhu, Ji Zhang, Jingkuan Song, Lianli Gao, Heng Tao Shen

User-Centric Object Navigation: A Benchmark with Integrated User Habits for Personalized Embodied Object Search

Abstract (English): In the evolving field of robotics, the challenge of Object Navigation (ON) in household environments has attracted significant interest. Existing ON benchmarks typically place objects in locations guided by general scene priors, without accounting for the specific placement habits of individual users. This omission limits the adaptability of navigation agents in personalized household environments. To address this, we introduce User-centric Object Navigation (UcON), a new benchmark that incorporates user-specific object placement habits, referred to as user habits. This benchmark requires agents to leverage these user habits for more informed decision-making during navigation. UcON encompasses approximately 22,600 user habits across 489 object categories. UcON is, to our knowledge, the first benchmark that explicitly formalizes and evaluates habit-conditioned object navigation at scale and covers the widest range of target object categories. Additionally, we propose a habit retrieval module to extract and utilize habits related to target objects, enabling agents to infer their likely locations more effectively. Experimental results demonstrate that current SOTA methods exhibit substantial performance degradation under habit-driven object placement, while integrating user habits consistently improves success rates. Code is available at https://github.com/whcpumpkin/User-Centric-Object-Navigation.

摘要（中文）: 在不断发展的机器人领域中，家庭环境中面向对象导航（ON）的挑战引起了广泛关注。现有的ON基准测试通常将对象放置在由通用场景先验知识引导的位置，而没有考虑个体用户的特定放置习惯。这种疏忽限制了导航智能体在个性化家庭环境中的适应性。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了以用户为中心的面向对象导航（UcON），这是一个新的基准测试，它纳入了用户特定的对象放置习惯，我们称之为用户习惯。该基准测试要求智能体利用这些用户习惯，以便在导航过程中做出更明智的决策。UcON涵盖了大约22,600个用户习惯，涉及489个对象类别。据我们所知，UcON是第一个明确形式化和大规模评估习惯条件下的对象导航，并且涵盖了最广泛的目标对象类别的基准测试。此外，我们提出了一种习惯检索模块，用于提取和利用与目标对象相关的习惯，使智能体能够更有效地推断其可能的位置。实验结果表明，当前的SOTA方法在习惯驱动的对象放置下表现出显著的性能下降，而集成用户习惯则持续提高成功率。代码可在https://github.com/whcpumpkin/User-Centric-Object-Navigation获取。

Authors: Hongcheng Wang, Jinyu Zhu, Hao Dong

ECO: Energy-Constrained Optimization with Reinforcement Learning for Humanoid Walking

Abstract (English): Achieving stable and energy-efficient locomotion is essential for humanoid robots to operate continuously in real-world applications. Existing MPC and RL approaches often rely on energy-related metrics embedded within a multi-objective optimization framework, which require extensive hyperparameter tuning and often result in suboptimal policies. To address these challenges, we propose ECO (Energy-Constrained Optimization), a constrained RL framework that separates energy-related metrics from rewards, reformulating them as explicit inequality constraints. This method provides a clear and interpretable physical representation of energy costs, enabling more efficient and intuitive hyperparameter tuning for improved energy efficiency. ECO introduces dedicated constraints for energy consumption and reference motion, enforced by the Lagrangian method, to achieve stable, symmetric, and energy-efficient walking for humanoid robots. We evaluated ECO against MPC, standard RL with reward shaping, and four state-of-the-art constrained RL methods. Experiments, including sim-to-sim and sim-to-real transfers on the kid-sized humanoid robot BRUCE, demonstrate that ECO significantly reduces energy consumption compared to baselines while maintaining robust walking performance. These results highlight a substantial advancement in energy-efficient humanoid locomotion. All experimental demonstrations can be found on the project website: https://sites.google.com/view/eco-humanoid.

摘要（中文）: 人形机器人要在真实应用环境中持续运行，实现稳定和节能的运动至关重要。现有的基于模型预测控制（MPC）和强化学习（RL）的方法通常依赖于嵌入在多目标优化框架中的能量相关指标，这需要大量的超参数调整，并常常导致次优策略。为了应对这些挑战，我们提出了ECO（能量约束优化），一种约束强化学习框架，它将能量相关指标从奖励中分离出来，并将其重新表述为显式不等式约束。该方法提供了能量成本的清晰且可解释的物理表示，从而能够进行更有效且直观的超参数调整，以提高能源效率。ECO引入了用于能量消耗和参考运动的专用约束，通过拉格朗日方法强制执行，以实现人形机器人的稳定、对称和节能行走。我们通过对儿童尺寸的人形机器人BRUCE的模拟到模拟和模拟到真实环境的转移实验，将ECO与MPC、使用奖励塑造的标准RL以及四种最先进的约束RL方法进行了评估。实验表明，与基线相比，ECO显著降低了能耗，同时保持了强大的行走性能。这些结果突出了在节能人形机器人运动方面取得的重大进展。所有实验演示都可以在项目网站上找到：https://sites.google.com/view/eco-humanoid。

TLDR: The paper introduces Energy-Constrained Optimization (ECO), a constrained RL framework for energy-efficient humanoid robot walking, demonstrating significant energy reduction compared to existing methods via sim-to-sim and sim-to-real experiments on the BRUCE robot.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种能量约束优化 (ECO) 框架，用于节能的人形机器人行走，并通过在 BRUCE 机器人上进行的仿真到仿真和仿真到真实实验，证明了与现有方法相比，能量消耗显著降低。

Authors: Weidong Huang, Jingwen Zhang, Jiongye Li, Shibowen Zhang, Jiayang Wu, Jiayi Wang, Hangxin Liu, Yaodong Yang, Yao Su

Bridging the Indoor-Outdoor Gap: Vision-Centric Instruction-Guided Embodied Navigation for the Last Meters

Abstract (English): Embodied navigation holds significant promise for real-world applications such as last-mile delivery. However, most existing approaches are confined to either indoor or outdoor environments and rely heavily on strong assumptions, such as access to precise coordinate systems. While current outdoor methods can guide agents to the vicinity of a target using coarse-grained localization, they fail to enable fine-grained entry through specific building entrances, critically limiting their utility in practical deployment scenarios that require seamless outdoor-to-indoor transitions. To bridge this gap, we introduce a novel task: out-to-in prior-free instruction-driven embodied navigation. This formulation explicitly eliminates reliance on accurate external priors, requiring agents to navigate solely based on egocentric visual observations guided by instructions. To tackle this task, we propose a vision-centric embodied navigation framework that leverages image-based prompts to drive decision-making. Additionally, we present the first open-source dataset for this task, featuring a pipeline that integrates trajectory-conditioned video synthesis into the data generation process. Through extensive experiments, we demonstrate that our proposed method consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines across key metrics including success rate and path efficiency.

摘要（中文）: 具身导航在诸如最后一英里配送等实际应用中具有巨大的潜力。然而，现有的大多数方法都局限于室内或室外环境，并且严重依赖于强假设，例如对精确坐标系统的访问。虽然目前的室外方法可以使用粗粒度的定位引导智能体到达目标附近，但它们无法实现通过特定建筑物入口的精细化进入，这严重限制了它们在需要无缝室外到室内过渡的实际部署场景中的效用。为了弥合这一差距，我们引入了一项新任务：无先验知识的指令驱动的室外到室内具身导航。这种表述明确消除了对精确外部先验的依赖，要求智能体仅根据以自我为中心的视觉观察在指令的引导下进行导航。为了解决这个任务，我们提出了一种以视觉为中心的具身导航框架，该框架利用基于图像的提示来驱动决策。此外，我们还提出了该任务的第一个开源数据集，该数据集具有将轨迹条件视频合成集成到数据生成过程中的流程。通过广泛的实验，我们证明了我们提出的方法在包括成功率和路径效率在内的关键指标上始终优于最先进的基线方法。

TLDR: This paper introduces a new task and dataset for instruction-guided embodied navigation that bridges the indoor-outdoor gap without relying on precise coordinate systems, using a vision-centric approach. They demonstrate improved performance compared to SOTA baselines.

Authors: Yuxiang Zhao, Yirong Yang, Yanqing Zhu, Yanfen Shen, Chiyu Wang, Zhining Gu, Pei Shi, Wei Guo, Mu Xu

Now You See That: Learning End-to-End Humanoid Locomotion from Raw Pixels

Abstract (English): Achieving robust vision-based humanoid locomotion remains challenging due to two fundamental issues: the sim-to-real gap introduces significant perception noise that degrades performance on fine-grained tasks, and training a unified policy across diverse terrains is hindered by conflicting learning objectives. To address these challenges, we present an end-to-end framework for vision-driven humanoid locomotion. For robust sim-to-real transfer, we develop a high-fidelity depth sensor simulation that captures stereo matching artifacts and calibration uncertainties inherent in real-world sensing. We further propose a vision-aware behavior distillation approach that combines latent space alignment with noise-invariant auxiliary tasks, enabling effective knowledge transfer from privileged height maps to noisy depth observations. For versatile terrain adaptation, we introduce terrain-specific reward shaping integrated with multi-critic and multi-discriminator learning, where dedicated networks capture the distinct dynamics and motion priors of each terrain type. We validate our approach on two humanoid platforms equipped with different stereo depth cameras. The resulting policy demonstrates robust performance across diverse environments, seamlessly handling extreme challenges such as high platforms and wide gaps, as well as fine-grained tasks including bidirectional long-term staircase traversal.

摘要（中文）: 基于视觉的人形机器人稳健运动一直是具有挑战性的，这归因于两个根本性问题：仿真到真实的鸿沟引入了显著的感知噪声，降低了对精细任务的表现；以及在多样地形上训练统一策略受限于相互冲突的学习目标。为了应对这些挑战，我们提出了一种用于视觉驱动的人形机器人运动的端到端框架。为了实现稳健的仿真到真实迁移，我们开发了一种高保真度深度传感器仿真，用于捕捉真实世界传感中固有的立体匹配伪影和标定不确定性。我们进一步提出了一种视觉感知行为蒸馏方法，该方法将潜在空间对齐与噪声不变辅助任务相结合，从而能够从特权高度图有效地迁移知识到含噪深度观测。为了实现通用地形适应，我们引入了与多重评论家和多重判别器学习相结合的特定地形奖励塑形，其中专用网络捕捉每种地形类型的独特动力学和运动先验。我们在配备不同立体深度相机的两个人形机器人平台上验证了我们的方法。结果策略在各种环境中展示了稳健的性能，无缝处理了诸如高平台和宽间隙等极端挑战，以及包括双向长期楼梯遍历等精细任务。

TLDR: This paper presents an end-to-end framework for vision-driven humanoid locomotion, addressing sim-to-real transfer and versatile terrain adaptation using techniques like high-fidelity depth sensor simulation, vision-aware behavior distillation, and terrain-specific reward shaping.

Authors: Wandong Sun, Yongbo Su, Leoric Huang, Alex Zhang, Dwyane Wei, Mu San, Daniel Tian, Ellie Cao, Finn Yan, Ethan Xie, Zongwu Xie

Towards Adaptive Environment Generation for Training Embodied Agents

Abstract (English): Embodied agents struggle to generalize to new environments, even when those environments share similar underlying structures to their training settings. Most current approaches to generating these training environments follow an open-loop paradigm, without considering the agent's current performance. While procedural generation methods can produce diverse scenes, diversity without feedback from the agent is inefficient. The generated environments may be trivially easy, providing limited learning signal. To address this, we present a proof-of-concept for closed-loop environment generation that adapts difficulty to the agent's current capabilities. Our system employs a controllable environment representation, extracts fine-grained performance feedback beyond binary success or failure, and implements a closed-loop adaptation mechanism that translates this feedback into environment modifications. This feedback-driven approach generates training environments that more challenging in the ways the agent needs to improve, enabling more efficient learning and better generalization to novel settings.

摘要（中文）: 具身智能体难以泛化到新的环境中，即使这些环境与它们的训练环境共享相似的底层结构。 目前生成这些训练环境的大多数方法都遵循一种开环范式，而不考虑智能体当前的性能。 虽然过程化生成方法可以产生多样化的场景，但没有来自智能体的反馈的多样性是低效的。 生成的环境可能过于简单，提供的学习信号有限。 为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种闭环环境生成的概念验证，该生成方式将难度调整到智能体当前的能力。 我们的系统采用了一种可控的环境表示，提取了除了二元成功或失败之外的细粒度性能反馈，并实现了一种闭环适应机制，将这种反馈转化为环境修改。 这种反馈驱动的方法生成训练环境，使其在智能体需要改进的方面更具挑战性，从而实现更高效的学习，并更好地泛化到新的设置中。

TLDR: This paper introduces a closed-loop environment generation method for embodied agents that adapts environment difficulty based on agent performance, aiming to improve learning efficiency and generalization.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种用于具身智能体的闭环环境生成方法，该方法可以根据智能体的表现调整环境难度，旨在提高学习效率和泛化能力。

Authors: Teresa Yeo, Dulaj Weerakoon, Dulanga Weerakoon, Archan Misra

Nipping the Drift in the Bud: Retrospective Rectification for Robust Vision-Language Navigation

Abstract (English): Vision-Language Navigation (VLN) requires embodied agents to interpret natural language instructions and navigate through complex continuous 3D environments. However, the dominant imitation learning paradigm suffers from exposure bias, where minor deviations during inference lead to compounding errors. While DAgger-style approaches attempt to mitigate this by correcting error states, we identify a critical limitation: Instruction-State Misalignment. Forcing an agent to learn recovery actions from off-track states often creates supervision signals that semantically conflict with the original instruction. In response to these challenges, we introduce BudVLN, an online framework that learns from on-policy rollouts by constructing supervision to match the current state distribution. BudVLN performs retrospective rectification via counterfactual re-anchoring and decision-conditioned supervision synthesis, using a geodesic oracle to synthesize corrective trajectories that originate from valid historical states, ensuring semantic consistency. Experiments on the standard R2R-CE and RxR-CE benchmarks demonstrate that BudVLN consistently mitigates distribution shift and achieves state-of-the-art performance in both Success Rate and SPL.

摘要（中文）: 视觉-语言导航 (VLN) 要求具身智能体解释自然语言指令并在复杂的连续3D环境中导航。然而，主流的模仿学习范式存在暴露偏差，即推理过程中的微小偏差会导致误差累积。虽然DAgger类方法试图通过纠正错误状态来缓解这个问题，但我们发现了一个关键的局限性：指令-状态失配。强制智能体从偏离轨道的状态中学习恢复动作，往往会产生与原始指令语义冲突的监督信号。为应对这些挑战，我们引入了BudVLN，一个在线框架，通过构建与当前状态分布相匹配的监督信号，从在线策略的展开中学习。BudVLN通过反事实重锚定和决策条件监督合成执行回顾性纠正，使用测地线预言机合成从有效历史状态出发的纠正轨迹，从而确保语义一致性。在标准R2R-CE和RxR-CE基准上的实验表明，BudVLN能够始终如一地缓解分布偏移，并在成功率和SPL两方面都达到最先进的性能。

TLDR: BudVLN addresses instruction-state misalignment in vision-language navigation by using retrospective rectification with counterfactual re-anchoring and decision-conditioned supervision, achieving state-of-the-art results on R2R-CE and RxR-CE benchmarks.

简要说明: BudVLN通过追溯校正和反事实重新锚定，以及决策条件监督，解决了视觉语言导航中的指令-状态错位问题，并在R2R-CE和RxR-CE基准测试中取得了最先进的结果。

Authors: Gang He, Zhenyang Liu, Kepeng Xu, Li Xu, Tong Qiao, Wenxin Yu, Chang Wu, Weiying Xie

HiWET: Hierarchical World-Frame End-Effector Tracking for Long-Horizon Humanoid Loco-Manipulation

Abstract (English): Humanoid loco-manipulation requires executing precise manipulation tasks while maintaining dynamic stability amid base motion and impacts. Existing approaches typically formulate commands in body-centric frames, fail to inherently correct cumulative world-frame drift induced by legged locomotion. We reformulate the problem as world-frame end-effector tracking and propose HiWET, a hierarchical reinforcement learning framework that decouples global reasoning from dynamic execution. The high-level policy generates subgoals that jointly optimize end-effector accuracy and base positioning in the world frame, while the low-level policy executes these commands under stability constraints. We introduce a Kinematic Manifold Prior (KMP) that embeds the manipulation manifold into the action space via residual learning, reducing exploration dimensionality and mitigating kinematically invalid behaviors. Extensive simulation and ablation studies demonstrate that HiWET achieves precise and stable end-effector tracking in long-horizon world-frame tasks. We validate zero-shot sim-to-real transfer of the low-level policy on a physical humanoid, demonstrating stable locomotion under diverse manipulation commands. These results indicate that explicit world-frame reasoning combined with hierarchical control provides an effective and scalable solution for long-horizon humanoid loco-manipulation.

摘要（中文）: 人形机器人步态操纵需要在基座运动和冲击扰动下，执行精确的机械臂操作任务，同时保持动态稳定性。现有的方法通常在以人体为中心的坐标系中制定指令，无法固有地纠正腿式运动引起的累积世界坐标系漂移。我们将问题重新表述为世界坐标系下的末端执行器跟踪，并提出了HiWET，一种分层强化学习框架，将全局推理与动态执行解耦。高层策略生成子目标，在世界坐标系中联合优化末端执行器的精度和基座定位，而低层策略在稳定约束下执行这些指令。我们引入了一种运动学流形先验（KMP），通过残差学习将操纵流形嵌入到动作空间中，从而降低探索维度，并减轻运动学无效行为。大量的模拟和消融研究表明，HiWET在长时程世界坐标系任务中实现了精确且稳定的末端执行器跟踪。我们在物理人形机器人上验证了低层策略的零样本模拟到真实世界的迁移，展示了在各种操纵指令下的稳定步态。这些结果表明，显式的世界坐标系推理与分层控制相结合，为长时程人形机器人步态操纵提供了一种有效且可扩展的解决方案。

TLDR: HiWET, a hierarchical RL framework, is proposed for humanoid loco-manipulation, achieving accurate world-frame end-effector tracking and stable locomotion, validated by sim-to-real transfer.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一个名为HiWET的层次化强化学习框架，用于人形机器人移动操作，实现了精确的世界坐标系末端执行器跟踪和稳定的运动，并通过模拟到真实的迁移进行了验证。

Authors: Zhanxiang Cao, Liyun Yan, Yang Zhang, Sirui Chen, Jianming Ma, Tianyue Zhan, Shengcheng Fu, Yufei Jia, Cewu Lu, Yue Gao

Action Hallucination in Generative Visual-Language-Action Models

Abstract (English): Robot Foundation Models such as Vision-Language-Action models are rapidly reshaping how robot policies are trained and deployed, replacing hand-designed planners with end-to-end generative action models. While these systems demonstrate impressive generalization, it remains unclear whether they fundamentally resolve the long-standing challenges of robotics. We address this question by analyzing action hallucinations that violate physical constraints and their extension to plan-level failures. Focusing on latent-variable generative policies, we show that hallucinations often arise from structural mismatches between feasible robot behavior and common model architectures. We study three such barriers -- topological, precision, and horizon -- and show how they impose unavoidable tradeoffs. Our analysis provides mechanistic explanations for reported empirical failures of generative robot policies and suggests principled directions for improving reliability and trustworthiness, without abandoning their expressive power.

摘要（中文）: 基于视觉-语言-动作模型的机器人基础模型正在迅速重塑机器人策略的训练和部署方式，以端到端生成式动作模型取代手工设计的规划器。虽然这些系统展现出令人瞩目的泛化能力，但它们是否从根本上解决了机器人领域的长期挑战仍不清楚。我们通过分析违反物理约束的动作幻觉及其对规划层面失败的扩展来探讨这个问题。通过聚焦于隐变量生成式策略，我们表明幻觉通常源于可行机器人行为与常见

Authors: Harold Soh, Eugene Lim

Coupled Local and Global World Models for Efficient First Order RL

Abstract (English): World models offer a promising avenue for more faithfully capturing complex dynamics, including contacts and non-rigidity, as well as complex sensory information, such as visual perception, in situations where standard simulators struggle. However, these models are computationally complex to evaluate, posing a challenge for popular RL approaches that have been successfully used with simulators to solve complex locomotion tasks but yet struggle with manipulation. This paper introduces a method that bypasses simulators entirely, training RL policies inside world models learned from robots' interactions with real environments. At its core, our approach enables policy training with large-scale diffusion models via a novel decoupled first-order gradient (FoG) method: a full-scale world model generates accurate forward trajectories, while a lightweight latent-space surrogate approximates its local dynamics for efficient gradient computation. This coupling of a local and global world model ensures high-fidelity unrolling alongside computationally tractable differentiation. We demonstrate the efficacy of our method on the Push-T manipulation task, where it significantly outperforms PPO in sample efficiency. We further evaluate our approach through an ego-centric object manipulation task with a quadruped. Together, these results demonstrate that learning inside data-driven world models is a promising pathway for solving hard-to-model RL tasks in image space without reliance on hand-crafted physics simulators.

摘要（中文）: 世界模型为更真实地捕捉复杂动力学提供了一种有前景的途径，包括接触和非刚性，以及复杂的感官信息，例如视觉感知，这些情景是标准模拟器难以应对的。然而，这些模型在计算上评估起来很复杂，对已成功用于求解复杂运动任务，但仍在操控任务中挣扎的、流行的强化学习方法构成了挑战。本文介绍了一种完全绕过模拟器的方法，在从机器人与真实环境交互中学习到的世界模型内部训练强化学习策略。其核心在于，我们的方法通过一种新颖的解耦一阶梯度 (FoG) 方法，实现了大规模扩散模型的策略训练：一个全尺寸的世界模型生成精确的前向轨迹，而一个轻量级的潜在空间代理近似其局部动力学，以实现高效的梯度计算。这种局部和全局世界模型的耦合确保了高保真的轨迹展开，同时也保证了计算上可行的微分。我们在 Push-T 操控任务上展示了我们方法的有效性，其样本效率显著优于 PPO。我们进一步通过四足机器人的以自我为中心的物体操控任务评估了我们的方法。总之，这些结果表明，在数据驱动的世界模型中进行学习，是解决图像空间中难以建模的强化学习任务的一种有希望的途径，而无需依赖手工设计的物理模拟器。

TLDR: The paper introduces a novel approach for training RL policies within learned world models, using a coupled local and global architecture for efficient and accurate gradient computation, demonstrated on challenging manipulation tasks.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种新的RL策略训练方法，该方法在学习到的世界模型中进行，使用耦合的局部和全局架构来实现高效准确的梯度计算，并在具有挑战性的操作任务中进行了演示。

Authors: Joseph Amigo, Rooholla Khorrambakht, Nicolas Mansard, Ludovic Righetti

CommCP: Efficient Multi-Agent Coordination via LLM-Based Communication with Conformal Prediction

Abstract (English): To complete assignments provided by humans in natural language, robots must interpret commands, generate and answer relevant questions for scene understanding, and manipulate target objects. Real-world deployments often require multiple heterogeneous robots with different manipulation capabilities to handle different assignments cooperatively. Beyond the need for specialized manipulation skills, effective information gathering is important in completing these assignments. To address this component of the problem, we formalize the information-gathering process in a fully cooperative setting as an underexplored multi-agent multi-task Embodied Question Answering (MM-EQA) problem, which is a novel extension of canonical Embodied Question Answering (EQA), where effective communication is crucial for coordinating efforts without redundancy. To address this problem, we propose CommCP, a novel LLM-based decentralized communication framework designed for MM-EQA. Our framework employs conformal prediction to calibrate the generated messages, thereby minimizing receiver distractions and enhancing communication reliability. To evaluate our framework, we introduce an MM-EQA benchmark featuring diverse, photo-realistic household scenarios with embodied questions. Experimental results demonstrate that CommCP significantly enhances the task success rate and exploration efficiency over baselines. The experiment videos, code, and dataset are available on our project website: https://comm-cp.github.io.

摘要（中文）: 为了完成人类以自然语言提供的任务，机器人必须理解指令，生成并回答与场景理解相关的提问，并操纵目标物体。现实世界的部署通常需要多个具有不同操作能力的异构机器人协同合作来处理不同的任务。除了需要专门的操作技能外，有效的信息收集对于完成这些任务也很重要。为了解决这一问题，我们将完全合作环境下的信息收集过程形式化为一个尚未充分探索的多智能体多任务具身问答（MM-EQA）问题，这是经典具身问答（EQA）的一个新的扩展，其中有效的沟通对于协调工作，避免冗余至关重要。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了CommCP，一种基于大型语言模型（LLM）的新型去中心化通信框架，专为MM-EQA设计。 我们的框架采用保角预测来校准生成的消息，从而最大限度地减少接收者的干扰，并提高通信的可靠性。为了评估我们的框架，我们引入了一个MM-EQA基准，其中包含具有具身问题的多样化、逼真的家庭场景。实验结果表明，与基线相比，CommCP显著提高了任务成功率和探索效率。 实验视频、代码和数据集可在我们的项目网站上找到：https://comm-cp.github.io。

TLDR: The paper introduces CommCP, a novel LLM-based decentralized communication framework using conformal prediction for multi-agent multi-task Embodied Question Answering (MM-EQA), and demonstrates its effectiveness on a new benchmark with improved task success and exploration efficiency.

Authors: Xiaopan Zhang, Zejin Wang, Zhixu Li, Jianpeng Yao, Jiachen Li

InterPrior: Scaling Generative Control for Physics-Based Human-Object Interactions

Abstract (English): Humans rarely plan whole-body interactions with objects at the level of explicit whole-body movements. High-level intentions, such as affordance, define the goal, while coordinated balance, contact, and manipulation can emerge naturally from underlying physical and motor priors. Scaling such priors is key to enabling humanoids to compose and generalize loco-manipulation skills across diverse contexts while maintaining physically coherent whole-body coordination. To this end, we introduce InterPrior, a scalable framework that learns a unified generative controller through large-scale imitation pretraining and post-training by reinforcement learning. InterPrior first distills a full-reference imitation expert into a versatile, goal-conditioned variational policy that reconstructs motion from multimodal observations and high-level intent. While the distilled policy reconstructs training behaviors, it does not generalize reliably due to the vast configuration space of large-scale human-object interactions. To address this, we apply data augmentation with physical perturbations, and then perform reinforcement learning finetuning to improve competence on unseen goals and initializations. Together, these steps consolidate the reconstructed latent skills into a valid manifold, yielding a motion prior that generalizes beyond the training data, e.g., it can incorporate new behaviors such as interactions with unseen objects. We further demonstrate its effectiveness for user-interactive control and its potential for real robot deployment.

摘要（中文）: 人类极少在显式全身运动的层面上规划与物体的全身交互。诸如可供性之类的高层意图定义了目标，而协调的平衡、接触和操控则可以自然地从潜在的物理和运动先验中涌现。扩展这些先验是使人形机器人能够在各种环境中组合和泛化loco-manipulation（移动操作）技能，同时保持物理上连贯的全身协调的关键。为此，我们引入了InterPrior，这是一个可扩展的框架，通过大规模模仿预训练和强化学习后训练来学习统一的生成控制器。InterPrior首先将一个全参考模仿专家提炼成一个通用的、目标条件化的变分策略，该策略从多模态观察和高层意图中重建运动。虽然提炼出的策略重建了训练行为，但由于大规模人-物交互的巨大配置空间，它不能可靠地泛化。为了解决这个问题，我们应用带有物理扰动的数据增强，然后进行强化学习微调，以提高在未见过的目标和初始化条件下的能力。总而言之，这些步骤将重建的潜在技能整合到一个有效的流形中，产生一个超越训练数据的运动先验，例如，它可以整合新的行为，如与未见过的物体的交互。我们进一步证明了其在用户交互控制中的有效性以及在真实机器人部署中的潜力。

TLDR: The paper introduces InterPrior, a framework for learning a unified generative controller for physics-based human-object interactions, using imitation pretraining and reinforcement learning finetuning to achieve scalable and generalizable loco-manipulation skills.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一个名为InterPrior的框架，用于学习基于物理的人-物交互的统一生成控制器，通过模仿预训练和强化学习微调来实现可扩展和可泛化的loco-manipulation技能。

Authors: Sirui Xu, Samuel Schulter, Morteza Ziyadi, Xialin He, Xiaohan Fei, Yu-Xiong Wang, Liangyan Gui

Visuo-Tactile World Models

Abstract (English): We introduce multi-task Visuo-Tactile World Models (VT-WM), which capture the physics of contact through touch reasoning. By complementing vision with tactile sensing, VT-WM better understands robot-object interactions in contact-rich tasks, avoiding common failure modes of vision-only models under occlusion or ambiguous contact states, such as objects disappearing, teleporting, or moving in ways that violate basic physics. Trained across a set of contact-rich manipulation tasks, VT-WM improves physical fidelity in imagination, achieving 33% better performance at maintaining object permanence and 29% better compliance with the laws of motion in autoregressive rollouts. Moreover, experiments show that grounding in contact dynamics also translates to planning. In zero-shot real-robot experiments, VT-WM achieves up to 35% higher success rates, with the largest gains in multi-step, contact-rich tasks. Finally, VT-WM demonstrates significant downstream versatility, effectively adapting its learned contact dynamics to a novel task and achieving reliable planning success with only a limited set of demonstrations.

摘要（中文）: 我们引入了多任务视觉-触觉世界模型（VT-WM），它通过触觉推理来捕捉接触物理特性。通过利用触觉感知补充视觉，VT-WM更好地理解了富接触任务中的机器人-物体交互，避免了纯视觉模型在遮挡或模糊接触状态下的常见失效模式，例如物体消失、瞬移或以违反基本物理规律的方式移动。通过在一系列富接触操作任务中进行训练，VT-WM提高了想象中的物理保真度，在自回归展开中，保持物体永久性的性能提高了33%，对运动定律的遵守程度提高了29%。此外，实验表明，基于接触动力学的决策规划也有效。在零样本真实机器人实验中，VT-WM的成功率提高了35%，在多步骤、富接触任务中增益最为显著。最后，VT-WM表现出显著的下游通用性，能够有效地将其学习到的接触动力学适应于新任务，并仅通过少量演示即可实现可靠的规划成功。

TLDR: The paper introduces Visuo-Tactile World Models (VT-WM) that integrate tactile sensing with vision to improve robot-object interaction in contact-rich tasks, demonstrating better physical fidelity, planning, and zero-shot transfer to real robots.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了视觉-触觉世界模型 (VT-WM)，通过结合触觉感知和视觉来改善机器人在接触丰富的任务中的对象交互，展示了更好的物理保真度、规划能力和到真实机器人的零样本迁移能力。

Authors: Carolina Higuera, Sergio Arnaud, Byron Boots, Mustafa Mukadam, Francois Robert Hogan, Franziska Meier

Extended to Reality: Prompt Injection in 3D Environments

Abstract (English): Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have advanced the capabilities to interpret and act on visual input in 3D environments, empowering diverse applications such as robotics and situated conversational agents. When MLLMs reason over camera-captured views of the physical world, a new attack surface emerges: an attacker can place text-bearing physical objects in the environment to override MLLMs' intended task. While prior work has studied prompt injection in the text domain and through digitally edited 2D images, it remains unclear how these attacks function in 3D physical environments. To bridge the gap, we introduce PI3D, a prompt injection attack against MLLMs in 3D environments, realized through text-bearing physical object placement rather than digital image edits. We formulate and solve the problem of identifying an effective 3D object pose (position and orientation) with injected text, where the attacker's goal is to induce the MLLM to perform the injected task while ensuring that the object placement remains physically plausible. Experiments demonstrate that PI3D is an effective attack against multiple MLLMs under diverse camera trajectories. We further evaluate existing defenses and show that they are insufficient to defend against PI3D.

摘要（中文）: 多模态大型语言模型（MLLM）已在理解和作用于3D环境中的视觉输入方面取得了进展，从而推动了机器人和情境会话代理等多种应用。当MLLM推理物理世界的摄像头捕获视图时，出现了一个新的攻击面：攻击者可以在环境中放置带有文本的物理对象，以覆盖MLLM的预期任务。虽然先前的工作已经研究了文本领域以及通过数字编辑的2D图像的提示注入攻击，但这些攻击如何在3D物理环境中发挥作用仍不清楚。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出了PI3D，这是一种针对3D环境中MLLM的提示注入攻击，通过带有文本的物理对象放置而非数字图像编辑来实现。我们制定并解决了识别带有注入文本的有效3D对象姿态（位置和方向）的问题，其中攻击者的目标是诱导MLLM执行注入的任务，同时确保对象放置在物理上是合理的。实验表明，PI3D是一种有效的攻击，能够对抗多种在不同摄像头轨迹下的MLLM。我们进一步评估了现有的防御措施，并表明它们不足以防御PI3D。

TLDR: This paper introduces PI3D, a novel prompt injection attack that leverages text-bearing physical objects in 3D environments to manipulate multimodal LLMs, demonstrating its effectiveness and the limitations of current defenses.

简要说明: 本文介绍了PI3D，一种新型的提示注入攻击，它利用3D环境中的文本物理对象来操纵多模态LLM，证明了其有效性以及当前防御措施的局限性。

Authors: Zhuoheng Li, Ying Chen

From Features to Actions: Explainability in Traditional and Agentic AI Systems

Abstract (English): Over the last decade, explainable AI has primarily focused on interpreting individual model predictions, producing post-hoc explanations that relate inputs to outputs under a fixed decision structure. Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have enabled agentic AI systems whose behaviour unfolds over multi-step trajectories. In these settings, success and failure are determined by sequences of decisions rather than a single output. While useful, it remains unclear how explanation approaches designed for static predictions translate to agentic settings where behaviour emerges over time. In this work, we bridge the gap between static and agentic explainability by comparing attribution-based explanations with trace-based diagnostics across both settings. To make this distinction explicit, we empirically compare attribution-based explanations used in static classification tasks with trace-based diagnostics used in agentic benchmarks (TAU-bench Airline and AssistantBench). Our results show that while attribution methods achieve stable feature rankings in static settings (Spearman $ρ= 0.86$), they cannot be applied reliably to diagnose execution-level failures in agentic trajectories. In contrast, trace-grounded rubric evaluation for agentic settings consistently localizes behaviour breakdowns and reveals that state tracking inconsistency is 2.7$\times$ more prevalent in failed runs and reduces success probability by 49\%. These findings motivate a shift towards trajectory-level explainability for agentic systems when evaluating and diagnosing autonomous AI behaviour. Resources: https://github.com/VectorInstitute/unified-xai-evaluation-framework https://vectorinstitute.github.io/unified-xai-evaluation-framework

摘要（中文）: 过去十年中，可解释人工智能主要集中于解释单个模型预测，产生后验解释，这些解释在固定的决策结构下将输入与输出联系起来。大型语言模型（LLMs）的最新进展推动了智能体AI系统的发展，其行为在多步轨迹中展开。在这种情境下，成功和失败取决于一系列决策，而非单一输出。虽然有价值，但为静态预测设计的解释方法如何转化为智能体情境，行为随时间推移而涌现，仍然不清楚。在这项工作中，我们通过比较基于归因的解释和基于轨迹的诊断，弥合了静态和智能体可解释性之间的差距。为了明确区分这一点，我们实证性地比较了用于静态分类任务的基于归因的解释和用于智能体基准测试（TAU-bench Airline 和 AssistantBench）的基于轨迹的诊断。我们的结果表明，虽然归因方法在静态环境中实现了稳定的特征排序（Spearman $ρ= 0.86$），但它们不能可靠地应用于诊断智能体轨迹中的执行级故障。相比之下，智能体情境下基于轨迹的评估能够一致地定位行为崩溃，并揭示状态跟踪不一致在失败运行中更为普遍（占比2.7倍），并降低成功概率达49%。这些发现推动了在评估和诊断自主AI行为时，转向智能体系统的轨迹级可解释性。 资源： https://github.com/VectorInstitute/unified-xai-evaluation-framework https://vectorinstitute.github.io/unified-xai-evaluation-framework

TLDR: This paper compares attribution-based explanations in static classification with trace-based diagnostics in agentic AI systems, finding that attribution methods are unreliable for diagnosing execution failures in agentic trajectories, motivating a shift towards trajectory-level explainability.

简要说明: 本文比较了静态分类中基于属性的解释与智能体AI系统中基于轨迹的诊断，发现属性方法无法可靠地诊断智能体轨迹中的执行故障，从而推动了向智能体系统的轨迹级别可解释性的转变。

Authors: Sindhuja Chaduvula, Jessee Ho, Kina Kim, Aravind Narayanan, Mahshid Alinoori, Muskan Garg, Dhanesh Ramachandram, Shaina Raza

ScaleEnv: Scaling Environment Synthesis from Scratch for Generalist Interactive Tool-Use Agent Training

Abstract (English): Training generalist agents capable of adapting to diverse scenarios requires interactive environments for self-exploration. However, interactive environments remain critically scarce, and existing synthesis methods suffer from significant limitations regarding environmental diversity and scalability. To address these challenges, we introduce ScaleEnv, a framework that constructs fully interactive environments and verifiable tasks entirely from scratch. Specifically, ScaleEnv ensures environment reliability through procedural testing, and guarantees task completeness and solvability via tool dependency graph expansion and executable action verification. By enabling agents to learn through exploration within ScaleEnv, we demonstrate significant performance improvements on unseen, multi-turn tool-use benchmarks such as $τ^2$-Bench and VitaBench, highlighting strong generalization capabilities. Furthermore, we investigate the relationship between increasing number of domains and model generalization performance, providing empirical evidence that scaling environmental diversity is critical for robust agent learning.

摘要（中文）: 训练能够适应各种场景的通用智能体需要用于自我探索的交互式环境。然而，交互式环境仍然极度稀缺，并且现有的合成方法在环境多样性和可扩展性方面存在显著限制。为了解决这些挑战，我们引入了ScaleEnv，一个从头构建完全交互式环境和可验证任务的框架。具体而言，ScaleEnv通过程序化测试确保环境的可靠性，并通过工具依赖关系图扩展和可执行动作验证保证任务的完整性和可解性。通过使智能体在ScaleEnv中探索学习，我们在未见过的多轮工具使用基准测试（例如$τ^2$-Bench和VitaBench）上展示了显著的性能提升，突出了强大的泛化能力。此外，我们研究了增加领域数量与模型泛化性能之间的关系，提供了经验证据表明，扩展环境多样性对于鲁棒的智能体学习至关重要。

TLDR: The paper introduces ScaleEnv, a framework for generating diverse and scalable interactive environments from scratch, enabling the training of generalist agents with improved generalization on tool-use benchmarks.

Authors: Dunwei Tu, Hongyan Hao, Hansi Yang, Yihao Chen, Yi-Kai Zhang, Zhikang Xia, Yu Yang, Yueqing Sun, Xingchen Liu, Furao Shen, Qi Gu, Hui Su, Xunliang Cai

Generating Data-Driven Reasoning Rubrics for Domain-Adaptive Reward Modeling

Abstract (English): An impediment to using Large Language Models (LLMs) for reasoning output verification is that LLMs struggle to reliably identify errors in thinking traces, particularly in long outputs, domains requiring expert knowledge, and problems without verifiable rewards. We propose a data-driven approach to automatically construct highly granular reasoning error taxonomies to enhance LLM-driven error detection on unseen reasoning traces. Our findings indicate that classification approaches that leverage these error taxonomies, or "rubrics", demonstrate strong error identification compared to baseline methods in technical domains like coding, math, and chemical engineering. These rubrics can be used to build stronger LLM-as-judge reward functions for reasoning model training via reinforcement learning. Experimental results show that these rewards have the potential to improve models' task accuracy on difficult domains over models trained by general LLMs-as-judges by +45%, and approach performance of models trained by verifiable rewards while using as little as 20% as many gold labels. Through our approach, we extend the usage of reward rubrics from assessing qualitative model behavior to assessing quantitative model correctness on tasks typically learned via RLVR rewards. This extension opens the door for teaching models to solve complex technical problems without a full dataset of gold labels, which are often highly costly to procure.

摘要（中文）: 使用大型语言模型(LLM)进行推理输出验证的一个障碍是，LLM难以可靠地识别思维轨迹中的错误，尤其是在长输出、需要专家知识的领域以及没有可验证奖励的问题中。我们提出了一种数据驱动的方法，用于自动构建高度精细化的推理错误分类法，以增强LLM驱动的对未见推理轨迹的错误检测能力。我们的研究结果表明，与基线方法相比，利用这些错误分类法，或“评分标准”，的分类方法在编码、数学和化学工程等技术领域表现出强大的错误识别能力。这些评分标准可用于构建更强大的LLM作为裁判的奖励函数，以通过强化学习进行推理模型训练。实验结果表明，与通过通用LLM作为裁判训练的模型相比，这些奖励函数有潜力将模型在困难领域上的任务准确率提高+45%，并且在使用仅20%的黄金标签的情况下，接近通过可验证奖励训练的模型的性能。通过我们的方法，我们将奖励评分标准的使用从评估定性模型行为扩展到评估通常通过RLVR奖励学习的任务中的定量模型正确性。这种扩展为在没有完整黄金标签数据集的情况下，教授模型解决复杂技术问题打开了大门，而这些黄金标签的获取通常成本高昂。

TLDR: The paper introduces a data-driven approach to generate reasoning rubrics for improving LLM-based error detection in reasoning traces, leading to better reward modeling and performance in complex technical domains. The method reduces the reliance on costly labeled data for reinforcement learning.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种数据驱动的方法来生成用于改进LLM推理轨迹中错误检测的推理规则，从而在复杂技术领域实现更好的奖励建模和性能。该方法减少了对强化学习中昂贵标记数据的依赖。

Authors: Kate Sanders, Nathaniel Weir, Sapana Chaudhary, Kaj Bostrom, Huzefa Rangwala

SPARC: Separating Perception And Reasoning Circuits for Test-time Scaling of VLMs

Abstract (English): Despite recent successes, test-time scaling - i.e., dynamically expanding the token budget during inference as needed - remains brittle for vision-language models (VLMs): unstructured chains-of-thought about images entangle perception and reasoning, leading to long, disorganized contexts where small perceptual mistakes may cascade into completely wrong answers. Moreover, expensive reinforcement learning with hand-crafted rewards is required to achieve good performance. Here, we introduce SPARC (Separating Perception And Reasoning Circuits), a modular framework that explicitly decouples visual perception from reasoning. Inspired by sequential sensory-to-cognitive processing in the brain, SPARC implements a two-stage pipeline where the model first performs explicit visual search to localize question-relevant regions, then conditions its reasoning on those regions to produce the final answer. This separation enables independent test-time scaling with asymmetric compute allocation (e.g., prioritizing perceptual processing under distribution shift), supports selective optimization (e.g., improving the perceptual stage alone when it is the bottleneck for end-to-end performance), and accommodates compressed contexts by running global search at lower image resolutions and allocating high-resolution processing only to selected regions, thereby reducing total visual tokens count and compute. Across challenging visual reasoning benchmarks, SPARC outperforms monolithic baselines and strong visual-grounding approaches. For instance, SPARC improves the accuracy of Qwen3VL-4B on the $V^*$ VQA benchmark by 6.7 percentage points, and it surpasses "thinking with images" by 4.6 points on a challenging OOD task despite requiring a 200$\times$ lower token budget.

摘要（中文）: 尽管近期取得了一些成功，但测试时缩放——即在推理过程中根据需要动态扩展token预算——对于视觉语言模型（VLMs）而言仍然很脆弱：关于图像的非结构化思维链会纠缠感知和推理，导致冗长、无序的上下文，其中微小的感知错误可能会级联成完全错误的答案。此外，获得良好的性能，还需要通过手工设计的奖励进行昂贵的强化学习。在此，我们介绍SPARC（分离感知和推理回路），这是一个模块化框架，它显式地将视觉感知与推理解耦。受到大脑中顺序感觉-认知处理的启发，SPARC实现了一个两阶段流程：模型首先执行显式视觉搜索以定位与问题相关的区域，然后基于这些区域进行推理，以产生最终答案。这种分离能够实现独立的测试时缩放，具有非对称的计算资源分配（例如，在分布偏移下优先考虑感知处理），支持选择性优化（例如，当感知阶段是端到端性能的瓶颈时，单独改进它），并且通过在较低图像分辨率下运行全局搜索并将高分辨率处理仅分配给选定区域来适应压缩上下文，从而降低总视觉token数量和计算量。在具有挑战性的视觉推理基准测试中，SPARC优于单体基线模型和强大的视觉 grounding 方法。例如，SPARC在$V^*$ VQA基准测试中将Qwen3VL-4B的准确率提高了6.7个百分点，并且在一个具有挑战性的OOD任务中，它超越了“图像思考” 4.6个点，尽管它需要的token预算降低了200倍。

TLDR: The paper introduces SPARC, a modular VLM framework that separates visual perception and reasoning into a two-stage pipeline, enabling test-time scaling, selective optimization, and reduced compute, achieving strong performance on visual reasoning benchmarks.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为SPARC的模块化视觉语言模型框架，该框架将视觉感知和推理分离为两阶段流程，从而实现测试时扩展、选择性优化和降低计算需求，并在视觉推理基准测试中实现了强大的性能。

Authors: Niccolo Avogaro, Nayanika Debnath, Li Mi, Thomas Frick, Junling Wang, Zexue He, Hang Hua, Konrad Schindler, Mattia Rigotti

SeeUPO: Sequence-Level Agentic-RL with Convergence Guarantees

Abstract (English): Reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as the predominant paradigm for training large language model (LLM)-based AI agents. However, existing backbone RL algorithms lack verified convergence guarantees in agentic scenarios, especially in multi-turn settings, which can lead to training instability and failure to converge to optimal policies. In this paper, we systematically analyze how different combinations of policy update mechanisms and advantage estimation methods affect convergence properties in single/multi-turn scenarios. We find that REINFORCE with Group Relative Advantage Estimation (GRAE) can converge to the globally optimal under undiscounted conditions, but the combination of PPO & GRAE breaks PPO's original monotonic improvement property. Furthermore, we demonstrate that mainstream backbone RL algorithms cannot simultaneously achieve both critic-free and convergence guarantees in multi-turn scenarios. To address this, we propose SeeUPO (Sequence-level Sequential Update Policy Optimization), a critic-free approach with convergence guarantees for multi-turn interactions. SeeUPO models multi-turn interaction as sequentially executed multi-agent bandit problems. Through turn-by-turn sequential policy updates in reverse execution order, it ensures monotonic improvement and convergence to global optimal solution via backward induction. Experiments on AppWorld and BFCL v4 demonstrate SeeUPO's substantial improvements over existing backbone algorithms: relative gains of 43.3%-54.6% on Qwen3-14B and 24.1%-41.9% on Qwen2.5-14B (averaged across benchmarks), along with superior training stability.

摘要（中文）: 强化学习（RL）已成为训练基于大型语言模型（LLM）的人工智能代理的主要范例。然而，现有的主干强化学习算法在代理场景中缺乏经过验证的收敛性保证，尤其是在多轮设置中，这可能导致训练不稳定和未能收敛到最佳策略。 在本文中，我们系统地分析了不同的策略更新机制和优势估计方法如何影响单轮/多轮场景中的收敛特性。我们发现，使用分组相对优势估计（GRAE）的REINFORCE算法可以在非折扣条件下收敛到全局最优解，但PPO与GRAE的结合打破了PPO最初的单调改进特性。此外，我们证明了主流主干强化学习算法无法在多轮场景中同时实现无评论家和收敛性保证。 为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种具有多轮交互收敛性保证的无评论家方法：SeeUPO（序列级序贯更新策略优化）。SeeUPO将多轮交互建模为顺序执行的多智能体bandit问题。通过以反向执行顺序逐轮地进行序列策略更新，它利用反向归纳确保了单调改进并收敛到全局最优解。 在AppWorld和BFCL v4上的实验表明，SeeUPO对现有主干算法有显著改进：在Qwen3-14B上相对提升了43.3%-54.6%，在Qwen2.5-14B上相对提升了24.1%-41.9%（跨基准测试的平均值），同时具有卓越的训练稳定性。

TLDR: The paper introduces SeeUPO, a novel critic-free reinforcement learning algorithm with convergence guarantees for LLM-based agents in multi-turn settings, demonstrating significant performance improvements over existing methods. It addresses training instability issues found in mainstream RL algorithms in agentic scenarios.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种名为 SeeUPO 的新型无评论家强化学习算法，该算法为基于大型语言模型（LLM）的智能体在多轮交互中提供了收敛保证，并显示出比现有方法显着的性能改进。它解决了主流 RL 算法在智能体场景中发现的训练不稳定问题。

Authors: Tianyi Hu, Qingxu Fu, Yanxi Chen, Zhaoyang Liu, Bolin Ding

Progress Constraints for Reinforcement Learning in Behavior Trees

Abstract (English): Behavior Trees (BTs) provide a structured and reactive framework for decision-making, commonly used to switch between sub-controllers based on environmental conditions. Reinforcement Learning (RL), on the other hand, can learn near-optimal controllers but sometimes struggles with sparse rewards, safe exploration, and long-horizon credit assignment. Combining BTs with RL has the potential for mutual benefit: a BT design encodes structured domain knowledge that can simplify RL training, while RL enables automatic learning of the controllers within BTs. However, naive integration of BTs and RL can lead to some controllers counteracting other controllers, possibly undoing previously achieved subgoals, thereby degrading the overall performance. To address this, we propose progress constraints, a novel mechanism where feasibility estimators constrain the allowed action set based on theoretical BT convergence results. Empirical evaluations in a 2D proof-of-concept and a high-fidelity warehouse environment demonstrate improved performance, sample efficiency, and constraint satisfaction, compared to prior methods of BT-RL integration.

摘要（中文）: 行为树 (BTs) 为决策提供了一个结构化和反应式的框架，通常用于根据环境条件在子控制器之间切换。另一方面，强化学习 (RL) 可以学习接近最优的控制器，但有时会面临稀疏奖励、安全探索和长时程信用分配的挑战。将 BTs 与 RL 结合具有互惠互利的可能性：BT 设计可以编码结构化的领域知识，从而简化 RL 训练，而 RL 能够自动学习 BTs 内部的控制器。然而，BTs 和 RL 的简单集成可能会导致一些控制器相互对抗，可能撤销先前实现的子目标，从而降低整体性能。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种名为进度约束的新机制，其中可行性估计器根据理论上的 BT 收敛结果来约束允许的动作集。在二维概念验证和高保真仓库环境中的实证评估表明，与以前的 BT-RL 集成方法相比，我们的方法在性能、样本效率和约束满足方面都有所提高。

TLDR: This paper introduces progress constraints for Reinforcement Learning in Behavior Trees to prevent controller counteraction and improve performance, sample efficiency, and constraint satisfaction, demonstrated in 2D and warehouse environments.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种用于行为树中强化学习的进度约束方法，旨在防止控制器之间的相互抵消，并提高性能、样本效率和约束满足度。该方法在2D和仓库环境中得到了验证。

Authors: Finn Rietz, Mart Kartašev, Petter Ögren, Johannes A. Stork

AgentCPM-Explore: Realizing Long-Horizon Deep Exploration for Edge-Scale Agents

Abstract (English): While Large Language Model (LLM)-based agents have shown remarkable potential for solving complex tasks, existing systems remain heavily reliant on large-scale models, leaving the capabilities of edge-scale models largely underexplored. In this paper, we present the first systematic study on training agentic models at the 4B-parameter scale. We identify three primary bottlenecks hindering the performance of edge-scale models: catastrophic forgetting during Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT), sensitivity to reward signal noise during Reinforcement Learning (RL), and reasoning degradation caused by redundant information in long-context scenarios. To address the issues, we propose AgentCPM-Explore, a compact 4B agent model with high knowledge density and strong exploration capability. We introduce a holistic training framework featuring parameter-space model fusion, reward signal denoising, and contextual information refinement. Through deep exploration, AgentCPM-Explore achieves state-of-the-art (SOTA) performance among 4B-class models, matches or surpasses 8B-class SOTA models on four benchmarks, and even outperforms larger-scale models such as Claude-4.5-Sonnet or DeepSeek-v3.2 in five benchmarks. Notably, AgentCPM-Explore achieves 97.09% accuracy on GAIA text-based tasks under pass@64. These results provide compelling evidence that the bottleneck for edge-scale models is not their inherent capability ceiling, but rather their inference stability. Based on our well-established training framework, AgentCPM-Explore effectively unlocks the significant, yet previously underestimated, potential of edge-scale models.

摘要（中文）: 虽然基于大型语言模型（LLM）的智能体在解决复杂任务方面展现出卓越的潜力，但现有系统仍然严重依赖大规模模型，边缘规模模型的能力在很大程度上未被探索。在本文中，我们首次对训练40亿参数规模的智能体模型进行了系统性研究。我们确定了阻碍边缘规模模型性能的三个主要瓶颈：监督微调（SFT）期间的灾难性遗忘、强化学习（RL）期间对奖励信号噪声的敏感性，以及长上下文场景中冗余信息导致的推理退化。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了AgentCPM-Explore，一种紧凑的40亿参数智能体模型，具有高知识密度和强大的探索能力。我们引入了一个整体训练框架，包括参数空间模型融合、奖励信号去噪和上下文信息提炼。通过深度探索，AgentCPM-Explore在40亿参数级别模型中实现了最先进 (SOTA) 的性能，在四个基准测试中匹配或超越了 80 亿参数级别 SOTA 模型，甚至在五个基准测试中优于更大规模的模型，如 Claude-4.5-Sonnet 或 DeepSeek-v3.2。值得注意的是，AgentCPM-Explore在 pass@64 下的 GAIA 基于文本的任务上实现了 97.09% 的准确率。这些结果提供了令人信服的证据，表明边缘规模模型的瓶颈不是其固有的能力上限，而是其推理稳定性。基于我们完善的训练框架，AgentCPM-Explore 有效地释放了边缘规模模型显著但以前被低估的潜力。

TLDR: This paper introduces AgentCPM-Explore, a 4B-parameter agent model with a novel training framework that achieves SOTA performance on several benchmarks, demonstrating the potential of edge-scale models.

简要说明: 本文介绍了AgentCPM-Explore，一个具有新型训练框架的40亿参数规模的代理模型，在多个基准测试上实现了SOTA性能，展示了边缘设备模型的潜力。

Authors: Haotian Chen, Xin Cong, Shengda Fan, Yuyang Fu, Ziqin Gong, Yaxi Lu, Yishan Li, Boye Niu, Chengjun Pan, Zijun Song, Huadong Wang, Yesai Wu, Yueying Wu, Zihao Xie, Yukun Yan, Zhong Zhang, Yankai Lin, Zhiyuan Liu, Maosong Sun

TrajAD: Trajectory Anomaly Detection for Trustworthy LLM Agents

Abstract (English): We address the problem of runtime trajectory anomaly detection, a critical capability for enabling trustworthy LLM agents. Current safety measures predominantly focus on static input/output filtering. However, we argue that ensuring LLM agents reliability requires auditing the intermediate execution process. In this work, we formulate the task of Trajectory Anomaly Detection. The goal is not merely detection, but precise error localization. This capability is essential for enabling efficient rollback-and-retry. To achieve this, we construct TrajBench, a dataset synthesized via a perturb-and-complete strategy to cover diverse procedural anomalies. Using this benchmark, we investigate the capability of models in process supervision. We observe that general-purpose LLMs, even with zero-shot prompting, struggle to identify and localize these anomalies. This reveals that generalized capabilities do not automatically translate to process reliability. To address this, we propose TrajAD, a specialized verifier trained with fine-grained process supervision. Our approach outperforms baselines, demonstrating that specialized supervision is essential for building trustworthy agents.

摘要（中文）: 本文探讨了运行时轨迹异常检测问题，这是实现可信赖的大语言模型 (LLM) 代理的关键能力。当前的安全性措施主要集中在静态的输入/输出过滤上。然而，我们认为确保 LLM 代理的可靠性需要审计中间执行过程。本文正式提出了轨迹异常检测任务。目标不仅是检测，更是精确定位错误。这种能力对于实现高效的回滚重试机制至关重要。为了实现这一目标，我们构建了 TrajBench，一个通过扰动补全策略合成的数据集，以涵盖各种程序性异常。利用这一基准，我们研究了模型在过程监督方面的能力。我们观察到，即使使用零样本提示，通用 LLM 也难以识别和定位这些异常。这表明通用能力并不会自动转化为过程可靠性。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了 TrajAD，一个经过细粒度过程监督训练的专门验证器。我们的方法优于基线方法，证明了专门的监督对于构建可信赖的代理至关重要。

TLDR: The paper introduces TrajAD, a method for runtime anomaly detection in LLM agent trajectories, addressing the limitations of current static safety measures and the poor performance of general LLMs in process supervision. They also introduce TrajBench, a dataset synthesized for this purpose.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了TrajAD，一种用于LLM Agent轨迹运行时异常检测的方法，解决了当前静态安全措施的局限性以及通用LLM在过程监督方面的表现不佳。同时他们引入了TrajBench，一个为此目的合成的数据集。

Authors: Yibing Liu, Chong Zhang, Zhongyi Han, Hansong Liu, Yong Wang, Yang Yu, Xiaoyan Wang, Yilong Yin

TrailBlazer: History-Guided Reinforcement Learning for Black-Box LLM Jailbreaking

Abstract (English): Large Language Models (LLMs) have become integral to many domains, making their safety a critical priority. Prior jailbreaking research has explored diverse approaches, including prompt optimization, automated red teaming, obfuscation, and reinforcement learning (RL) based methods. However, most existing techniques fail to effectively leverage vulnerabilities revealed in earlier interaction turns, resulting in inefficient and unstable attacks. Since jailbreaking involves sequential interactions in which each response influences future actions, reinforcement learning provides a natural framework for this problem. Motivated by this, we propose a history-aware RL-based jailbreak framework that analyzes and reweights vulnerability signals from prior steps to guide future decisions. We show that incorporating historical information alone improves jailbreak success rates. Building on this insight, we introduce an attention-based reweighting mechanism that highlights critical vulnerabilities within the interaction history, enabling more efficient exploration with fewer queries. Extensive experiments on AdvBench and HarmBench demonstrate that our method achieves state-of-the-art jailbreak performance while significantly improving query efficiency. These results underscore the importance of historical vulnerability signals in reinforcement learning-driven jailbreak strategies and offer a principled pathway for advancing adversarial research on LLM safeguards.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型（LLMs）已经成为许多领域不可或缺的一部分，其安全性至关重要。先前的越狱研究已经探索了多种方法，包括提示优化、自动化红队、混淆和基于强化学习（RL）的方法。然而，大多数现有技术未能有效利用在早期交互轮次中暴露的漏洞，导致攻击效率低下且不稳定。由于越狱涉及顺序交互，其中每个响应都会影响未来的行动，因此强化学习为该问题提供了一个自然的框架。受此启发，我们提出了一种历史感知的基于RL的越狱框架，该框架分析并重新加权来自先前步骤的漏洞信号，以指导未来的决策。我们证明，仅纳入历史信息就能提高越狱成功率。基于这一洞察，我们 introduce了一种基于注意力的重新加权机制，该机制突出显示交互历史中的关键漏洞，从而能够以更少的查询进行更有效的探索。在AdvBench和HarmBench上的大量实验表明，我们的方法实现了最先进的越狱性能，同时显著提高了查询效率。这些结果强调了历史漏洞信号在强化学习驱动的越狱策略中的重要性，并为推进LLM安全防护方面的对抗性研究提供了一条有原则的途径。

TLDR: The paper introduces TrailBlazer, a history-aware reinforcement learning framework for jailbreaking LLMs, which leverages vulnerability signals from past interactions to improve jailbreak success rates and query efficiency.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为TrailBlazer的、基于历史信息的强化学习框架，用于破解大型语言模型。该框架利用过去交互中的漏洞信号来提高破解成功率和查询效率。

Authors: Sung-Hoon Yoon, Ruizhi Qian, Minda Zhao, Weiyue Li, Mengyu Wang

MosaicThinker: On-Device Visual Spatial Reasoning for Embodied AI via Iterative Construction of Space Representation

Abstract (English): When embodied AI is expanding from traditional object detection and recognition to more advanced tasks of robot manipulation and actuation planning, visual spatial reasoning from the video inputs is necessary to perceive the spatial relationships of objects and guide device actions. However, existing visual language models (VLMs) have very weak capabilities in spatial reasoning due to the lack of knowledge about 3D spatial information, especially when the reasoning task involve complex spatial relations across multiple video frames. In this paper, we present a new inference-time computing technique for on-device embodied AI, namely \emph{MosaicThinker}, which enhances the on-device small VLM's spatial reasoning capabilities on difficult cross-frame reasoning tasks. Our basic idea is to integrate fragmented spatial information from multiple frames into a unified space representation of global semantic map, and further guide the VLM's spatial reasoning over the semantic map via a visual prompt. Experiment results show that our technique can greatly enhance the accuracy of cross-frame spatial reasoning on resource-constrained embodied AI devices, over reasoning tasks with diverse types and complexities.

摘要（中文）: 当具身人工智能从传统的物体检测和识别扩展到机器人操作和执行规划等更高级的任务时，从视频输入中进行视觉空间推理对于感知物体的空间关系和指导设备动作至关重要。然而，由于缺乏关于3D空间信息的知识，现有的视觉语言模型（VLMs）在空间推理方面能力非常薄弱，尤其是在推理任务涉及跨越多个视频帧的复杂空间关系时。在本文中，我们提出了一种用于端侧具身人工智能的新的推理时计算技术，即{\emph{MosaicThinker}}，它增强了端侧小型VLM在困难的跨帧推理任务上的空间推理能力。我们的基本思想是将来自多个帧的碎片化空间信息整合到全局语义地图的统一空间表示中，并通过视觉提示进一步引导VLM在语义地图上进行空间推理。实验结果表明，我们的技术可以极大地提高资源受限的具身AI设备上跨帧空间推理的准确性，适用于具有不同类型和复杂性的推理任务。

TLDR: The paper introduces MosaicThinker, a method to improve spatial reasoning in VLMs for on-device embodied AI by creating a unified space representation from multiple frames and guiding VLM reasoning with visual prompts.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为 MosaicThinker 的方法，通过从多个帧创建统一的空间表示，并使用视觉提示引导 VLM 推理，来提高 VLM 在设备上进行具身 AI 的空间推理能力。

Authors: Haoming Wang, Qiyao Xue, Weichen Liu, Wei Gao

Trifuse: Enhancing Attention-Based GUI Grounding via Multimodal Fusion

Abstract (English): GUI grounding maps natural language instructions to the correct interface elements, serving as the perception foundation for GUI agents. Existing approaches predominantly rely on fine-tuning multimodal large language models (MLLMs) using large-scale GUI datasets to predict target element coordinates, which is data-intensive and generalizes poorly to unseen interfaces. Recent attention-based alternatives exploit localization signals in MLLMs attention mechanisms without task-specific fine-tuning, but suffer from low reliability due to the lack of explicit and complementary spatial anchors in GUI images. To address this limitation, we propose Trifuse, an attention-based grounding framework that explicitly integrates complementary spatial anchors. Trifuse integrates attention, OCR-derived textual cues, and icon-level caption semantics via a Consensus-SinglePeak (CS) fusion strategy that enforces cross-modal agreement while retaining sharp localization peaks. Extensive evaluations on four grounding benchmarks demonstrate that Trifuse achieves strong performance without task-specific fine-tuning, substantially reducing the reliance on expensive annotated data. Moreover, ablation studies reveal that incorporating OCR and caption cues consistently improves attention-based grounding performance across different backbones, highlighting its effectiveness as a general framework for GUI grounding.

摘要（中文）: GUI接合（Grounding）将自然语言指令映射到正确的界面元素，作为GUI代理的感知基础。现有方法主要依赖于使用大规模GUI数据集对多模态大型语言模型（MLLM）进行微调，以预测目标元素的坐标，但这数据密集，且对未见过界面的泛化能力较差。最近基于注意力机制的替代方案利用MLLM注意力机制中的定位信号，而无需进行特定任务的微调，但由于GUI图像中缺乏明确且互补的空间锚点，导致可靠性较低。为了解决这个局限性，我们提出了Trifuse，一种基于注意力的接合框架，它显式地集成了互补的空间锚点。Trifuse通过共识-单峰（CS）融合策略整合注意力、OCR衍生的文本线索以及图标级描述语义，该策略强制执行跨模态一致性，同时保留清晰的定位峰值。在四个接合基准上的广泛评估表明，Trifuse在没有特定任务微调的情况下实现了强大的性能，大大降低了对昂贵标注数据的依赖。此外，消融研究表明，整合OCR和描述线索能够持续提高基于注意力的接合性能，适用于不同的骨干网络，突显了其作为GUI接合通用框架的有效性。

TLDR: The paper proposes Trifuse, a novel attention-based framework for GUI grounding that integrates attention, OCR, and icon-level caption semantics to improve localization reliability without task-specific fine-tuning, achieving strong performance on several benchmarks.

简要说明: 该论文提出了 Trifuse，一种新颖的基于注意力的 GUI grounding 框架，它整合了注意力机制、OCR 和图标级标题语义，以提高定位可靠性，无需针对特定任务进行微调，并在多个基准测试中取得了良好的性能。

Authors: Longhui Ma, Di Zhao, Siwei Wang, Zhao Lv, Miao Wang

The Optimal Token Baseline: Variance Reduction for Long-Horizon LLM-RL

Abstract (English): Reinforcement Learning (RL) for Large Language Models (LLMs) often suffers from training collapse in long-horizon tasks due to exploding gradient variance. To mitigate this, a baseline is commonly introduced for advantage computation; however, traditional value models remain difficult to optimize, and standard group-based baselines overlook sequence heterogeneity. Although classic optimal baseline theory can achieve global variance reduction, it neglects token heterogeneity and requires prohibitive gradient-based computation. In this work, we derive the Optimal Token Baseline (OTB) from first principles, proving that gradient updates should be weighted inversely to their cumulative gradient norm. To ensure efficiency, we propose the Logit-Gradient Proxy that approximates the gradient norm using only forward-pass probabilities. Our method achieves training stability and matches the performance of large group sizes ($N=32$) with only $N=4$, reducing token consumption by over 65% across single-turn and tool-integrated reasoning tasks.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型（LLMs）的强化学习（RL）由于梯度方差爆炸，经常在长程任务中遭遇训练崩溃。为了缓解这个问题，通常引入基线来计算优势函数；然而，传统价值模型仍然难以优化，并且标准的分组基线忽略了序列异质性。虽然经典的最佳基线理论可以实现全局方差缩减，但它忽略了token异质性，并需要高昂的基于梯度的计算。在这项工作中，我们从第一性原理推导了最佳Token基线（OTB），证明梯度更新应该与其累积梯度范数成反比加权。为了确保效率，我们提出了Logit梯度代理，它仅使用前向传递概率来近似梯度范数。我们的方法实现了训练稳定性，并在单轮和工具集成推理任务中，以仅为N=4的分组大小匹配了大型分组（N=32）的性能，从而减少了超过65%的token消耗。

TLDR: This paper introduces the Optimal Token Baseline (OTB) for LLM-RL, which reduces gradient variance during long-horizon tasks by weighting gradient updates inversely to their cumulative gradient norm, achieving improved training stability and efficiency compared to traditional methods.

简要说明: 本文介绍了用于LLM-RL的Optimal Token Baseline (OTB)，通过对梯度更新进行加权，权重与累积梯度范数成反比，从而降低了长程任务中的梯度方差，与传统方法相比，实现了更好的训练稳定性和效率。

Authors: Yingru Li, Jiawei Xu, Ziniu Li, Jiacai Liu, Wei Liu, Yuxuan Tong, Longtao Zheng, Zhenghai Xue, Yaxiang Zhang, Tianle Cai, Ge Zhang, Qian Liu, Baoxiang Wang

RuleSmith: Multi-Agent LLMs for Automated Game Balancing

Abstract (English): Game balancing is a longstanding challenge requiring repeated playtesting, expert intuition, and extensive manual tuning. We introduce RuleSmith, the first framework that achieves automated game balancing by leveraging the reasoning capabilities of multi-agent LLMs. It couples a game engine, multi-agent LLMs self-play, and Bayesian optimization operating over a multi-dimensional rule space. As a proof of concept, we instantiate RuleSmith on CivMini, a simplified civilization-style game containing heterogeneous factions, economy systems, production rules, and combat mechanics, all governed by tunable parameters. LLM agents interpret textual rulebooks and game states to generate actions, to conduct fast evaluation of balance metrics such as win-rate disparities. To search the parameter landscape efficiently, we integrate Bayesian optimization with acquisition-based adaptive sampling and discrete projection: promising candidates receive more evaluation games for accurate assessment, while exploratory candidates receive fewer games for efficient exploration. Experiments show that RuleSmith converges to highly balanced configurations and provides interpretable rule adjustments that can be directly applied to downstream game systems. Our results illustrate that LLM simulation can serve as a powerful surrogate for automating design and balancing in complex multi-agent environments.

摘要（中文）: 游戏平衡是一个长期存在的挑战，需要反复的试玩、专家直觉和大量的手动调整。我们引入 RuleSmith，这是第一个通过利用多智能体 LLM 的推理能力来实现游戏自动平衡的框架。它将游戏引擎、多智能体 LLM 自博弈以及在多维度规则空间上运行的贝叶斯优化相结合。作为概念验证，我们在 CivMini 上实例化了 RuleSmith，这是一个简化的文明风格游戏，包含异构派系、经济系统、生产规则和战斗机制，所有这些都受可调参数控制。LLM 智能体解释文字规则手册和游戏状态以生成行动，从而快速评估如胜率差异等平衡指标。为了有效地搜索参数空间，我们将贝叶斯优化与基于采集的自适应采样和离散投影相结合：有希望的候选者会收到更多的评估游戏以进行准确评估，而探索性候选者会收到较少的游戏以进行高效探索。实验表明，RuleSmith 收敛于高度平衡的配置，并提供可解释的规则调整，这些调整可以直接应用于下游游戏系统。我们的结果表明，LLM 模拟可以作为自动化复杂多智能体环境中设计和平衡的强大替代方案。

TLDR: RuleSmith uses multi-agent LLMs and Bayesian optimization to automatically balance complex games like CivMini, showing LLMs can simulate and optimize multi-agent environments.

简要说明: RuleSmith 使用多智能体 LLM 和贝叶斯优化来自动平衡像 CivMini 这样复杂的游戏，表明 LLM 可以模拟和优化多智能体环境。
