Authors: Ziyao Zeng, Chen Liu, Tianyu Liu, Hao Wang, Xiatao Sun, Fengyu Yang, Xiaofeng Liu, Zhiwen Fan

Learning Rate Scaling across LoRA Ranks and Transfer to Full Finetuning

Abstract (English): Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) is a standard tool for parameter-efficient finetuning of large models. While it induces a small memory footprint, its training dynamics can be surprisingly complex as they depend on several hyperparameters such as initialization, adapter rank, and learning rate. In particular, it is unclear how the optimal learning rate scales with adapter rank, which forces practitioners to re-tune the learning rate whenever the rank is changed. In this paper, we introduce Maximal-Update Adaptation ($μ$A), a theoretical framework that characterizes how the "optimal" learning rate should scale with model width and adapter rank to produce stable, non-vanishing feature updates under standard configurations. $μ$A is inspired from the Maximal-Update Parametrization ($μ$P) in pretraining. Our analysis leverages techniques from hyperparameter transfer and reveals that the optimal learning rate exhibits different scaling patterns depending on initialization and LoRA scaling factor. Specifically, we identify two regimes: one where the optimal learning rate remains roughly invariant across ranks, and another where it scales inversely with rank. We further identify a configuration that allows learning rate transfer from LoRA to full finetuning, drastically reducing the cost of learning rate tuning for full finetuning. Experiments across language, vision, vision--language, image generation, and reinforcement learning tasks validate our scaling rules and show that learning rates tuned on LoRA transfer reliably to full finetuning.

摘要（中文）: 低秩适配(LoRA)是大型模型参数高效微调的标准工具。虽然它引入了较小的内存占用，但其训练动态可能出人意料地复杂，因为它依赖于诸如初始化、适配器秩和学习率等多个超参数。特别是，目前尚不清楚最佳学习率如何随适配器秩变化，这迫使实践者在每次更改秩时都必须重新调整学习率。在本文中，我们介绍最大更新适配($μ$A)，这是一个理论框架，它描述了“最佳”学习率应如何随模型宽度和适配器秩变化，以在标准配置下产生稳定、非消失的特征更新。$μ$A的灵感来自预训练中的最大更新参数化($μ$P)。我们的分析利用了超参数迁移技术，并且揭示了最佳学习率根据初始化和LoRA缩放因子的不同而表现出不同的缩放模式。具体来说，我们确定了两种情况：一种是最佳学习率在不同秩之间大致不变，另一种是它与秩成反比。我们进一步确定了一种配置，允许从LoRA到全量微调的学习率迁移，从而大大降低了全量微调的学习率调整成本。在语言、视觉、视觉-语言、图像生成和强化学习任务中的实验验证了我们的缩放规则，并表明在LoRA上调整的学习率可以可靠地迁移到全量微调。

TLDR: This paper introduces Maximal-Update Adaptation (μA), a theoretical framework for scaling learning rates with LoRA rank, and identifies configurations for transferring learning rates from LoRA to full finetuning, validated across multiple tasks.

简要说明: 本文提出了最大更新适应（μA），这是一个将学习率与LoRA秩缩放的理论框架，并确定了将学习率从LoRA转移到完整微调的配置，并在多个任务中进行了验证。

Authors: Nan Chen, Soledad Villar, Soufiane Hayou

Self-Improving World Modelling with Latent Actions

Abstract (English): Internal modelling of the world -- predicting transitions between previous states $X$ and next states $Y$ under actions $Z$ -- is essential to reasoning and planning for LLMs and VLMs. Learning such models typically requires costly action-labelled trajectories. We propose SWIRL, a self-improvement framework that learns from state-only sequences by treating actions as a latent variable and alternating between Forward World Modelling (FWM) $P_θ(Y|X,Z)$ and an Inverse Dynamics Modelling (IDM) $Q_φ(Z|X,Y)$. SWIRL iterates two phases: (1) Variational Information Maximisation, which updates the FWM to generate next states that maximise conditional mutual information with latent actions given prior states, encouraging identifiable consistency; and (2) ELBO Maximisation, which updates the IDM to explain observed transitions, effectively performing coordinate ascent. Both models are trained with reinforcement learning (specifically, GRPO) with the opposite frozen model's log-probability as a reward signal. We provide theoretical learnability guarantees for both updates, and evaluate SWIRL on LLMs and VLMs across multiple environments: single-turn and multi-turn open-world visual dynamics and synthetic textual environments for physics, web, and tool calling. SWIRL achieves gains of 16% on AURORABench, 28% on ByteMorph, 16% on WorldPredictionBench, and 14% on StableToolBench.

摘要（中文）: 世界内部建模——即预测在动作 $Z$ 作用下，从先前状态 $X$ 到下一状态 $Y$ 的转移——对于 LLM 和 VLM 的推理和规划至关重要。学习此类模型通常需要耗费巨大的标注动作轨迹。我们提出了 SWIRL，一个自我改进框架，它通过将动作视为潜变量，从仅包含状态的序列中学习，并在前向世界建模 (FWM) $P_θ(Y|X,Z)$ 和逆动力学建模 (IDM) $Q_φ(Z|X,Y)$ 之间交替进行。SWIRL 迭代两个阶段：（1）变分信息最大化，更新 FWM 以生成下一状态，从而最大化给定先前状态的潜变量动作的条件互信息，鼓励可识别一致性；(2) ELBO 最大化，更新 IDM 以解释观察到的转移，有效地执行坐标上升。两个模型都通过强化学习（特别是 GRPO）进行训练，使用相反的冻结模型的对数概率作为奖励信号。我们为这两个更新提供了理论上的可学习性保证，并在横跨多个环境的 LLM 和 VLM 上评估了 SWIRL：单轮和多轮开放世界视觉动力学，以及用于物理、网络和工具调用的合成文本环境。SWIRL 在 AURORABench 上实现了 16% 的增长，在 ByteMorph 上实现了 28% 的增长，在 WorldPredictionBench 上实现了 16% 的增长，在 StableToolBench 上实现了 14% 的增长。

TLDR: The paper introduces SWIRL, a self-improvement framework for learning world models from state-only sequences by alternating between Forward World Modelling (FWM) and Inverse Dynamics Modelling (IDM) using reinforcement learning, showing performance gains across diverse LLM and VLM tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为SWIRL的自提升框架，用于从仅包含状态的序列中学习世界模型。该方法通过交替使用前向世界建模(FWM)和逆动力学建模(IDM)，并结合强化学习，在各种LLM和VLM任务中表现出性能提升。

Authors: Yifu Qiu, Zheng Zhao, Waylon Li, Yftah Ziser, Anna Korhonen, Shay B. Cohen, Edoardo M. Ponti

DyTopo: Dynamic Topology Routing for Multi-Agent Reasoning via Semantic Matching

Abstract (English): Multi-agent systems built from prompted large language models can improve multi-round reasoning, yet most existing pipelines rely on fixed, trajectory-wide communication patterns that are poorly matched to the stage-dependent needs of iterative problem solving. We introduce DyTopo, a manager-guided multi-agent framework that reconstructs a sparse directed communication graph at each round. Conditioned on the manager's round goal, each agent outputs lightweight natural-language query (need) and \key (offer) descriptors; DyTopo embeds these descriptors and performs semantic matching, routing private messages only along the induced edges. Across code generation and mathematical reasoning benchmarks and four LLM backbones, DyTopo consistently outperforms over the strongest baseline (avg. +6.2). Beyond accuracy, DyTopo yields an interpretable coordination trace via the evolving graphs, enabling qualitative inspection of how communication pathways reconfigure across rounds.

摘要（中文）: 由提示的大型语言模型构建的多智能体系统能够提升多轮推理能力，然而，现有的大部分流程依赖于固定的、贯穿整个轨迹的通信模式，这与迭代问题求解中阶段相关的需求不匹配。我们引入了 DyTopo，一种由管理器引导的多智能体框架，它在每一轮次重构一个稀疏的有向通信图。基于管理器设定的轮次目标，每个智能体输出轻量级的自然语言查询（需求）和\关键词（供应）描述符；DyTopo 会嵌入这些描述符并执行语义匹配，仅沿着诱导的边路由私有消息。在代码生成和数学推理基准测试以及四个大型语言模型后端上，DyTopo 始终优于最强的基线（平均 +6.2）。除了准确率之外，DyTopo 还通过不断演化的图产生可解释的协调轨迹，从而能够对通信路径如何在各个轮次之间重新配置进行定性检查。

TLDR: The paper introduces DyTopo, a manager-guided multi-agent framework using semantic matching to dynamically reconstruct a sparse communication graph at each round for improved multi-agent reasoning, demonstrating superior performance on code generation and mathematical reasoning tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了DyTopo，一个由管理者引导的多智能体框架，它利用语义匹配在每一轮动态地重建一个稀疏的通信图，以提高多智能体推理的能力。实验表明，该框架在代码生成和数学推理任务上具有优越的性能。

Authors: Yuxing Lu, Yucheng Hu, Xukai Zhao, Jiuxin Cao

Learning Query-Aware Budget-Tier Routing for Runtime Agent Memory

Abstract (English): Memory is increasingly central to Large Language Model (LLM) agents operating beyond a single context window, yet most existing systems rely on offline, query-agnostic memory construction that can be inefficient and may discard query-critical information. Although runtime memory utilization is a natural alternative, prior work often incurs substantial overhead and offers limited explicit control over the performance-cost trade-off. In this work, we present \textbf{BudgetMem}, a runtime agent memory framework for explicit, query-aware performance-cost control. BudgetMem structures memory processing as a set of memory modules, each offered in three budget tiers (i.e., \textsc{Low}/\textsc{Mid}/\textsc{High}). A lightweight router performs budget-tier routing across modules to balance task performance and memory construction cost, which is implemented as a compact neural policy trained with reinforcement learning. Using BudgetMem as a unified testbed, we study three complementary strategies for realizing budget tiers: implementation (method complexity), reasoning (inference behavior), and capacity (module model size). Across LoCoMo, LongMemEval, and HotpotQA, BudgetMem surpasses strong baselines when performance is prioritized (i.e., high-budget setting), and delivers better accuracy-cost frontiers under tighter budgets. Moreover, our analysis disentangles the strengths and weaknesses of different tiering strategies, clarifying when each axis delivers the most favorable trade-offs under varying budget regimes.

摘要（中文）: 记忆对于在单个上下文窗口之外运行的大型语言模型 (LLM) 代理变得日益重要，但现有的大多数系统依赖于离线、与查询无关的记忆构建方法，这种方法效率低下，并且可能丢弃对查询至关重要的信息。虽然运行时记忆利用是一种自然的替代方案，但之前的工作常常产生大量的开销，并且对性能-成本的权衡提供有限的显式控制。在这项工作中，我们提出了 \textbf{BudgetMem}，一个用于显式、查询感知的性能-成本控制的运行时代理记忆框架。BudgetMem 将记忆处理构建为一组记忆模块，每个模块提供三个预算等级（即 \textsc{Low}/\textsc{Mid}/\textsc{High}）。一个轻量级的路由器执行跨模块的预算等级路由，以平衡任务性能和记忆构建成本，该路由器被实现为一个使用强化学习训练的紧凑型神经网络策略。我们将 BudgetMem 作为一个统一的测试平台，研究了实现预算等级的三个互补策略：实现（方法复杂度）、推理（推理行为）和容量（模块模型大小）。在 LoCoMo、LongMemEval 和 HotpotQA 上，当性能优先时（即高预算设置），BudgetMem 超越了强大的基线，并且在更严格的预算下提供了更好的准确率-成本前沿。此外，我们的分析解开了不同分层策略的优点和缺点，阐明了在不同的预算机制下，每个维度何时能提供最有利的权衡。

TLDR: The paper introduces BudgetMem, a runtime agent memory framework that uses reinforcement learning to dynamically allocate memory resources based on query relevance and budget constraints, achieving better performance-cost trade-offs in LLM agents.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了BudgetMem，一个运行时代理内存框架，它使用强化学习根据查询相关性和预算约束动态分配内存资源，从而在LLM代理中实现更好的性能-成本权衡。

Authors: Haozhen Zhang, Haodong Yue, Tao Feng, Quanyu Long, Jianzhu Bao, Bowen Jin, Weizhi Zhang, Xiao Li, Jiaxuan You, Chengwei Qin, Wenya Wang

Jackpot: Optimal Budgeted Rejection Sampling for Extreme Actor-Policy Mismatch Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Reinforcement learning (RL) for large language models (LLMs) remains expensive, particularly because the rollout is expensive. Decoupling rollout generation from policy optimization (e.g., leveraging a more efficient model to rollout) could enable substantial efficiency gains, yet doing so introduces a severe distribution mismatch that destabilizes learning. We propose Jackpot, a framework that leverages Optimal Budget Rejection Sampling (OBRS) to directly reduce the discrepancy between the rollout model and the evolving policy. Jackpot integrates a principled OBRS procedure, a unified training objective that jointly updates the policy and rollout models, and an efficient system implementation enabled by top-$k$ probability estimation and batch-level bias correction. Our theoretical analysis shows that OBRS consistently moves the rollout distribution closer to the target distribution under a controllable acceptance budget. Empirically, \sys substantially improves training stability compared to importance-sampling baselines, achieving performance comparable to on-policy RL when training Qwen3-8B-Base for up to 300 update steps of batchsize 64. Taken together, our results show that OBRS-based alignment brings us a step closer to practical and effective decoupling of rollout generation from policy optimization for RL for LLMs.

摘要（中文）: 针对大型语言模型 (LLM) 的强化学习 (RL) 仍然成本高昂，尤其是由于 rollout 过程的耗费巨大。将 rollout 生成与策略优化解耦（例如，利用更高效的模型进行 rollout）可以带来显著的效率提升，然而这样做会引入严重的分布不匹配，从而导致学习不稳定。我们提出了 Jackpot，一种利用最优预算拒绝采样 (OBRS) 直接减少 rollout 模型与演化策略之间差异的框架。Jackpot 集成了一个基于原则的 OBRS 程序、一个联合更新策略和 rollout 模型的统一训练目标，以及一个通过 top-$k$ 概率估计和批次级偏差校正实现的高效系统实现。我们的理论分析表明，OBRS 在可控的接受预算下始终能使 rollout 分布更接近目标分布。实验结果表明，相比于基于重要性采样的基线方法，\sys 显著提高了训练稳定性，在使用批大小为 64 的 Qwen3-8B-Base 进行最多 300 步更新时，实现了与在线策略 RL 相当的性能。总而言之，我们的结果表明，基于 OBRS 的对齐使我们朝着 LLM 的 RL 中 rollout 生成与策略优化的实际且有效的解耦迈进了一步。

TLDR: This paper introduces Jackpot, a reinforcement learning framework that uses Optimal Budget Rejection Sampling (OBRS) to address the distribution mismatch problem when decoupling rollout generation from policy optimization in LLMs, achieving improved training stability.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Jackpot，一个强化学习框架，它使用最优预算拒绝采样(OBRS)来解决LLM中将 rollout 生成与策略优化分离时出现的分布不匹配问题，从而提高了训练稳定性。

Authors: Zhuoming Chen, Hongyi Liu, Yang Zhou, Haizhong Zheng, Beidi Chen

PlanViz: Evaluating Planning-Oriented Image Generation and Editing for Computer-Use Tasks

Abstract (English): Unified multimodal models (UMMs) have shown impressive capabilities in generating natural images and supporting multimodal reasoning. However, their potential in supporting computer-use planning tasks, which are closely related to our lives, remain underexplored. Image generation and editing in computer-use tasks require capabilities like spatial reasoning and procedural understanding, and it is still unknown whether UMMs have these capabilities to finish these tasks or not. Therefore, we propose PlanViz, a new benchmark designed to evaluate image generation and editing for computer-use tasks. To achieve the goal of our evaluation, we focus on sub-tasks which frequently involve in daily life and require planning steps. Specifically, three new sub-tasks are designed: route planning, work diagramming, and web&UI displaying. We address challenges in data quality ensuring by curating human-annotated questions and reference images, and a quality control process. For challenges of comprehensive and exact evaluation, a task-adaptive score, PlanScore, is proposed. The score helps understanding the correctness, visual quality and efficiency of generated images. Through experiments, we highlight key limitations and opportunities for future research on this topic.

摘要（中文）: 统一多模态模型（UMMs）在生成自然图像和支持多模态推理方面表现出令人印象深刻的能力。然而，它们在支持计算机使用规划任务方面的潜力，即与我们的生活密切相关的任务，仍未得到充分探索。计算机使用任务中的图像生成和编辑需要空间推理和程序理解等能力，而UMMs是否具备完成这些任务的能力仍然未知。因此，我们提出了PlanViz，这是一个新的基准，旨在评估计算机使用任务中的图像生成和编辑。为了实现我们的评估目标，我们专注于日常生活中经常涉及并需要规划步骤的子任务。具体而言，我们设计了三个新的子任务：路线规划、工作流程图绘制和网页&UI显示。我们通过收集人工标注的问题和参考图像，并采用质量控制流程，来应对数据质量保证方面的挑战。针对全面而精确的评估挑战，我们提出了一种任务自适应评分方法PlanScore。该评分方法有助于理解生成图像的正确性、视觉质量和效率。通过实验，我们强调了该主题未来研究中的关键局限性与机遇。

TLDR: The paper introduces PlanViz, a new benchmark for evaluating the ability of unified multimodal models to generate and edit images for computer-use tasks requiring spatial reasoning and procedural understanding, focusing on route planning, work diagramming, and web&UI displaying.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一个新的基准测试PlanViz，用于评估统一多模态模型在为计算机使用任务生成和编辑图像方面的能力，这些任务需要空间推理和程序理解，重点是路线规划、工作图表和Web&UI显示。

CauCLIP: Bridging the Sim-to-Real Gap in Surgical Video Understanding via Causality-Inspired Vision-Language Modeling

Abstract (English): Surgical phase recognition is a critical component for context-aware decision support in intelligent operating rooms, yet training robust models is hindered by limited annotated clinical videos and large domain gaps between synthetic and real surgical data. To address this, we propose CauCLIP, a causality-inspired vision-language framework that leverages CLIP to learn domain-invariant representations for surgical phase recognition without access to target domain data. Our approach integrates a frequency-based augmentation strategy to perturb domain-specific attributes while preserving semantic structures, and a causal suppression loss that mitigates non-causal biases and reinforces causal surgical features. These components are combined in a unified training framework that enables the model to focus on stable causal factors underlying surgical workflows. Experiments on the SurgVisDom hard adaptation benchmark demonstrate that our method substantially outperforms all competing approaches, highlighting the effectiveness of causality-guided vision-language models for domain-generalizable surgical video understanding.

摘要（中文）: 手术阶段识别是智能手术室中上下文感知决策支持的关键组成部分，然而，训练稳健的模型受到带标注的临床视频数据有限以及合成手术数据与真实手术数据之间存在巨大领域差异的阻碍。为了解决这个问题，我们提出CauCLIP，一个受因果关系启发的视觉-语言框架，它利用CLIP学习领域不变表示，用于手术阶段识别，且无需访问目标领域数据。我们的方法集成了一种基于频率的增强策略，用于扰动领域特定的属性，同时保持语义结构；以及一个因果抑制损失，用于缓解非因果性偏差并强化因果性手术特征。这些组件被整合到一个统一的训练框架中，使模型能够专注于手术工作流程中稳定的因果因素。在SurgVisDom硬适应基准上的实验表明，我们的方法显著优于所有竞争方法，突出了因果关系引导的视觉-语言模型在领域泛化的手术视频理解中的有效性。

TLDR: CauCLIP uses a causality-inspired vision-language approach with frequency-based augmentation and causal suppression loss to improve surgical phase recognition by leveraging CLIP for domain-invariant representations, achieving state-of-the-art performance on a hard adaptation benchmark.

简要说明: CauCLIP 采用了一种因果关系启发的视觉语言方法，结合基于频率的增强和因果抑制损失，利用 CLIP 学习领域不变的表示，从而提高手术阶段识别能力，并在一个困难的适应性基准上实现了最先进的性能。

Authors: Yuxin He, An Li, Cheng Xue

LAB-Det: Language as a Domain-Invariant Bridge for Training-Free One-Shot Domain Generalization in Object Detection

Abstract (English): Foundation object detectors such as GLIP and Grounding DINO excel on general-domain data but often degrade in specialized and data-scarce settings like underwater imagery or industrial defects. Typical cross-domain few-shot approaches rely on fine-tuning scarce target data, incurring cost and overfitting risks. We instead ask: Can a frozen detector adapt with only one exemplar per class without training? To answer this, we introduce training-free one-shot domain generalization for object detection, where detectors must adapt to specialized domains with only one annotated exemplar per class and no weight updates. To tackle this task, we propose LAB-Det, which exploits Language As a domain-invariant Bridge. Instead of adapting visual features, we project each exemplar into a descriptive text that conditions and guides a frozen detector. This linguistic conditioning replaces gradient-based adaptation, enabling robust generalization in data-scarce domains. We evaluate on UODD (underwater) and NEU-DET (industrial defects), two widely adopted benchmarks for data-scarce detection, where object boundaries are often ambiguous, and LAB-Det achieves up to 5.4 mAP improvement over state-of-the-art fine-tuned baselines without updating a single parameter. These results establish linguistic adaptation as an efficient and interpretable alternative to fine-tuning in specialized detection settings.

摘要（中文）: 诸如GLIP和Grounding DINO的基础目标检测器在通用领域数据上表现出色，但在水下图像或工业缺陷等专业化和数据稀缺的环境中，性能通常会下降。典型的跨域少样本方法依赖于对稀缺的目标数据进行微调，从而产生开销和过拟合风险。我们转而提出疑问：是否可以在不进行训练的情况下，仅用每个类别的一个样本让一个冻结的检测器进行适应？为了回答这个问题，我们引入了一种免训练的单样本域泛化目标检测方法，其中检测器必须适应专业领域，每个类别仅有一个带标注的样本，且没有权重更新。为了解决这个任务，我们提出了LAB-Det，它利用语言作为一种领域不变的桥梁。LAB-Det不适应视觉特征，而是将每个样本投影到一个描述性的文本中，这个文本对冻结的检测器进行条件约束和引导。这种语言条件约束取代了基于梯度的适应，从而在数据稀缺的领域中实现鲁棒的泛化。我们在UODD（水下）和NEU-DET（工业缺陷）这两个广泛采用的数据稀缺检测基准上进行了评估，这些基准中目标边界通常是模糊的，LAB-Det在不更新任何参数的情况下，实现了比最先进的微调基线最多5.4 mAP的提升。这些结果确立了在专业检测环境中，语言适应是微调的一种高效且可解释的替代方案。

TLDR: The paper introduces LAB-Det, a training-free one-shot domain generalization method for object detection that leverages language as a domain-invariant bridge to adapt a frozen detector to specialized domains with only one annotated exemplar per class, achieving improved mAP over fine-tuned baselines.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了LAB-Det，一种无需训练的单样本域泛化目标检测方法，它利用语言作为领域不变的桥梁，使冻结的检测器能够适应特定领域，每个类别仅需一个带注释的样本，并且比微调的基线实现了改进的mAP。

Authors: Xu Zhang, Zhe Chen, Jing Zhang, Dacheng Tao

POINTS-GUI-G: GUI-Grounding Journey

Abstract (English): The rapid advancement of vision-language models has catalyzed the emergence of GUI agents, which hold immense potential for automating complex tasks, from online shopping to flight booking, thereby alleviating the burden of repetitive digital workflows. As a foundational capability, GUI grounding is typically established as a prerequisite for end-to-end task execution. It enables models to precisely locate interface elements, such as text and icons, to perform accurate operations like clicking and typing. Unlike prior works that fine-tune models already possessing strong spatial awareness (e.g., Qwen3-VL), we aim to master the full technical pipeline by starting from a base model with minimal grounding ability, such as POINTS-1.5. We introduce POINTS-GUI-G-8B, which achieves state-of-the-art performance with scores of 59.9 on ScreenSpot-Pro, 66.0 on OSWorld-G, 95.7 on ScreenSpot-v2, and 49.9 on UI-Vision. Our model's success is driven by three key factors: (1) Refined Data Engineering, involving the unification of diverse open-source datasets format alongside sophisticated strategies for augmentation, filtering, and difficulty grading; (2) Improved Training Strategies, including continuous fine-tuning of the vision encoder to enhance perceptual accuracy and maintaining resolution consistency between training and inference; and (3) Reinforcement Learning (RL) with Verifiable Rewards. While RL is traditionally used to bolster reasoning, we demonstrate that it significantly improves precision in the perception-intensive GUI grounding task. Furthermore, GUI grounding provides a natural advantage for RL, as rewards are easily verifiable and highly accurate.

摘要（中文）: 视觉-语言模型的快速发展催化了图形用户界面代理的出现，这些代理在自动化复杂任务（从在线购物到机票预订）方面具有巨大的潜力，从而减轻了重复性数字工作流程的负担。作为一项基础能力，GUI定位通常被确立为端到端任务执行的先决条件。它使模型能够精确定位界面元素，如文本和图标，以执行诸如点击和打字等精确操作。与以往微调已经具有强大空间感知能力的模型（例如，Qwen3-VL）的研究不同，我们旨在通过从一个具有最少定位能力的基础模型（例如，POINTS-1.5）开始，来掌握完整的技术流程。我们推出了POINTS-GUI-G-8B，它实现了最先进的性能，在ScreenSpot-Pro上的得分为59.9，在OSWorld-G上的得分为66.0，在ScreenSpot-v2上的得分为95.7，在UI-Vision上的得分为49.9。我们模型的成功归功于三个关键因素：（1）精细的数据工程，包括统一各种开源数据集格式，以及复杂的增强、过滤和难度分级策略；（2）改进的训练策略，包括持续微调视觉编码器以提高感知精度，并在训练和推理之间保持分辨率一致性；（3）带有可验证奖励的强化学习（RL）。虽然RL传统上用于增强推理能力，但我们证明它可以显著提高感知密集型的GUI定位任务的精度。此外，GUI定位为RL提供了一个天然的优势，因为奖励易于验证并且高度准确。

TLDR: The paper introduces POINTS-GUI-G-8B, a GUI grounding model built from a base model (POINTS-1.5) with minimal initial grounding ability. It utilizes refined data engineering, improved training strategies (including vision encoder fine-tuning and resolution consistency), and reinforcement learning to achieve state-of-the-art performance on several GUI grounding benchmarks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了POINTS-GUI-G-8B，一个GUI定位模型，它从一个初始定位能力很弱的基础模型(POINTS-1.5)构建而来。该模型利用精炼的数据工程、改进的训练策略(包括视觉编码器微调和分辨率一致性)以及强化学习，在多个GUI定位基准测试中实现了最先进的性能。

Authors: Zhongyin Zhao, Yuan Liu, Yikun Liu, Haicheng Wang, Le Tian, Xiao Zhou, Yangxiu You, Zilin Yu, Yang Yu, Jie Zhou

Driving with DINO: Vision Foundation Features as a Unified Bridge for Sim-to-Real Generation in Autonomous Driving

Abstract (English): Driven by the emergence of Controllable Video Diffusion, existing Sim2Real methods for autonomous driving video generation typically rely on explicit intermediate representations to bridge the domain gap. However, these modalities face a fundamental Consistency-Realism Dilemma. Low-level signals (e.g., edges, blurred images) ensure precise control but compromise realism by "baking in" synthetic artifacts, whereas high-level priors (e.g., depth, semantics, HDMaps) facilitate photorealism but lack the structural detail required for consistent guidance. In this work, we present Driving with DINO (DwD), a novel framework that leverages Vision Foundation Module (VFM) features as a unified bridge between the simulation and real-world domains. We first identify that these features encode a spectrum of information, from high-level semantics to fine-grained structure. To effectively utilize this, we employ Principal Subspace Projection to discard the high-frequency elements responsible for "texture baking," while concurrently introducing Random Channel Tail Drop to mitigate the structural loss inherent in rigid dimensionality reduction, thereby reconciling realism with control consistency. Furthermore, to fully leverage DINOv3's high-resolution capabilities for enhancing control precision, we introduce a learnable Spatial Alignment Module that adapts these high-resolution features to the diffusion backbone. Finally, we propose a Causal Temporal Aggregator employing causal convolutions to explicitly preserve historical motion context when integrating frame-wise DINO features, which effectively mitigates motion blur and guarantees temporal stability. Project page: https://albertchen98.github.io/DwD-project/

摘要（中文）: 受控视频扩散技术的兴起推动了自动驾驶视频生成的现有Sim2Real方法，这些方法通常依赖于显式的中间表示来弥合领域差距。然而，这些模式面临着一个根本性的“一致性-真实性困境”。低层次信号（例如，边缘、模糊图像）确保了精确的控制，但通过“烘焙”合成伪影损害了真实性，而高层次先验（例如，深度、语义、高清地图）有助于照片般的真实感，但缺乏一致性引导所需的结构细节。在这项工作中，我们提出了“基于DINO的驾驶”（DwD），这是一种新颖的框架，利用视觉基础模块（VFM）特征作为仿真和真实世界领域之间的统一桥梁。我们首先确定这些特征编码着一系列信息，从高层次语义到精细结构。为了有效地利用这一点，我们采用主子空间投影来丢弃负责“纹理烘焙”的高频元素，同时引入随机通道尾部丢弃，以减轻刚性降维中固有的结构损失，从而协调真实性和控制一致性。此外，为了充分利用DINOv3的高分辨率能力来增强控制精度，我们引入了一个可学习的空间对齐模块，该模块将这些高分辨率特征适配到扩散骨干网络。最后，我们提出了一个因果时间聚合器，该聚合器采用因果卷积来显式地保留历史运动上下文，以便在集成逐帧DINO特征时，从而有效地减轻运动模糊并保证时间稳定性。项目主页：https://albertchen98.github.io/DwD-project/

TLDR: The paper introduces Driving with DINO (DwD), a novel Sim2Real video generation framework for autonomous driving that leverages Vision Foundation Module (VFM) features from DINO as a unified bridge, using techniques to reconcile realism with control consistency and enhance control precision and temporal stability.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Driving with DINO (DwD)，一个新颖的Sim2Real自动驾驶视频生成框架，该框架利用DINO的视觉基础模块(VFM)特征作为一个统一的桥梁，并采用多种技术来协调真实感与控制一致性，同时增强控制精度和时间稳定性。

Authors: Xuyang Chen, Conglang Zhang, Chuanheng Fu, Zihao Yang, Kaixuan Zhou, Yizhi Zhang, Jianan He, Yanfeng Zhang, Mingwei Sun, Zengmao Wang, Zhen Dong, Xiaoxiao Long, Liqiu Meng

EgoAVU: Egocentric Audio-Visual Understanding

Abstract (English): Understanding egocentric videos plays a vital role for embodied intelligence. Recent multi-modal large language models (MLLMs) can accept both visual and audio inputs. However, due to the challenge of obtaining text labels with coherent joint-modality information, whether MLLMs can jointly understand both modalities in egocentric videos remains under-explored. To address this problem, we introduce EgoAVU, a scalable data engine to automatically generate egocentric audio-visual narrations, questions, and answers. EgoAVU enriches human narrations with multimodal context and generates audio-visual narrations through cross-modal correlation modeling. Token-based video filtering and modular, graph-based curation ensure both data diversity and quality. Leveraging EgoAVU, we construct EgoAVU-Instruct, a large-scale training dataset of 3M samples, and EgoAVU-Bench, a manually verified evaluation split covering diverse tasks. EgoAVU-Bench clearly reveals the limitations of existing MLLMs: they bias heavily toward visual signals, often neglecting audio cues or failing to correspond audio with the visual source. Finetuning MLLMs on EgoAVU-Instruct effectively addresses this issue, enabling up to 113% performance improvement on EgoAVU-Bench. Such benefits also transfer to other benchmarks such as EgoTempo and EgoIllusion, achieving up to 28% relative performance gain. Code will be released to the community.

摘要（中文）: 理解以自我为中心的视频对于具身智能至关重要。 近期多模态大型语言模型（MLLMs）可以接受视觉和音频输入。 然而，由于获取具有连贯联合模态信息的文本标签存在挑战，MLLMs是否能联合理解以自我为中心的视频中的两种模态仍有待探索。 为了解决这个问题，我们引入了EgoAVU，一个可扩展的数据引擎，用于自动生成以自我为中心的音视频叙述、问题和答案。 EgoAVU通过多模态上下文丰富人类叙述，并通过跨模态相关性建模生成音视频叙述。 基于令牌的视频过滤和模块化的、基于图的整理确保了数据的多样性和质量。 利用EgoAVU，我们构建了EgoAVU-Instruct，一个包含300万个样本的大规模训练数据集，以及EgoAVU-Bench，一个涵盖各种任务的手动验证评估集。 EgoAVU-Bench清晰地揭示了现有MLLMs的局限性：它们严重偏向视觉信号，经常忽略音频线索或无法将音频与视觉来源对应。 在EgoAVU-Instruct上微调MLLMs有效解决了这个问题，从而在EgoAVU-Bench上实现了高达113%的性能提升。 这种优势也转移到了其他基准测试，例如EgoTempo和EgoIllusion，实现了高达28%的相对性能提升。 代码将向社区发布。

TLDR: The paper introduces EgoAVU, a data engine for generating egocentric audio-visual datasets for training and evaluating MLLMs and demonstrates finetuning on the generated dataset improves MLLM performance in understanding audio-visual cues in egocentric videos.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了EgoAVU，一个用于生成以自我为中心的音频-视觉数据集的数据引擎，用于训练和评估MLLM，并证明在生成的数据集上进行微调可以提高MLLM在理解以自我为中心的视频中的音频-视觉线索方面的性能。

Authors: Ashish Seth, Xinhao Mei, Changsheng Zhao, Varun Nagaraja, Ernie Chang, Gregory P. Meyer, Gael Le Lan, Yunyang Xiong, Vikas Chandra, Yangyang Shi, Dinesh Manocha, Zhipeng Cai

Predicting Camera Pose from Perspective Descriptions for Spatial Reasoning

Abstract (English): Multi-image spatial reasoning remains challenging for current multimodal large language models (MLLMs). While single-view perception is inherently 2D, reasoning over multiple views requires building a coherent scene understanding across viewpoints. In particular, we study perspective taking, where a model must build a coherent 3D understanding from multi-view observations and use it to reason from a new, language-specified viewpoint. We introduce CAMCUE, a pose-aware multi-image framework that uses camera pose as an explicit geometric anchor for cross-view fusion and novel-view reasoning. CAMCUE injects per-view pose into visual tokens, grounds natural-language viewpoint descriptions to a target camera pose, and synthesizes a pose-conditioned imagined target view to support answering. To support this setting, we curate CAMCUE-DATA with 27,668 training and 508 test instances pairing multi-view images and poses with diverse target-viewpoint descriptions and perspective-shift questions. We also include human-annotated viewpoint descriptions in the test split to evaluate generalization to human language. CAMCUE improves overall accuracy by 9.06% and predicts target poses from natural-language viewpoint descriptions with over 90% rotation accuracy within 20° and translation accuracy within a 0.5 error threshold. This direct grounding avoids expensive test-time search-and-match, reducing inference time from 256.6s to 1.45s per example and enabling fast, interactive use in real-world scenarios.

摘要（中文）: 多图像空间推理对于当前的多模态大型语言模型(MLLMs)来说仍然具有挑战性。单视角的感知本质上是二维的，而对多个视角的推理需要跨视角构建连贯的场景理解。特别是，我们研究了透视转换，即模型必须从多视角观察中建立连贯的三维理解，并用它来从新的、语言指定的视点进行推理。我们提出了CAMCUE，一个姿态感知的多图像框架，它使用相机姿态作为明确的几何锚点，进行跨视图融合和新视图推理。CAMCUE将每个视角的姿态注入视觉标记中，将自然语言的视点描述与目标相机姿态关联起来，并合成一个姿态条件下的想象目标视图以支持回答。为了支持这个设置，我们整理了CAMCUE-DATA，其中包含27,668个训练实例和508个测试实例，它们将多视角图像和姿态与不同的目标视点描述和透视转换问题配对。我们还在测试集中包含了人工标注的视点描述，以评估对人类语言的泛化能力。CAMCUE将总体准确率提高了9.06%，并能根据自然语言视点描述预测目标姿态，其旋转精度在20°以内超过90%，平移精度在0.5误差阈值内。这种直接关联避免了昂贵的测试时搜索匹配，将每个示例的推理时间从256.6秒减少到1.45秒，从而能够在现实场景中实现快速、交互式的使用。

TLDR: The paper introduces CAMCUE, a pose-aware multi-image framework using camera pose as a geometric anchor for cross-view fusion, enabling novel-view reasoning and achieving state-of-the-art results in predicting camera pose from perspective descriptions.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了CAMCUE，一个姿态感知的多图像框架，它使用相机姿态作为几何锚点来进行跨视图融合，从而实现新视角推理，并在从视角描述预测相机姿态方面取得了最先进的结果。

Authors: Xuejun Zhang, Aditi Tiwari, Zhenhailong Wang, Heng Ji

Thinking with Geometry: Active Geometry Integration for Spatial Reasoning

Abstract (English): Recent progress in spatial reasoning with Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) increasingly leverages geometric priors from 3D encoders. However, most existing integration strategies remain passive: geometry is exposed as a global stream and fused in an indiscriminate manner, which often induces semantic-geometry misalignment and redundant signals. We propose GeoThinker, a framework that shifts the paradigm from passive fusion to active perception. Instead of feature mixing, GeoThinker enables the model to selectively retrieve geometric evidence conditioned on its internal reasoning demands. GeoThinker achieves this through Spatial-Grounded Fusion applied at carefully selected VLM layers, where semantic visual priors selectively query and integrate task-relevant geometry via frame-strict cross-attention, further calibrated by Importance Gating that biases per-frame attention toward task-relevant structures. Comprehensive evaluation results show that GeoThinker sets a new state-of-the-art in spatial intelligence, achieving a peak score of 72.6 on the VSI-Bench. Furthermore, GeoThinker demonstrates robust generalization and significantly improved spatial perception across complex downstream scenarios, including embodied referring and autonomous driving. Our results indicate that the ability to actively integrate spatial structures is essential for next-generation spatial intelligence. Code can be found at https://github.com/Li-Hao-yuan/GeoThinker.

摘要（中文）: 多模态大型语言模型(MLLMs)在空间推理方面的最新进展越来越多地利用来自3D编码器的几何先验。然而，目前大多数的集成策略仍然是被动的：几何信息被作为全局流暴露出来并以不加区分的方式融合，这常常会导致语义-几何对齐偏差和冗余信号。我们提出了GeoThinker，一个将范式从被动融合转变为主动感知的框架。GeoThinker并非进行特征混合，而是使模型能够根据其内部推理需求选择性地检索几何证据。 GeoThinker通过在精心选择的VLM层应用空间对齐融合来实现这一点，在此过程中，语义视觉先验通过帧严格交叉注意力选择性地查询和集成任务相关的几何信息，并通过重要性门控进一步校准，从而将每帧注意力偏向于任务相关的结构。全面评估结果表明，GeoThinker在空间智能方面建立了新的技术水平，在VSI-Bench上实现了高达72.6的峰值分数。此外，GeoThinker展示了强大的泛化能力，并显著提高了复杂下游场景中的空间感知能力，包括具身指代和自动驾驶。我们的结果表明，主动集成空间结构的能力对于下一代空间智能至关重要。代码可在https://github.com/Li-Hao-yuan/GeoThinker找到。

TLDR: The paper introduces GeoThinker, a framework for MLLMs that actively integrates geometric information for spatial reasoning using spatial-grounded fusion and importance gating, achieving state-of-the-art performance on spatial intelligence benchmarks and demonstrating improved generalization in complex scenarios.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了GeoThinker，一个用于多模态大型语言模型的框架，通过空间锚定融合和重要性门控主动整合几何信息以进行空间推理，在空间智能基准测试中实现了最先进的性能，并在复杂的场景中展示了更好的泛化能力。

Authors: Haoyuan Li, Qihang Cao, Tao Tang, Kun Xiang, Zihan Guo, Jianhua Han, Hang Xu, Xiaodan Liang

V-Retrver: Evidence-Driven Agentic Reasoning for Universal Multimodal Retrieval

Abstract (English): Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have recently been applied to universal multimodal retrieval, where Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning improves candidate reranking. However, existing approaches remain largely language-driven, relying on static visual encodings and lacking the ability to actively verify fine-grained visual evidence, which often leads to speculative reasoning in visually ambiguous cases. We propose V-Retrver, an evidence-driven retrieval framework that reformulates multimodal retrieval as an agentic reasoning process grounded in visual inspection. V-Retrver enables an MLLM to selectively acquire visual evidence during reasoning via external visual tools, performing a multimodal interleaved reasoning process that alternates between hypothesis generation and targeted visual verification.To train such an evidence-gathering retrieval agent, we adopt a curriculum-based learning strategy combining supervised reasoning activation, rejection-based refinement, and reinforcement learning with an evidence-aligned objective. Experiments across multiple multimodal retrieval benchmarks demonstrate consistent improvements in retrieval accuracy (with 23.0% improvements on average), perception-driven reasoning reliability, and generalization.

摘要（中文）: 最近，多模态大型语言模型（MLLM）已被应用于通用多模态检索，其中思维链（CoT）推理提高了候选重新排序的性能。然而，现有方法在很大程度上仍然是语言驱动的，依赖于静态的视觉编码，并且缺乏主动验证细粒度视觉证据的能力，这通常会导致在视觉模糊情况下出现推测性推理。我们提出了一种证据驱动的检索框架V-Retrver，它将多模态检索重塑为一种基于视觉检查的 Agentic 推理过程。V-Retrver 使 MLLM 能够在推理过程中通过外部视觉工具选择性地获取视觉证据，从而执行一个在假设生成和目标视觉验证之间交替进行的多模态交错推理过程。为了训练这种证据收集检索 Agent，我们采用了一种基于课程的学习策略，该策略结合了有监督的推理激活、基于拒绝的细化以及具有证据对齐目标的强化学习。在多个多模态检索基准上的实验表明，在检索准确率（平均提升 23.0%）、感知驱动的推理可靠性和泛化性方面均有持续提高。

TLDR: V-Retrver introduces an evidence-driven agentic reasoning framework for multimodal retrieval, using visual tools to actively verify visual evidence during reasoning, achieving significant improvements in retrieval accuracy and generalization.

简要说明: V-Retrver 引入了一个证据驱动的智能体推理框架用于多模态检索，通过视觉工具主动验证推理过程中的视觉证据，从而显著提高了检索准确性和泛化能力。

Authors: Dongyang Chen, Chaoyang Wang, Dezhao SU, Xi Xiao, Zeyu Zhang, Jing Xiong, Qing Li, Yuzhang Shang, Shichao Ka

VisRefiner: Learning from Visual Differences for Screenshot-to-Code Generation

Abstract (English): Screenshot-to-code generation aims to translate user interface screenshots into executable frontend code that faithfully reproduces the target layout and style. Existing multimodal large language models perform this mapping directly from screenshots but are trained without observing the visual outcomes of their generated code. In contrast, human developers iteratively render their implementation, compare it with the design, and learn how visual differences relate to code changes. Inspired by this process, we propose VisRefiner, a training framework that enables models to learn from visual differences between rendered predictions and reference designs. We construct difference-aligned supervision that associates visual discrepancies with corresponding code edits, allowing the model to understand how appearance variations arise from implementation changes. Building on this, we introduce a reinforcement learning stage for self-refinement, where the model improves its generated code by observing both the rendered output and the target design, identifying their visual differences, and updating the code accordingly. Experiments show that VisRefiner substantially improves single-step generation quality and layout fidelity, while also endowing models with strong self-refinement ability. These results demonstrate the effectiveness of learning from visual differences for advancing screenshot-to-code generation.

摘要（中文）: 截图到代码生成旨在将用户界面截图翻译成可执行的前端代码，忠实地再现目标布局和样式。现有的多模态大型语言模型直接从截图中执行此映射，但训练时未观察到其生成代码的视觉结果。相比之下，人类开发者会迭代地渲染他们的实现，将其与设计进行比较，并学习视觉差异如何与代码更改相关联。受此过程的启发，我们提出了 VisRefiner，一个训练框架，使模型能够从渲染的预测和参考设计之间的视觉差异中学习。我们构建了差异对齐的监督，将视觉差异与相应的代码编辑相关联，从而使模型能够理解外观变化如何由实现更改引起。在此基础上，我们引入了一个用于自我精炼的强化学习阶段，在该阶段，模型通过观察渲染的输出和目标设计，识别它们的视觉差异，并相应地更新代码，从而改进其生成的代码。实验表明，VisRefiner 大幅度提高了单步生成质量和布局保真度，同时也赋予模型强大的自我精炼能力。这些结果证明了从视觉差异中学习对于推进截图到代码生成的有效性。

TLDR: The paper introduces VisRefiner, a training framework that allows screenshot-to-code generation models to learn from visual differences between rendered code and target designs, enhancing generation quality and layout fidelity through reinforcement learning.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了VisRefiner，一个训练框架，使截图到代码生成模型能够从渲染代码和目标设计之间的视觉差异中学习，通过强化学习提高生成质量和布局保真度。

Authors: Jie Deng, Kaichun Yao, Libo Zhang

Can vision language models learn intuitive physics from interaction?

Abstract (English): Pre-trained vision language models do not have good intuitions about the physical world. Recent work has shown that supervised fine-tuning can improve model performance on simple physical tasks. However, fine-tuned models do not appear to learn robust physical rules that can generalize to new contexts. Based on research in cognitive science, we hypothesize that models need to interact with an environment to properly learn its physical dynamics. We train models that learn through interaction with the environment using reinforcement learning. While learning from interaction allows models to improve their within-task performance, it fails to produce models with generalizable physical intuitions. We find that models trained on one task do not reliably generalize to related tasks, even if the tasks share visual statistics and physical principles, and regardless of whether the models are trained through interaction.

摘要（中文）: 预训练的视觉-语言模型对物理世界的直觉不足。 近期研究表明，有监督的微调可以提高模型在简单物理任务上的性能。 然而，经过微调的模型似乎并没有学习到能够泛化到新环境中的稳健物理规则。 基于认知科学的研究，我们假设模型需要与环境交互才能正确学习其物理动力学。 我们训练了通过强化学习与环境交互来学习的模型。 虽然从交互中学习能让模型提高其任务内的性能，但它无法产生具有可泛化物理直觉的模型。 我们发现，即使任务共享视觉统计和物理原理，且无论模型是否通过交互进行训练，在一个任务上训练的模型也无法可靠地泛化到相关任务。

TLDR: This paper investigates whether reinforcement learning-based interaction can help vision-language models learn generalizable intuitive physics, finding that it improves within-task performance but not generalization across related tasks.

简要说明: 本文研究了基于强化学习的交互是否能帮助视觉语言模型学习可泛化的直观物理学，发现它提高了任务内的性能，但不能泛化到相关任务。

Authors: Luca M. Schulze Buschoff, Konstantinos Voudouris, Can Demircan, Eric Schulz

On the Role of Iterative Computation in Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): How does the amount of compute available to a reinforcement learning (RL) policy affect its learning? Can policies using a fixed amount of parameters, still benefit from additional compute? The standard RL framework does not provide a language to answer these questions formally. Empirically, deep RL policies are often parameterized as neural networks with static architectures, conflating the amount of compute and the number of parameters. In this paper, we formalize compute bounded policies and prove that policies which use more compute can solve problems and generalize to longer-horizon tasks that are outside the scope of policies with less compute. Building on prior work in algorithmic learning and model-free planning, we propose a minimal architecture that can use a variable amount of compute. Our experiments complement our theory. On a set 31 different tasks spanning online and offline RL, we show that $(1)$ this architecture achieves stronger performance simply by using more compute, and $(2)$ stronger generalization on longer-horizon test tasks compared to standard feedforward networks or deep residual network using up to 5 times more parameters.

摘要（中文）: 强化学习(RL)策略可用的计算量如何影响其学习过程？使用固定数量参数的策略是否仍然可以从额外的计算量中获益？标准的RL框架没有提供一种正式回答这些问题的语言。在实践中，深度RL策略通常被参数化为具有静态架构的神经网络，这将计算量与参数量混淆。在本文中，我们形式化了计算量受限的策略，并证明了使用更多计算量的策略可以解决那些超出计算量较少策略范围的问题，并且能够泛化到更长视野的任务上。基于算法学习和无模型规划方面的先前工作，我们提出了一种可以使用可变计算量的最小架构。我们的实验补充了我们的理论。在一组涵盖在线和离线RL的31个不同任务上，我们表明 $(1)$ 这种架构仅仅通过使用更多的计算量就能获得更强的性能，并且 $(2)$ 与使用多达5倍参数的标准前馈网络或深度残差网络相比，在更长视野的测试任务上具有更强的泛化能力。

TLDR: This paper formalizes compute-bounded policies in RL and demonstrates that increased computation, even with fixed parameters, improves performance and generalization on longer-horizon tasks compared to standard architectures with significantly more parameters.

简要说明: 该论文形式化了强化学习中计算受限策略的概念，并证明即使在参数固定的情况下，增加计算量也能提高性能和泛化能力，尤其是在长时间跨度的任务中，效果优于使用更多参数的传统架构。

Authors: Raj Ghugare, Michał Bortkiewicz, Alicja Ziarko, Benjamin Eysenbach

f-GRPO and Beyond: Divergence-Based Reinforcement Learning Algorithms for General LLM Alignment

Abstract (English): Recent research shows that Preference Alignment (PA) objectives act as divergence estimators between aligned (chosen) and unaligned (rejected) response distributions. In this work, we extend this divergence-based perspective to general alignment settings, such as reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), where only environmental rewards are available. Within this unified framework, we propose f-Group Relative Policy Optimization (f-GRPO), a class of on-policy reinforcement learning, and f-Hybrid Alignment Loss (f-HAL), a hybrid on/off policy objectives, for general LLM alignment based on variational representation of f-divergences. We provide theoretical guarantees that these classes of objectives improve the average reward after alignment. Empirically, we validate our framework on both RLVR (Math Reasoning) and PA tasks (Safety Alignment), demonstrating superior performance and flexibility compared to current methods.

摘要（中文）: 近期研究表明，偏好对齐（PA）目标本质上是已对齐（选中）和未对齐（拒绝）响应分布之间的散度估计器。在这项工作中，我们将这种基于散度的视角扩展到一般的对齐设置，例如具有可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR），其中只提供环境奖励。在这种统一框架下，我们提出了f-组相对策略优化（f-GRPO），一种基于f-散度变分表示的，用于通用LLM对齐的on-policy强化学习方法；以及f-混合对齐损失（f-HAL），一种混合on/off-policy目标。我们提供理论保证，证明这些目标函数类能够提升对齐后的平均奖励。在实验方面，我们在RLVR（数学推理）和PA任务（安全对齐）上验证了我们框架的有效性，结果表明与现有方法相比，我们的框架具有更优越的性能和灵活性。

TLDR: This paper introduces divergence-based reinforcement learning algorithms (f-GRPO and f-HAL) for aligning LLMs in various settings (RLVR and Preference Alignment), offering theoretical guarantees and empirical validation.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种基于散度的强化学习算法（f-GRPO 和 f-HAL），用于在各种设置（RLVR 和偏好对齐）中对齐 LLM，并提供了理论保证和经验验证。

Authors: Rajdeep Haldar, Lantao Mei, Guang Lin, Yue Xing, Qifan Song

SURE: Safe Uncertainty-Aware Robot-Environment Interaction using Trajectory Optimization

Abstract (English): Robotic tasks involving contact interactions pose significant challenges for trajectory optimization due to discontinuous dynamics. Conventional formulations typically assume deterministic contact events, which limit robustness and adaptability in real-world settings. In this work, we propose SURE, a robust trajectory optimization framework that explicitly accounts for contact timing uncertainty. By allowing multiple trajectories to branch from possible pre-impact states and later rejoin a shared trajectory, SURE achieves both robustness and computational efficiency within a unified optimization framework. We evaluate SURE on two representative tasks with unknown impact times. In a cart-pole balancing task involving uncertain wall location, SURE achieves an average improvement of 21.6% in success rate when branch switching is enabled during control. In an egg-catching experiment using a robotic manipulator, SURE improves the success rate by 40%. These results demonstrate that SURE substantially enhances robustness compared to conventional nominal formulations.

摘要（中文）: 涉及接触交互的机器人任务由于动力学的不连续性，对轨迹优化提出了重大挑战。传统的公式通常假设确定性的接触事件，这限制了在实际环境中的鲁棒性和适应性。在这项工作中，我们提出了SURE，一种鲁棒的轨迹优化框架，它明确考虑了接触时间的不确定性。通过允许多条轨迹从可能的碰撞前状态分支，并在之后重新汇合到一条共享的轨迹上，SURE在一个统一的优化框架内实现了鲁棒性和计算效率。我们通过两个具有未知冲击时间的代表性任务评估SURE。在一个涉及不确定墙体位置的倒立摆平衡任务中，当在控制过程中启用分支切换时，SURE的成功率平均提高了21.6%。 在一个使用机器人机械臂的抓蛋实验中，SURE将成功率提高了40%。这些结果表明，与传统的标称公式相比，SURE大大提高了鲁棒性。

TLDR: The paper introduces SURE, a trajectory optimization framework for robot-environment interaction that handles contact timing uncertainty by branching trajectories, demonstrating improved success rates in cart-pole balancing and egg-catching tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为SURE的轨迹优化框架，用于机器人与环境的交互，通过分支轨迹来处理接触时间的不确定性，并在推车-杆平衡和抓蛋任务中展示了更高的成功率。

Authors: Zhuocheng Zhang, Haizhou Zhao, Xudong Sun, Aaron M. Johnson, Majid Khadiv

SuReNav: Superpixel Graph-based Constraint Relaxation for Navigation in Over-constrained Environments

Abstract (English): We address the over-constrained planning problem in semi-static environments. The planning objective is to find a best-effort solution that avoids all hard constraint regions while minimally traversing the least risky areas. Conventional methods often rely on pre-defined area costs, limiting generalizations. Further, the spatial continuity of navigation spaces makes it difficult to identify regions that are passable without overestimation. To overcome these challenges, we propose SuReNav, a superpixel graph-based constraint relaxation and navigation method that imitates human-like safe and efficient navigation. Our framework consists of three components: 1) superpixel graph map generation with regional constraints, 2) regional-constraint relaxation using graph neural network trained on human demonstrations for safe and efficient navigation, and 3) interleaving relaxation, planning, and execution for complete navigation. We evaluate our method against state-of-the-art baselines on 2D semantic maps and 3D maps from OpenStreetMap, achieving the highest human-likeness score of complete navigation while maintaining a balanced trade-off between efficiency and safety. We finally demonstrate its scalability and generalization performance in real-world urban navigation with a quadruped robot, Spot.

摘要（中文）: 我们研究半静态环境下的超约束规划问题。规划目标是找到一个尽力而为的解决方案，既要避开所有硬约束区域，又要尽可能少地穿越风险最小的区域。传统方法通常依赖于预定义的区域代价，限制了泛化能力。此外，导航空间的连续性使得难以识别在不产生过度估计的情况下能够通过的区域。为了克服这些挑战，我们提出SuReNav，一种基于超像素图的约束松弛和导航方法，旨在模仿人类的安全性及效率的导航方式。我们的框架包含三个组成部分：1）带有区域约束的超像素图地图生成；2）利用图神经网络，基于人类安全高效导航的演示数据进行训练，以实现区域约束的松弛；3）交错进行松弛、规划和执行，以完成整个导航过程。我们在来自OpenStreetMap的2D语义地图和3D地图上，将我们的方法与最先进的基线方法进行比较，在保证效率和安全之间的平衡折衷下，实现了最高的完整导航人类相似度得分。最后，我们在一只四足机器人Spot上，通过真实世界的城市导航，展示了它的可扩展性和泛化性能。

TLDR: The paper presents SuReNav, a superpixel graph-based navigation method that uses GNNs trained on human demonstrations to relax constraints and navigate efficiently in over-constrained environments, demonstrated on both simulated and real-world robotic platforms.

简要说明: 该论文提出了SuReNav，一种基于超像素图的导航方法，利用在人类演示上训练的GNN来放宽约束并在过度约束的环境中有效地导航，并在模拟和真实的机器人平台上进行了演示。

Authors: Keonyoung Koh, Moonkyeong Jung, Samuel Seungsup Lee, Daehyung Park

Crowd-FM: Learned Optimal Selection of Conditional Flow Matching-generated Trajectories for Crowd Navigation

Abstract (English): Safe and computationally efficient local planning for mobile robots in dense, unstructured human crowds remains a fundamental challenge. Moreover, ensuring that robot trajectories are similar to how a human moves will increase the acceptance of the robot in human environments. In this paper, we present Crowd-FM, a learning-based approach to address both safety and human-likeness challenges. Our approach has two novel components. First, we train a Conditional Flow-Matching (CFM) policy over a dataset of optimally controlled trajectories to learn a set of collision-free primitives that a robot can choose at any given scenario. The chosen optimal control solver can generate multi-modal collision-free trajectories, allowing the CFM policy to learn a diverse set of maneuvers. Secondly, we learn a score function over a dataset of human demonstration trajectories that provides a human-likeness score for the flow primitives. At inference time, computing the optimal trajectory requires selecting the one with the highest score. Our approach improves the state-of-the-art by showing that our CFM policy alone can produce collision-free navigation with a higher success rate than existing learning-based baselines. Furthermore, when augmented with inference-time refinement, our approach can outperform even expensive optimisation-based planning approaches. Finally, we validate that our scoring network can select trajectories closer to the expert data than a manually designed cost function.

摘要（中文）: 在稠密、非结构化的人群中，为移动机器人进行安全且计算高效的局部规划仍然是一个根本性的挑战。此外，确保机器人轨迹类似于人类的移动方式将提高机器人在人类环境中的接受度。在本文中，我们提出了一种基于学习的方法 Crowd-FM，以应对安全性和类人性的挑战。我们的方法有两个新的组成部分。首先，我们在最优控制轨迹的数据集上训练一个条件流匹配（CFM）策略，以学习一组机器人可以在任何给定场景中选择的无碰撞原语。所选的最优控制求解器可以生成多模态的无碰撞轨迹，从而使CFM策略能够学习各种各样的机动动作。其次，我们在人类演示轨迹的数据集上学习一个评分函数，该函数为流原语提供类人性得分。在推理时，计算最优轨迹需要选择得分最高的轨迹。我们的方法改进了现有技术水平，表明我们的CFM策略本身就能产生比现有基于学习的基线方法更高成功率的无碰撞导航。此外，当通过推理时优化进行增强时，我们的方法甚至可以优于昂贵的基于优化的规划方法。最后，我们验证了我们的评分网络可以选择比手动设计的代价函数更接近专家数据的轨迹。

TLDR: This paper introduces Crowd-FM, a learning-based approach for safe and human-like robot navigation in crowded environments, using conditional flow matching to generate collision-free primitives and a learned score function to select human-like trajectories.

简要说明: 本文介绍了Crowd-FM，一种基于学习的方法，用于在拥挤环境中实现安全且类人的机器人导航。该方法使用条件流匹配生成无碰撞的运动基元，并使用学习的评分函数来选择类人的轨迹。

Authors: Antareep Singha, Laksh Nanwani, Mathai Mathew P., Samkit Jain, Phani Teja Singamaneni, Arun Kumar Singh, K. Madhava Krishna

RAPID: Reconfigurable, Adaptive Platform for Iterative Design

Abstract (English): Developing robotic manipulation policies is iterative and hypothesis-driven: researchers test tactile sensing, gripper geometries, and sensor placements through real-world data collection and training. Yet even minor end-effector changes often require mechanical refitting and system re-integration, slowing iteration. We present RAPID, a full-stack reconfigurable platform designed to reduce this friction. RAPID is built around a tool-free, modular hardware architecture that unifies handheld data collection and robot deployment, and a matching software stack that maintains real-time awareness of the underlying hardware configuration through a driver-level Physical Mask derived from USB events. This modular hardware architecture reduces reconfiguration to seconds and makes systematic multi-modal ablation studies practical, allowing researchers to sweep diverse gripper and sensing configurations without repeated system bring-up. The Physical Mask exposes modality presence as an explicit runtime signal, enabling auto-configuration and graceful degradation under sensor hot-plug events, so policies can continue executing when sensors are physically added or removed. System-centric experiments show that RAPID reduces the setup time for multi-modal configurations by two orders of magnitude compared to traditional workflows and preserves policy execution under runtime sensor hot-unplug events. The hardware designs, drivers, and software stack are open-sourced at https://rapid-kit.github.io/ .

摘要（中文）: 开发机器人操作策略是迭代且假设驱动的：研究人员通过真实世界的数据收集和训练来测试触觉传感、夹爪几何形状以及传感器放置。然而，即使是末端执行器的微小改动通常也需要机械重新装配和系统重新集成，从而减缓迭代速度。我们提出了RAPID，一个旨在减少这种摩擦的全栈可重构平台。RAPID围绕一个无工具、模块化的硬件架构构建，该架构统一了手持数据收集和机器人部署，以及一个与之匹配的软件栈，该软件栈通过源自USB事件的驱动级物理掩码，保持对底层硬件配置的实时感知。这种模块化硬件架构将重新配置时间缩短到几秒钟，并使系统的多模态消融研究成为可能，从而允许研究人员在无需重复系统启动的情况下扫描不同的夹爪和传感配置。物理掩码将模态存在性作为显式的运行时信号暴露出来，从而在传感器带电插拔事件下实现自动配置和优雅降级，以便策略可以在传感器被物理添加或移除时继续执行。以系统为中心的实验表明，与传统工作流程相比，RAPID将多模态配置的设置时间缩短了两个数量级，并可以在运行时传感器热插拔事件下保持策略执行。硬件设计、驱动程序和软件栈已在https://rapid-kit.github.io/开源。

TLDR: The paper introduces RAPID, a reconfigurable robotics platform aimed at significantly reducing the setup time for robotic manipulation experiments and enabling more efficient iterative design, featuring tool-free hardware and auto-configuring software.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一个名为RAPID的可重构机器人平台，旨在显著减少机器人操作实验的设置时间，并实现更高效的迭代设计，其特点是免工具硬件和自动配置软件。

Authors: Zi Yin, Fanhong Li, Shurui Zheng, Jia Liu

Humanoid Manipulation Interface: Humanoid Whole-Body Manipulation from Robot-Free Demonstrations

Abstract (English): Current approaches for humanoid whole-body manipulation, primarily relying on teleoperation or visual sim-to-real reinforcement learning, are hindered by hardware logistics and complex reward engineering. Consequently, demonstrated autonomous skills remain limited and are typically restricted to controlled environments. In this paper, we present the Humanoid Manipulation Interface (HuMI), a portable and efficient framework for learning diverse whole-body manipulation tasks across various environments. HuMI enables robot-free data collection by capturing rich whole-body motion using portable hardware. This data drives a hierarchical learning pipeline that translates human motions into dexterous and feasible humanoid skills. Extensive experiments across five whole-body tasks--including kneeling, squatting, tossing, walking, and bimanual manipulation--demonstrate that HuMI achieves a 3x increase in data collection efficiency compared to teleoperation and attains a 70% success rate in unseen environments.

摘要（中文）: 目前人形机器人全身操作的方法，主要依赖于遥操作或基于视觉的模拟到真实强化学习，但受到硬件物流和复杂奖励函数设计的限制。因此，所展示的自主技能仍然有限，并且通常局限于受控环境。在本文中，我们提出了一种人形操作交互界面（HuMI），这是一种便携且高效的框架，用于学习各种环境中多样的全身操作任务。HuMI 通过使用便携式硬件捕获丰富的全身运动，从而实现无需机器人的数据采集。这些数据驱动一个分层学习流程，将人类运动转化为灵巧且可行的人形机器人技能。横跨五个全身任务——包括跪姿、深蹲、抛掷、行走和双手动灵巧操作——的大量实验表明，与遥操作相比，HuMI 在数据采集效率方面实现了 3 倍的提升，并在未见环境中实现了 70% 的成功率。

TLDR: The paper introduces HuMI, a system for learning humanoid whole-body manipulation skills from robot-free human demonstrations, achieving better data collection efficiency and success rates in unseen environments compared to teleoperation.

Authors: Ruiqian Nai, Boyuan Zheng, Junming Zhao, Haodong Zhu, Sicong Dai, Zunhao Chen, Yihang Hu, Yingdong Hu, Tong Zhang, Chuan Wen, Yang Gao

Force Generative Imitation Learning: Bridging Position Trajectory and Force Commands through Control Technique

Abstract (English): In contact-rich tasks, while position trajectories are often easy to obtain, appropriate force commands are typically unknown. Although it is conceivable to generate force commands using a pretrained foundation model such as Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models, force control is highly dependent on the specific hardware of the robot, which makes the application of such models challenging. To bridge this gap, we propose a force generative model that estimates force commands from given position trajectories. However, when dealing with unseen position trajectories, the model struggles to generate accurate force commands. To address this, we introduce a feedback control mechanism. Our experiments reveal that feedback control does not converge when the force generative model has memory. We therefore adopt a model without memory, enabling stable feedback control. This approach allows the system to generate force commands effectively, even for unseen position trajectories, improving generalization for real-world robot writing tasks.

摘要（中文）: 在接触丰富的任务中，虽然位置轨迹通常容易获取，但合适的力指令通常是未知的。虽然可以想象使用预训练的基础模型，如视觉-语言-动作(VLA)模型来生成力指令，但力控制高度依赖于机器人的特定硬件，这使得此类模型的应用具有挑战性。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出了一种力生成模型，该模型从给定的位置轨迹估计力指令。然而，在处理未见过的位置轨迹时，该模型难以生成准确的力指令。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了一种反馈控制机制。我们的实验表明，当力生成模型具有记忆时，反馈控制不会收敛。因此，我们采用了一种没有记忆的模型，从而实现稳定的反馈控制。这种方法允许系统有效地生成力指令，即使对于未见过的位置轨迹，从而提高了真实世界机器人书写任务的泛化能力。

TLDR: This paper proposes a force generative model with feedback control to estimate force commands from position trajectories, addressing the challenge of applying foundation models to hardware-specific robot force control.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种带有反馈控制的力生成模型，用于从位置轨迹估计力指令，旨在解决将基础模型应用于特定硬件的机器人力控制的难题。

Authors: Hiroshi Sato, Sho Sakaino, Toshiaki Tsuji

The Law of Task-Achieving Body Motion: Axiomatizing Success of Robot Manipulation Actions

Abstract (English): Autonomous agents that perform everyday manipulation actions need to ensure that their body motions are semantically correct with respect to a task request, causally effective within their environment, and feasible for their embodiment. In order to enable robots to verify these properties, we introduce the Law of Task-Achieving Body Motion as an axiomatic correctness specification for body motions. To that end we introduce scoped Task-Environment-Embodiment (TEE) classes that represent world states as Semantic Digital Twins (SDTs) and define applicable physics models to decompose task achievement into three predicates: SatisfiesRequest for semantic request satisfaction over SDT state evolution; Causes for causal sufficiency under the scoped physics model; and CanPerform for safety and feasibility verification at the embodiment level. This decomposition yields a reusable, implementation-independent interface that supports motion synthesis and the verification of given body motions. It also supports typed failure diagnosis (semantic, causal, embodiment and out-of-scope), feasibility across robots and environments, and counterfactual reasoning about robot body motions. We demonstrate the usability of the law in practice by instantiating it for articulated container manipulation in kitchen environments on three contrasting mobile manipulation platforms

摘要（中文）: 执行日常操作的自主Agent需要确保它们的身体运动在语义上与任务请求相符、在环境中具有因果效力，并且对其自身机体而言是可行的。为了使机器人能够验证这些属性，我们引入了“任务实现身体运动法则”作为身体运动的公理化正确性规范。为此，我们引入了作用域限定的任务-环境-机体 (TEE) 类，将世界状态表示为语义数字孪生 (SDT)，并定义适用的物理模型，将任务实现分解为三个谓词：用于在SDT状态演化中实现语义请求的SatisfiesRequest；用于在作用域限定的物理模型下实现因果充分性的Causes；以及用于在机体层面进行安全性和可行性验证的CanPerform。这种分解产生了一个可重用、与实现无关的接口，支持运动合成和给定身体运动的验证。它还支持类型化的故障诊断（语义、因果、机体以及超出范围）、跨机器人和环境的可行性，以及关于机器人身体运动的反事实推理。我们通过在厨房环境中对三个对比鲜明的移动操作平台上的铰接容器操作进行实例化，来演示该法则在实践中的可用性。

TLDR: The paper introduces the "Law of Task-Achieving Body Motion," an axiomatic specification for robot body motions, decomposed into semantic, causal, and embodiment predicates for verification and diagnosis of manipulation actions across different robots and environments.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了“任务实现型身体运动定律”，这是一个机器人身体运动的公理化规范，分解为语义、因果和体现谓词，用于验证和诊断不同机器人和环境中操作行为。

Authors: Malte Huerkamp, Jonas Dech, Michael Beetz

MultiGraspNet: A Multitask 3D Vision Model for Multi-gripper Robotic Grasping

Abstract (English): Vision-based models for robotic grasping automate critical, repetitive, and draining industrial tasks. Existing approaches are typically limited in two ways: they either target a single gripper and are potentially applied on costly dual-arm setups, or rely on custom hybrid grippers that require ad-hoc learning procedures with logic that cannot be transferred across tasks, restricting their general applicability. In this work, we present MultiGraspNet, a novel multitask 3D deep learning method that predicts feasible poses simultaneously for parallel and vacuum grippers within a unified framework, enabling a single robot to handle multiple end effectors. The model is trained on the richly annotated GraspNet-1Billion and SuctionNet-1Billion datasets, which have been aligned for the purpose, and generates graspability masks quantifying the suitability of each scene point for successful grasps. By sharing early-stage features while maintaining gripper-specific refiners, MultiGraspNet effectively leverages complementary information across grasping modalities, enhancing robustness and adaptability in cluttered scenes. We characterize MultiGraspNet's performance with an extensive experimental analysis, demonstrating its competitiveness with single-task models on relevant benchmarks. We run real-world experiments on a single-arm multi-gripper robotic setup showing that our approach outperforms the vacuum baseline, grasping 16% percent more seen objects and 32% more of the novel ones, while obtaining competitive results for the parallel task.

摘要（中文）: 基于视觉的机器人抓取模型能够自动化关键、重复且耗费精力的工业任务。现有的方法通常在两个方面受到限制：它们要么针对单个夹爪，并可能应用于昂贵的双臂设置；要么依赖于定制的混合夹爪，这些夹爪需要特定的学习流程和逻辑，无法跨任务转移，从而限制了它们的一般适用性。在这项工作中，我们提出了MultiGraspNet，一种新颖的多任务3D深度学习方法，它在一个统一的框架内同时预测平行夹爪和真空吸盘的可行姿态，使单个机器人能够处理多个末端执行器。该模型在经过对齐的富含标注的GraspNet-1Billion和SuctionNet-1Billion数据集上进行训练，并生成可抓取性掩膜，量化场景中每个点成功抓取的适用性。通过共享早期阶段的特征，同时保持特定于夹爪的精炼器，MultiGraspNet有效地利用了跨抓取模式的互补信息，从而提高了在杂乱场景中的鲁棒性和适应性。我们通过广泛的实验分析来表征MultiGraspNet的性能，表明其在相关基准测试中与单任务模型具有竞争力。我们在单臂多夹爪机器人设置上进行了真实世界的实验，表明我们的方法优于真空吸盘基线，在已见过的物体上的抓取成功率高出16%，在未见过的物体上的抓取成功率高出32%，同时在平行抓取任务上获得了具有竞争力的结果。

TLDR: MultiGraspNet is a multitask 3D vision model that predicts feasible poses for parallel and vacuum grippers, demonstrating improved grasping performance in real-world robotic settings compared to single-gripper baselines.

简要说明: MultiGraspNet是一个多任务3D视觉模型，可以预测平行和真空吸盘的可行姿势。与单吸盘基线相比，该模型在真实机器人环境中展现出更好的抓取性能。

Authors: Stephany Ortuno-Chanelo, Paolo Rabino, Enrico Civitelli, Tatiana Tommasi, Raffaello Camoriano

Internalized Morphogenesis: A Self-Organizing Model for Growth, Replication, and Regeneration via Local Token Exchange in Modular Systems

Abstract (English): This study presents an internalized morphogenesis model for autonomous systems, such as swarm robotics and micro-nanomachines, that eliminates the need for external spatial computation. Traditional self-organizing models often require calculations across the entire coordinate space, including empty areas, which is impractical for resource-constrained physical modules. Our proposed model achieves complex morphogenesis through strictly local interactions between adjacent modules within the "body." By extending the "Ishida token model," modules exchange integer values using an RD-inspired discrete analogue without solving differential equations. The internal potential, derived from token accumulation and aging, guides autonomous growth, shrinkage, and replication. Simulations on a hexagonal grid demonstrated the emergence of limb-like extensions, self-division, and robust regeneration capabilities following structural amputation. A key feature is the use of the body boundary as a natural sink for information entropy (tokens) to maintain a dynamic equilibrium. These results indicate that sophisticated morphological behaviors can emerge from minimal, internal-only rules. This framework offers a computationally efficient and biologically plausible approach to developing self-repairing, adaptive, and autonomous hardware.

摘要（中文）: 本研究提出了一种用于自主系统的内化形态发生模型，例如集群机器人和微纳米机器，该模型消除了对外部空间计算的需求。传统的自组织模型通常需要在整个坐标空间（包括空白区域）进行计算，这对于资源受限的物理模块来说是不切实际的。我们提出的模型通过“身体”内相邻模块之间的严格局部交互来实现复杂的形态发生。通过扩展“石田令牌模型”，模块使用受RD（反应扩散）启发的离散类似物交换整数值，而无需求解微分方程。源自令牌累积和老化的内部势能引导自主生长、收缩和复制。在六边形网格上的仿真表明，肢状延伸的出现、自我分裂以及结构截肢后的强大再生能力。一个关键特征是利用身体边界作为信息熵（令牌）的天然汇，以维持动态平衡。这些结果表明，复杂的形态行为可以从最小的、仅限内部的规则中涌现。该框架为开发自修复、自适应和自主硬件提供了一种计算高效且生物学上合理的途径。

TLDR: The paper proposes an "internalized morphogenesis" model allowing autonomous systems to grow, replicate, and regenerate through local interactions of modules, demonstrating these capabilities in simulations and claiming biological plausibility and computational efficiency.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种“内在形态发生”模型，允许自治系统通过模块的局部交互来实现生长、复制和再生。该模型在模拟中展示了这些能力，并声称具有生物合理性和计算效率。

Authors: Takeshi Ishida

Robots That Generate Planarity Through Geometry

Abstract (English): Constraining motion to a flat surface is a fundamental requirement for equipment across science and engineering. Modern precision robotic motion systems, such as gantries, rely on the flatness of components, including guide rails and granite surface plates. However, translating this static flatness into motion requires precise internal alignment and tight-tolerance components that create long, error-sensitive reference chains. Here, we show that by using the geometric inversion of a sphere into a plane, we can produce robotic motion systems that derive planarity entirely from link lengths and connectivity. This allows planar motion to emerge from self-referencing geometric constraints, and without external metrology. We demonstrate these Flat-Plane Mechanisms (FPMs) from micron to meter scales and show that fabrication errors can be attenuated by an order of magnitude in the resulting flatness. Finally, we present a robotic FPM-based 3-axis positioning system that can be used for metrology surface scans ($\pm 12$-mm) and 3D printing inside narrow containers. This work establishes an alternative geometric foundation for planar motion that can be realized across size scales and opens new possibilities in metrology, fabrication, and micro-positioning.

摘要（中文）: 将运动限制在平面上是科学和工程领域设备的基本要求。现代精密机器人运动系统，如龙门架，依赖于包括导轨和花岗岩表面平板等组件的平面度。然而，将这种静态平面度转化为运动需要精密的内部对准和严格公差的组件，这会产生冗长且对误差敏感的参考链。在此，我们展示了通过使用球体到平面的几何反演，我们可以生产出完全从连杆长度和连接性推导出平面性的机器人运动系统。这使得平面运动能够从自参考几何约束中产生，而无需外部计量。我们展示了从微米到米级别的这些平面机构（FPM），并表明制造误差可以在最终的平面度中衰减一个数量级。最后，我们展示了一种基于机器人FPM的三轴定位系统，该系统可用于计量表面扫描（$\pm 12$ 毫米）和在狭窄容器内进行3D打印。这项工作为平面运动建立了一种替代的几何基础，该基础可以在各种尺寸尺度上实现，并为计量、制造和微定位开辟了新的可能性。

TLDR: This paper introduces a novel robotic motion system (Flat-Plane Mechanisms) that achieves planar motion through geometric constraints, minimizing the need for precise alignment and high-tolerance components. The system demonstrates error attenuation and potential applications in metrology and 3D printing.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种新型机器人运动系统（平面机构），该系统通过几何约束实现平面运动，最大限度地减少了对精确对准和高精度组件的需求。该系统展示了误差衰减以及在计量和3D打印中的潜在应用。

Authors: Jakub F. Kowalewski, Abdulaziz O. Alrashed, Jacob Alpert, Rishi Ponnapalli, Lucas R. Meza, Jeffrey Ian Lipton

MORPH Wheel: A Passive Variable-Radius Wheel Embedding Mechanical Behavior Logic for Input-Responsive Transformation

Abstract (English): This paper introduces the Mechacnially prOgrammed Radius-adjustable PHysical (MORPH) wheel, a fully passive variable-radius wheel that embeds mechanical behavior logic for torque-responsive transformation. Unlike conventional variable transmission systems relying on actuators, sensors, and active control, the MORPH wheel achieves passive adaptation solely through its geometry and compliant structure. The design integrates a torque-response coupler and spring-loaded connecting struts to mechanically adjust the wheel radius between 80 mm and 45 mm in response to input torque, without any electrical components. The MORPH wheel provides three unique capabilities rarely achieved simultaneously in previous passive designs: (1) bidirectional operation with unlimited rotation through a symmetric coupler; (2) high torque capacity exceeding 10 N with rigid power transmission in drive mode; and (3) precise and repeatable transmission ratio control governed by deterministic kinematics. A comprehensive analytical model was developed to describe the wheel's mechanical behavior logic, establishing threshold conditions for mode switching between direct drive and radius transformation. Experimental validation confirmed that the measured torque-radius and force-displacement characteristics closely follow theoretical predictions across wheel weights of 1.8-2.8kg. Robot-level demonstrations on varying loads (0-25kg), slopes, and unstructured terrains further verified that the MORPH wheel passively adjusts its radius to provide optimal transmission ratio. The MORPH wheel exemplifies a mechanically programmed structure, embedding intelligent, context-dependent behavior directly into its physical design. This approach offers a new paradigm for passive variable transmission and mechanical intelligence in robotic mobility systems operating in unpredictable or control-limited environments.

摘要（中文）: 本文介绍了一种机械编程半径可调物理轮（MORPH轮），它是一种完全被动的可变半径轮，嵌入了机械行为逻辑，用于响应扭矩的转换。与依赖于执行器、传感器和主动控制的传统变速系统不同，MORPH轮仅通过其几何结构和柔性结构实现被动适应。该设计集成了扭矩响应耦合器和弹簧加载的连接支柱，以机械方式在80毫米和45毫米之间调整车轮半径，从而响应输入扭矩，而无需任何电气元件。MORPH轮提供了三种独特的性能，这些性能很少在以前的被动设计中同时实现：（1）通过对称耦合器实现双向操作和无限旋转；（2）高扭矩容量，在驱动模式下超过10牛顿，并具有刚性动力传输；（3）精确且可重复的传动比控制，由确定的运动学控制。建立了一个全面的分析模型来描述车轮的机械行为逻辑，从而确定了直接驱动和半径转换之间模式切换的阈值条件。实验验证证实，在1.8-2.8公斤的车轮重量范围内，测量的扭矩-半径和力-位移特性与理论预测非常吻合。在不同负载（0-25公斤）、坡度和非结构化地形上的机器人层面的演示进一步验证了MORPH轮能够被动地调整其半径，从而提供最佳的传动比。MORPH轮例证了一种机械编程结构，将智能的、依赖于上下文的行为直接嵌入到其物理设计中。这种方法为被动可变速传动和在不可预测或控制受限环境中运行的机器人移动系统中的机械智能提供了新的范例。

TLDR: The paper presents a passive variable-radius wheel (MORPH wheel) that adjusts its radius in response to input torque, offering a novel solution for robotic mobility in unpredictable environments without requiring active control.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种被动式变半径轮（MORPH轮），它可以根据输入扭矩调整其半径，为在不可预测环境中运行的机器人移动提供了一种无需主动控制的新颖解决方案。

Authors: JaeHyung Jang, JuYeong Seo, Dae-Young Lee, Jee-Hwan Ryu

A Dialogue-Based Human-Robot Interaction Protocol for Wheelchair and Robotic Arm Integrated Control

Abstract (English): People with lower and upper body disabilities can benefit from wheelchairs and robotic arms to improve mobility and independence. Prior assistive interfaces, such as touchscreens and voice-driven predefined commands, often remain unintuitive and struggle to capture complex user intent. We propose a natural, dialogue based human robot interaction protocol that simulates an intelligent agent capable of communicating with users to understand intent and execute assistive actions. In a pilot study, five participants completed five assistive tasks (cleaning, drinking, feeding, drawer opening, and door opening) through dialogue-based interaction with a wheelchair and robotic arm. As a baseline, participants were required to open a door using the manual control (a wheelchair joystick and a game controller for the arm) and complete a questionnaire to gather their feedback. By analyzing the post-study questionnaires, we found that most participants enjoyed the dialogue-based interaction and assistive robot autonomy.

摘要（中文）: 肢体残疾人士可借助轮椅和机械臂来提高行动能力和独立性。现有的辅助界面，如触摸屏和语音驱动的预定义命令，通常不够直观，且难以捕捉复杂的用户意图。我们提出了一种自然的、基于对话的人机交互协议，该协议模拟了一个能够与用户通信以理解意图并执行辅助动作的智能代理。在一项初步研究中，五名参与者通过与轮椅和机械臂的基于对话的交互完成了五项辅助任务（清洁、饮水、喂食、抽屉开启和开门）。作为基线，参与者需要使用手动控制（轮椅操纵杆和机械臂游戏控制器）打开一扇门，并完成一份问卷调查以收集他们的反馈。通过分析研究后的问卷调查，我们发现大多数参与者喜欢基于对话的交互和辅助机器人的自主性。

TLDR: This paper presents a dialogue-based human-robot interaction protocol for controlling a wheelchair and robotic arm, demonstrating improved user experience compared to manual control in assistive tasks.

简要说明: 这篇论文提出了一种基于对话的人机交互协议，用于控制轮椅和机械臂，并证明在辅助任务中，与手动控制相比，用户体验有所改善。

Authors: Guangping Liu, Nicholas Hawkins, Billy Madden, Tipu Sultan, Madi Babaiasl

Addressing the Waypoint-Action Gap in End-to-End Autonomous Driving via Vehicle Motion Models

Abstract (English): End-to-End Autonomous Driving (E2E-AD) systems are typically grouped by the nature of their outputs: (i) waypoint-based models that predict a future trajectory, and (ii) action-based models that directly output throttle, steer and brake. Most recent benchmark protocols and training pipelines are waypoint-based, which makes action-based policies harder to train and compare, slowing their progress. To bridge this waypoint-action gap, we propose a novel, differentiable vehicle-model framework that rolls out predicted action sequences to their corresponding ego-frame waypoint trajectories while supervising in waypoint space. Our approach enables action-based architectures to be trained and evaluated, for the first time, within waypoint-based benchmarks without modifying the underlying evaluation protocol. We extensively evaluate our framework across multiple challenging benchmarks and observe consistent improvements over the baselines. In particular, on NAVSIM \texttt{navhard} our approach achieves state-of-the-art performance. Our code will be made publicly available upon acceptance.

摘要（中文）: 端到端自动驾驶(E2E-AD)系统通常根据其输出的性质进行分组：(i) 基于航路点的模型，预测未来的轨迹，以及 (ii) 基于动作的模型，直接输出油门、转向和刹车。最近的大多数基准协议和训练流程都是基于航路点的，这使得基于动作的策略更难训练和比较，从而减缓了它们的进展。为了弥合航路点-动作之间的差距，我们提出了一种新的、可微分的车辆模型框架，该框架将预测的动作序列展开为其相应的自车坐标系航路点轨迹，同时在航路点空间中进行监督。我们的方法首次使基于动作的架构能够在基于航路点的基准测试中进行训练和评估，而无需修改底层评估协议。我们广泛地评估了我们的框架在多个具有挑战性的基准测试中，并观察到相对于基线的持续改进。特别是在NAVSIM \texttt{navhard} 上，我们的方法实现了最先进的性能。我们的代码将在被接受后公开。

TLDR: The paper introduces a differentiable vehicle model framework that bridges the gap between action-based and waypoint-based end-to-end autonomous driving systems, enabling action-based models to be trained and evaluated on waypoint-based benchmarks, achieving state-of-the-art results on NAVSIM. The approach facilitates a more direct comparison of action-based models and waypoint-based models.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种可微分的车辆模型框架，弥合了基于动作和基于航点的端到端自动驾驶系统之间的差距，使得基于动作的模型可以在基于航点的基准上进行训练和评估，并在 NAVSIM 上实现了最先进的结果。该方法有助于更直接地比较基于动作的模型和基于航点的模型。

Authors: Jorge Daniel Rodríguez-Vidal, Gabriel Villalonga, Diego Porres, Antonio M. López Peña

AnyThermal: Towards Learning Universal Representations for Thermal Perception

Abstract (English): We present AnyThermal, a thermal backbone that captures robust task-agnostic thermal features suitable for a variety of tasks such as cross-modal place recognition, thermal segmentation, and monocular depth estimation using thermal images. Existing thermal backbones that follow task-specific training from small-scale data result in utility limited to a specific environment and task. Unlike prior methods, AnyThermal can be used for a wide range of environments (indoor, aerial, off-road, urban) and tasks, all without task-specific training. Our key insight is to distill the feature representations from visual foundation models such as DINOv2 into a thermal encoder using thermal data from these multiple environments. To bridge the diversity gap of the existing RGB-Thermal datasets, we introduce the TartanRGBT platform, the first open-source data collection platform with synced RGB-Thermal image acquisition. We use this payload to collect the TartanRGBT dataset - a diverse and balanced dataset collected in 4 environments. We demonstrate the efficacy of AnyThermal and TartanRGBT, achieving state-of-the-art results with improvements of up to 36% across diverse environments and downstream tasks on existing datasets.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了AnyThermal，一个热成像骨干网络，它能捕捉鲁棒的、任务无关的热成像特征，适用于各种任务，例如跨模态位置识别、热成像分割以及利用热成像的单目深度估计。现有的热成像骨干网络遵循从小规模数据中进行的任务特定训练，导致其效用仅限于特定环境和任务。与现有方法不同，AnyThermal可以用于广泛的环境（室内、航空、越野、城市）和任务，而无需进行任务特定的训练。我们的关键洞见是利用来自这些多种环境的热成像数据，将来自例如DINOv2等视觉基础模型的特征表示提炼到热成像编码器中。为了弥合现有RGB-Thermal数据集的多样性差距，我们引入了TartanRGBT平台，这是第一个具有同步RGB-Thermal图像采集的开源数据收集平台。我们利用此有效载荷收集了TartanRGBT数据集——一个在四种环境中收集的多元且平衡的数据集。我们展示了AnyThermal和TartanRGBT的有效性，在现有数据集上，在各种环境和下游任务中取得了最先进的结果，提高了高达36%。

TLDR: The paper introduces AnyThermal, a thermal backbone trained via distillation from visual foundation models on a new diverse RGB-Thermal dataset (TartanRGBT) for various tasks like place recognition, segmentation, and depth estimation, achieving state-of-the-art results without task-specific training.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了AnyThermal，一个通过视觉基础模型知识蒸馏训练的热成像骨干网络，使用新的多样化RGB-Thermal数据集(TartanRGBT)，用于各种任务，如地点识别，分割和深度估计，在没有特定任务训练的情况下实现了最先进的结果。

Authors: Parv Maheshwari, Jay Karhade, Yogesh Chawla, Isaiah Adu, Florian Heisen, Andrew Porco, Andrew Jong, Yifei Liu, Santosh Pitla, Sebastian Scherer, Wenshan Wang

Learning Event-Based Shooter Models from Virtual Reality Experiments

Abstract (English): Virtual reality (VR) has emerged as a powerful tool for evaluating school security measures in high-risk scenarios such as school shootings, offering experimental control and high behavioral fidelity. However, assessing new interventions in VR requires recruiting new participant cohorts for each condition, making large-scale or iterative evaluation difficult. These limitations are especially restrictive when attempting to learn effective intervention strategies, which typically require many training episodes. To address this challenge, we develop a data-driven discrete-event simulator (DES) that models shooter movement and in-region actions as stochastic processes learned from participant behavior in VR studies. We use the simulator to examine the impact of a robot-based shooter intervention strategy. Once shown to reproduce key empirical patterns, the DES enables scalable evaluation and learning of intervention strategies that are infeasible to train directly with human subjects. Overall, this work demonstrates a high-to-mid fidelity simulation workflow that provides a scalable surrogate for developing and evaluating autonomous school-security interventions.

摘要（中文）: 虚拟现实(VR)已成为评估高风险场景（如校园枪击案）中校园安全措施的强大工具，它提供了实验控制和高度的行为逼真度。然而，在VR中评估新的干预措施需要为每个条件招募新的参与者群体，这使得大规模或迭代评估变得困难。当试图学习有效的干预策略时，这些限制尤其突出，这些策略通常需要多次训练。为了应对这一挑战，我们开发了一种数据驱动的离散事件模拟器 (DES)，该模拟器将枪击者 movement 和区域内行为建模为从 VR 研究中参与者行为学习到的随机过程。我们利用该模拟器来检验一种基于机器人的枪击者干预策略的影响。一旦证明能够重现关键的经验模式，DES就能对干预策略进行可扩展的评估和学习，而这些策略直接用人类受试者进行训练是不可行的。总的来说，这项工作展示了一个高到中等逼真度的模拟工作流程，为开发和评估自主校园安全干预措施提供了一种可扩展的替代方案。

TLDR: This paper presents a data-driven discrete-event simulator (DES) learned from VR experiments of school shootings to evaluate and learn effective intervention strategies, particularly robot-based interventions, addressing the limitations of human-subject VR studies.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种数据驱动的离散事件模拟器（DES），该模拟器通过对校园枪击案的VR实验进行学习，以评估和学习有效的干预策略，特别是基于机器人的干预，从而解决了人类受试者VR研究的局限性。

Authors: Christopher A. McClurg, Alan R. Wagner

AEGPO: Adaptive Entropy-Guided Policy Optimization for Diffusion Models

Abstract (English): Reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) shows promise for aligning diffusion and flow models, yet policy optimization methods such as GRPO suffer from inefficient and static sampling strategies. These methods treat all prompts and denoising steps uniformly, ignoring substantial variations in sample learning value as well as the dynamic nature of critical exploration moments. To address this issue, we conduct a detailed analysis of the internal attention dynamics during GRPO training and uncover a key insight: attention entropy can serve as a powerful dual-signal proxy. First, across different samples, the relative change in attention entropy (ΔEntropy), which reflects the divergence between the current policy and the base policy, acts as a robust indicator of sample learning value. Second, during the denoising process, the peaks of absolute attention entropy (Entropy(t)), which quantify attention dispersion, effectively identify critical timesteps where high-value exploration occurs. Building on this observation, we propose Adaptive Entropy-Guided Policy Optimization (AEGPO), a novel dual-signal, dual-level adaptive optimization strategy. At the global level, AEGPO uses ΔEntropy to dynamically allocate rollout budgets, prioritizing prompts with higher learning value. At the local level, it exploits the peaks of Entropy(t) to guide exploration selectively at critical high-dispersion timesteps rather than uniformly across all denoising steps. By focusing computation on the most informative samples and the most critical moments, AEGPO enables more efficient and effective policy optimization. Experiments on text-to-image generation tasks demonstrate that AEGPO significantly accelerates convergence and achieves superior alignment performance compared to standard GRPO variants.

摘要（中文）: 从人类反馈中进行强化学习（RLHF）在对齐扩散模型和流模型方面展现出前景，然而，诸如GRPO之类的策略优化方法却受到低效且静态的采样策略的困扰。这些方法对所有提示词和去噪步骤一视同仁，忽略了样本学习价值的显著差异以及关键探索时刻的动态特性。 为了解决这个问题，我们对GRPO训练期间的内部注意力动态进行了详细分析，并揭示了一个关键见解：注意力熵可以作为一种强大的双信号代理。首先，在不同的样本中，注意力熵的相对变化（ΔEntropy），它反映了当前策略和基线策略之间的差异，可以作为样本学习价值的可靠指标。其次，在去噪过程中，绝对注意力熵的峰值（Entropy(t)），它量化了注意力的分散程度，可以有效地识别关键时间步，即发生高价值探索的时间点。 基于这一观察，我们提出了一种新颖的双信号、双层自适应优化策略，即自适应熵引导策略优化（AEGPO）。在全局层面上，AEGPO使用ΔEntropy来动态分配回滚预算，优先考虑具有更高学习价值的提示词。 在局部层面上，它利用Entropy(t)的峰值来选择性地引导在关键高分散时间步的探索，而不是均匀地跨越所有去噪步骤。 通过将计算集中在信息量最大的样本和最关键的时刻，AEGPO能够实现更高效和有效的策略优化。在文本到图像生成任务上的实验表明，与标准GRPO变体相比，AEGPO显著加速了收敛速度，并实现了卓越的对齐性能。

TLDR: The paper introduces AEGPO, an adaptive policy optimization method for diffusion models that uses attention entropy to prioritize prompts with high learning value and guide exploration at critical denoising timesteps, leading to faster convergence and better alignment performance.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了AEGPO，一种用于扩散模型的自适应策略优化方法，它利用注意力熵来优先处理具有高学习价值的提示语，并在关键的去噪时间步指导探索，从而实现更快的收敛和更好的对齐性能。
