Authors: Yuming Li, Qingyu Li, Chengyu Bai, Xiangyang Luo, Zeyue Xue, Wenyu Qin, Meng Wang, Yikai Wang, Shanghang Zhang

Semantically Labelled Automata for Multi-Task Reinforcement Learning with LTL Instructions

Abstract (English): We study multi-task reinforcement learning (RL), a setting in which an agent learns a single, universal policy capable of generalising to arbitrary, possibly unseen tasks. We consider tasks specified as linear temporal logic (LTL) formulae, which are commonly used in formal methods to specify properties of systems, and have recently been successfully adopted in RL. In this setting, we present a novel task embedding technique leveraging a new generation of semantic LTL-to-automata translations, originally developed for temporal synthesis. The resulting semantically labelled automata contain rich, structured information in each state that allow us to (i) compute the automaton efficiently on-the-fly, (ii) extract expressive task embeddings used to condition the policy, and (iii) naturally support full LTL. Experimental results in a variety of domains demonstrate that our approach achieves state-of-the-art performance and is able to scale to complex specifications where existing methods fail.

摘要（中文）: 我们研究多任务强化学习（RL），其中智能体学习一种通用的策略，能够泛化到任意的、可能未见过的任务。我们考虑以线性时序逻辑（LTL）公式指定的任务，这些公式常用于形式化方法中指定系统的属性，并且最近已成功应用于强化学习。在此背景下，我们提出了一种新颖的任务嵌入技术，该技术利用了新一代的语义化的LTL到自动机翻译，最初是为时间合成而开发的。由此产生的语义标记自动机在每个状态中包含丰富的、结构化的信息，这使得我们能够（i）有效地动态计算自动机，（ii）提取用于调节策略的富有表现力的任务嵌入，以及（iii）自然地支持完整的LTL。在各种领域中的实验结果表明，我们的方法实现了最先进的性能，并且能够扩展到现有方法失败的复杂规范。

TLDR: This paper introduces a novel task embedding technique using semantically labelled automata for multi-task reinforcement learning with LTL instructions, achieving state-of-the-art performance and scaling to complex specifications.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种新的任务嵌入技术，该技术使用语义标记的自动机来进行带有LTL指令的多任务强化学习，从而实现了最先进的性能并可扩展到复杂的规范。

Authors: Alessandro Abate, Giuseppe De Giacomo, Mathias Jackermeier, Jan Kretínský, Maximilian Prokop, Christoph Weinhuber

Pairwise is Not Enough: Hypergraph Neural Networks for Multi-Agent Pathfinding

Abstract (English): Multi-Agent Path Finding (MAPF) is a representative multi-agent coordination problem, where multiple agents are required to navigate to their respective goals without collisions. Solving MAPF optimally is known to be NP-hard, leading to the adoption of learning-based approaches to alleviate the online computational burden. Prevailing approaches, such as Graph Neural Networks (GNNs), are typically constrained to pairwise message passing between agents. However, this limitation leads to suboptimal behaviours and critical issues, such as attention dilution, particularly in dense environments where group (i.e. beyond just two agents) coordination is most critical. Despite the importance of such higher-order interactions, existing approaches have not been able to fully explore them. To address this representational bottleneck, we introduce HMAGAT (Hypergraph Multi-Agent Attention Network), a novel architecture that leverages attentional mechanisms over directed hypergraphs to explicitly capture group dynamics. Empirically, HMAGAT establishes a new state-of-the-art among learning-based MAPF solvers: e.g., despite having just 1M parameters and being trained on 100$\times$ less data, it outperforms the current SoTA 85M parameter model. Through detailed analysis of HMAGAT's attention values, we demonstrate how hypergraph representations mitigate the attention dilution inherent in GNNs and capture complex interactions where pairwise methods fail. Our results illustrate that appropriate inductive biases are often more critical than the training data size or sheer parameter count for multi-agent problems.

摘要（中文）: 多智能体路径规划（MAPF）是一个具有代表性的多智能体协调问题，其要求多个智能体在无碰撞的情况下导航到各自的目标。MAPF的最优求解已知是NP-难的，这促使人们采用基于学习的方法来减轻在线计算负担。目前主流的方法，例如图神经网络（GNNs），通常局限于智能体间的两两消息传递。然而，这种限制会导致次优行为和关键问题，例如注意力稀释，尤其是在密集环境中，此时群体（即超越仅两个智能体）协调最为关键。尽管这种高阶交互非常重要，但现有的方法未能充分探索它们。为了解决这个表征瓶颈，我们引入了HMAGAT（超图多智能体注意力网络），一种新型架构，它利用有向超图上的注意力机制来显式地捕获群体动态。在实验上，HMAGAT在基于学习的MAPF求解器中建立了一个新的最先进水平：例如，尽管只有100万个参数并且在减少100倍的数据上进行训练，但它优于当前最先进的具有8500万个参数的模型。通过对HMAGAT注意力值的详细分析，我们证明了超图表示如何缓解GNN中固有的注意力稀释，并捕获成对方法无法处理的复杂交互。我们的结果表明，对于多智能体问题，适当的归纳偏置通常比训练数据的大小或单纯的参数数量更为关键。

TLDR: The paper introduces HMAGAT, a hypergraph neural network for multi-agent pathfinding that captures group dynamics and outperforms existing pairwise GNN approaches, achieving state-of-the-art results with fewer parameters and less training data.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种用于多智能体路径规划的超图神经网络 HMAGAT，它能够捕捉群体动态，并优于现有的成对 GNN 方法，以更少的参数和更少的数据实现了最先进的结果。

Authors: Rishabh Jain, Keisuke Okumura, Michael Amir, Pietro Lio, Amanda Prorok

F-GRPO: Don't Let Your Policy Learn the Obvious and Forget the Rare

Abstract (English): Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) is commonly based on group sampling to estimate advantages and stabilize policy updates. In practice, large group sizes are not feasible due to computational limits, which biases learning toward trajectories that are already likely. Smaller groups often miss rare-correct trajectories while still containing mixed rewards, concentrating probability on common solutions. We derive the probability that updates miss rare-correct modes as a function of group size, showing non-monotonic behavior, and characterize how updates redistribute mass within the correct set, revealing that unsampled-correct mass can shrink even as total correct mass grows. Motivated by this analysis, we propose a difficulty-aware advantage scaling coefficient, inspired by Focal loss, that down-weights updates on high-success prompts. The lightweight modification can be directly integrated into any group-relative RLVR algorithm such as GRPO, DAPO, and CISPO. On Qwen2.5-7B across in-domain and out-of-domain benchmarks, our method improves pass@256 from 64.1 $\rightarrow$ 70.3 (GRPO), 69.3 $\rightarrow$ 72.5 (DAPO), and 73.2 $\rightarrow$ 76.8 (CISPO), while preserving or improving pass@1, without increasing group size or computational cost.

摘要（中文）: 基于可验证奖励的强化学习(RLVR)通常依赖于分组采样来估计优势函数并稳定策略更新。但在实践中，由于计算限制，大的组规模是不可行的，这导致学习偏向于已经很可能的轨迹。较小的组规模常常会遗漏罕见且正确的轨迹，同时依然包含混合奖励，从而将概率集中在常见的解决方案上。我们推导了更新遗漏罕见正确模式的概率作为组规模的函数，展示了非单调行为，并描述了更新如何在正确集合内重新分配概率质量，揭示了即使总的正确质量增长，未被采样的正确质量也会缩减。受此分析的启发，我们提出了一种难度感知的优势缩放系数，灵感来源于Focal loss，该系数降低了对高成功提示的更新权重。这种轻量级的修改可以直接集成到任何组相对的RLVR算法中，如GRPO、DAPO和CISPO。在使用通义千问2.5-7B模型，在领域内和领域外基准测试中，我们的方法将pass@256从64.1提升至 70.3 (GRPO)，从69.3提升至72.5 (DAPO)，以及从73.2提升至76.8 (CISPO)，同时保持或提高了pass@1，而没有增加组规模或计算成本。

TLDR: The paper introduces F-GRPO, a modification to Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) that addresses the bias towards common trajectories in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) by down-weighting high-success prompts. It achieves significant pass@k improvements on Qwen2.5-7B without increased computational cost.

简要说明: 本文介绍了F-GRPO，一种对Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO)的改进，通过降低高成功率提示的权重来解决可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）中对常见轨迹的偏差。它在Qwen2.5-7B上实现了显著的pass@k改进，且没有增加计算成本。

Authors: Daniil Plyusov, Alexey Gorbatovski, Boris Shaposhnikov, Viacheslav Sinii, Alexey Malakhov, Daniil Gavrilov

Trust Regions Sell, But Who's Buying? Overlap Geometry as an Alternative Trust Region for Policy Optimization

Abstract (English): Standard trust-region methods constrain policy updates via Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence. However, KL controls only an average divergence and does not directly prevent rare, large likelihood-ratio excursions that destabilize training--precisely the failure mode that motivates heuristics such as PPO's clipping. We propose overlap geometry as an alternative trust region, constraining distributional overlap via the Bhattacharyya coefficient (closely related to the Hellinger/Renyi-1/2 geometry). This objective penalizes separation in the ratio tails, yielding tighter control over likelihood-ratio excursions without relying on total variation bounds that can be loose in tail regimes. We derive Bhattacharyya-TRPO (BTRPO) and Bhattacharyya-PPO (BPPO), enforcing overlap constraints via square-root ratio updates: BPPO clips the square-root ratio q = sqrt(r), and BTRPO applies a quadratic Hellinger/Bhattacharyya penalty. Empirically, overlap-based updates improve robustness and aggregate performance as measured by RLiable under matched training budgets, suggesting overlap constraints as a practical, principled alternative to KL for stable policy optimization.

摘要（中文）: 标准信赖域方法通过Kullback-Leibler (KL) 散度约束策略更新。然而，KL 仅控制平均散度，并不能直接阻止罕见且较大的似然比偏离——而这正是导致训练不稳定的因素，并催生了PPO的裁剪等启发式方法。 我们提出将重叠几何作为一种替代信赖域，通过Bhattacharyya系数（与Hellinger/Renyi-1/2几何密切相关）来约束分布重叠。该目标惩罚比例尾部的分离，从而更严格地控制似然比偏离，而无需依赖在尾部区域可能较为宽松的全变差界限。 我们推导了Bhattacharyya-TRPO (BTRPO) 和 Bhattacharyya-PPO (BPPO)，通过平方根比例更新来强制执行重叠约束：BPPO裁剪平方根比例 q = sqrt(r)，而 BTRPO 应用二次 Hellinger/Bhattacharyya 惩罚。 经验表明，基于重叠的更新在匹配的训练预算下，提高了鲁棒性并改进了 RLiable 衡量的整体性能，表明重叠约束是一种实用、有原则的 KL 替代方案，可用于稳定策略优化。

TLDR: The paper proposes using overlap geometry based on the Bhattacharyya coefficient as an alternative trust region for policy optimization, aiming to improve robustness and performance by directly controlling likelihood-ratio excursions. They develop BTRPO and BPPO and demonstrate improved results under matched training budgets.

简要说明: 该论文提出使用基于Bhattacharyya系数的重叠几何作为策略优化的一种替代信任区域，旨在通过直接控制可能性比率偏移来提高鲁棒性和性能。他们开发了BTRPO和BPPO，并证明在匹配的训练预算下结果有所改善。

Authors: Gaurish Trivedi, Alakh Sharma, Kartikey Singh Bhandari, Yash Sinha, Pratik Narang, Dhruv Kumar, Jagat Sesh Challa

Sample-Efficient Policy Space Response Oracles with Joint Experience Best Response

Abstract (English): Multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) offers a scalable alternative to exact game-theoretic analysis but suffers from non-stationarity and the need to maintain diverse populations of strategies that capture non-transitive interactions. Policy Space Response Oracles (PSRO) address these issues by iteratively expanding a restricted game with approximate best responses (BRs), yet per-agent BR training makes it prohibitively expensive in many-agent or simulator-expensive settings. We introduce Joint Experience Best Response (JBR), a drop-in modification to PSRO that collects trajectories once under the current meta-strategy profile and reuses this joint dataset to compute BRs for all agents simultaneously. This amortizes environment interaction and improves the sample efficiency of best-response computation. Because JBR converts BR computation into an offline RL problem, we propose three remedies for distribution-shift bias: (i) Conservative JBR with safe policy improvement, (ii) Exploration-Augmented JBR that perturbs data collection and admits theoretical guarantees, and (iii) Hybrid BR that interleaves JBR with periodic independent BR updates. Across benchmark multi-agent environments, Exploration-Augmented JBR achieves the best accuracy-efficiency trade-off, while Hybrid BR attains near-PSRO performance at a fraction of the sample cost. Overall, JBR makes PSRO substantially more practical for large-scale strategic learning while preserving equilibrium robustness.

摘要（中文）: 多智能体强化学习 (MARL) 为精确的博弈论分析提供了一种可扩展的替代方案，但受到非平稳性和需要维持捕获非传递性交互的多样化策略群体的困扰。策略空间响应预言机 (PSRO) 通过迭代地使用近似最优应对 (BR) 扩展受限博弈来解决这些问题，然而，每个智能体的 BR 训练使得其在多智能体或模拟器代价高昂的设置中望而却步。我们引入了联合经验最优应对 (JBR)，这是 PSRO 的一个即插即用修改，它在当前元策略剖面下一次性收集轨迹，并重用这个联合数据集来同时计算所有智能体的 BR。这分摊了环境交互的成本，并提高了最优应对计算的样本效率。由于 JBR 将 BR 计算转化为离线强化学习问题，我们提出了三种针对分布偏移偏差的补救措施：（i）采用安全策略改进的保守 JBR，（ii）扰动数据收集并允许理论保障的探索增强 JBR，以及（iii）将 JBR 与周期性独立 BR 更新交错的混合 BR。在基准多智能体环境中，探索增强 JBR 实现了最佳的准确性-效率权衡，而混合 BR 以一小部分样本成本获得了接近 PSRO 的性能。总的来说，JBR 使 PSRO 在大规模战略学习中更具实用性，同时保持了均衡的稳健性。

TLDR: The paper introduces Joint Experience Best Response (JBR), a modification to Policy Space Response Oracles (PSRO) that improves sample efficiency by reusing joint trajectory data for computing best responses for all agents simultaneously in multi-agent reinforcement learning. They propose and evaluate several fixes for distribution-shift bias introduced by JBR.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了联合经验最佳响应 (JBR)，这是对策略空间响应预言 (PSRO) 的一项改进，通过重用联合轨迹数据来同时计算多智能体强化学习中所有智能体的最佳响应，从而提高样本效率。他们提出并评估了几种针对 JBR 引入的分布偏移偏差的修复方法。

Authors: Ariyan Bighashdel, Thiago D. Simão, Frans A. Oliehoek

Dynamics-Aligned Shared Hypernetworks for Zero-Shot Actuator Inversion

Abstract (English): Zero-shot generalization in contextual reinforcement learning remains a core challenge, particularly when the context is latent and must be inferred from data. A canonical failure mode is actuator inversion, where identical actions produce opposite physical effects under a latent binary context. We propose DMA*-SH, a framework where a single hypernetwork, trained solely via dynamics prediction, generates a small set of adapter weights shared across the dynamics model, policy, and action-value function. This shared modulation imparts an inductive bias matched to actuator inversion, while input/output normalization and random input masking stabilize context inference, promoting directionally concentrated representations. We provide theoretical support via an expressivity separation result for hypernetwork modulation, and a variance decomposition with policy-gradient variance bounds that formalize how within-mode compression improves learning under actuator inversion. For evaluation, we introduce the Actuator Inversion Benchmark (AIB), a suite of environments designed to isolate discontinuous context-to-dynamics interactions. On AIB's held-out actuator-inversion tasks, DMA*-SH achieves zero-shot generalization, outperforming domain randomization by 111.8% and surpassing a standard context-aware baseline by 16.1%.

摘要（中文）: 情境强化学习中的零样本泛化仍然是一个核心挑战，尤其是在情境是潜在的并且必须从数据中推断时。一个典型的失效模式是执行器反转，即在潜在的二元情境下，相同的动作会产生相反的物理效果。我们提出了DMA*-SH，一个框架，其中单个超网络仅通过动力学预测进行训练，生成一组小的适配器权重，这些权重在动力学模型、策略和动作值函数之间共享。这种共享的调制赋予了一种与执行器反转相匹配的归纳偏置，同时输入/输出归一化和随机输入掩码稳定了情境推断，促进了方向集中的表达。我们通过超网络调制的表达性分离结果提供了理论支持，以及一个具有策略梯度方差界限的方差分解，后者形式化了模式内压缩如何改善执行器反转下的学习。为了评估，我们引入了执行器反转基准（AIB），一套旨在隔离不连续的情境到动态交互的环境。在AIB的保留执行器反转任务上，DMA*-SH实现了零样本泛化，性能比域随机化提升了111.8%，并且超过了一个标准的情境感知基线16.1%。

TLDR: This paper introduces DMA*-SH, a hypernetwork-based framework for zero-shot actuator inversion in contextual RL, achieving significant performance gains on a novel benchmark (AIB). The approach uses dynamics prediction for training and shared adapter weights across dynamics model, policy, and value function.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种基于超网络的框架DMA*-SH，用于情境强化学习中的零样本执行器反演问题。该方法通过动态预测进行训练，并在动态模型、策略和价值函数之间共享自适应权重，在一个新的基准测试（AIB）上实现了显著的性能提升。

Authors: Jan Benad, Pradeep Kr. Banerjee, Frank Röder, Nihat Ay, Martin V. Butz, Manfred Eppe

BEAGLE: Behavior-Enforced Agent for Grounded Learner Emulation

Abstract (English): Simulating student learning behaviors in open-ended problem-solving environments holds potential for education research, from training adaptive tutoring systems to stress-testing pedagogical interventions. However, collecting authentic data is challenging due to privacy concerns and the high cost of longitudinal studies. While Large Language Models (LLMs) offer a promising path to student simulation, they suffer from competency bias, optimizing for efficient correctness rather than the erratic, iterative struggle characteristic of novice learners. We present BEAGLE, a neuro-symbolic framework that addresses this bias by incorporating Self-Regulated Learning (SRL) theory into a novel architecture. BEAGLE integrates three key technical innovations: (1) a semi-Markov model that governs the timing and transitions of cognitive behaviors and metacognitive behaviors; (2) Bayesian Knowledge Tracing with explicit flaw injection to enforce realistic knowledge gaps and "unknown unknowns"; and (3) a decoupled agent design that separates high-level strategy use from code generation actions to prevent the model from silently correcting its own intentional errors. In evaluations on Python programming tasks, BEAGLE significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines in reproducing authentic trajectories. In a human Turing test, users were unable to distinguish synthetic traces from real student data, achieving an accuracy indistinguishable from random guessing (52.8%).

摘要（中文）: 在开放式问题解决环境中模拟学生学习行为，对于教育研究具有潜力，从训练自适应辅导系统到压力测试教学干预措施皆可受益。然而，由于隐私问题和纵向研究的高成本，收集真实数据颇具挑战。虽然大型语言模型（LLMs）为学生模拟提供了一条有希望的途径，但它们存在能力偏差，优化了高效的正确性，而非新手学习者特有的不规律、迭代式挣扎。 我们提出了BEAGLE，一个神经符号框架，它通过将自我调节学习（SRL）理论融入一种新颖的架构中来解决这种偏差。 BEAGLE集成了三项关键技术创新：（1）一个半马尔可夫模型，用于控制认知行为和元认知行为的时间和转换；（2）具有显式缺陷注入的贝叶斯知识追踪，以强制执行真实的知识缺口和“未知的未知” ；（3）一种解耦的代理设计，将高层策略使用与代码生成动作分离，以防止模型静默地纠正其自身有意的错误。 在Python编程任务的评估中，BEAGLE在重现真实轨迹方面显著优于最先进的基线。在一个人工图灵测试中，用户无法区分合成轨迹与真实学生数据，达到的准确率与随机猜测无异(52.8%)。

TLDR: BEAGLE is a neuro-symbolic framework that simulates realistic student learning behaviors by incorporating Self-Regulated Learning theory and addressing competency bias in LLMs, showing promising results in mimicking human student performance on Python programming tasks.

简要说明: BEAGLE是一个神经符号框架，通过结合自我调节学习理论并解决LLM中的能力偏差来模拟真实的学生的学习行为，并在模拟人类学生在Python编程任务中的表现方面显示出令人鼓舞的结果。

Authors: Hanchen David Wang, Clayton Cohn, Zifan Xu, Siyuan Guo, Gautam Biswas, Meiyi Ma

Prism: Spectral Parameter Sharing for Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Parameter sharing is a key strategy in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) for improving scalability, yet conventional fully shared architectures often collapse into homogeneous behaviors. Recent methods introduce diversity through clustering, pruning, or masking, but typically compromise resource efficiency. We propose Prism, a parameter sharing framework that induces inter-agent diversity by representing shared networks in the spectral domain via singular value decomposition (SVD). All agents share the singular vector directions while learning distinct spectral masks on singular values. This mechanism encourages inter-agent diversity and preserves scalability. Extensive experiments on both homogeneous (LBF, SMACv2) and heterogeneous (MaMuJoCo) benchmarks show that Prism achieves competitive performance with superior resource efficiency.

摘要（中文）: 参数共享是多智能体强化学习（MARL）中提高可扩展性的关键策略，然而，传统的完全共享架构常常会崩溃到同质化行为。最近的方法通过聚类、剪枝或掩码引入多样性，但通常会牺牲资源效率。我们提出 Prism，一个参数共享框架，通过奇异值分解（SVD）在谱域中表示共享网络来诱导智能体间的差异性。所有智能体共享奇异向量方向，同时学习奇异值上的不同谱掩码。这种机制鼓励了智能体间的多样性，并保留了可扩展性。在同构（LBF, SMACv2）和异构（MaMuJoCo）基准测试上的大量实验表明，Prism 在实现具有竞争力的性能的同时，具有卓越的资源效率。

TLDR: The paper introduces Prism, a parameter sharing framework for MARL that uses spectral decomposition to induce diversity among agents while maintaining resource efficiency, achieving competitive performance on various benchmarks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 Prism，一个用于多智能体强化学习的参数共享框架，它使用谱分解来诱导智能体之间的多样性，同时保持资源效率，并在各种基准测试中取得了具有竞争力的性能。

Authors: Kyungbeom Kim, Seungwon Oh, Kyung-Joong Kim

Agentic Unlearning: When LLM Agent Meets Machine Unlearning

Abstract (English): In this paper, we introduce \textbf{agentic unlearning} which removes specified information from both model parameters and persistent memory in agents with closed-loop interaction. Existing unlearning methods target parameters alone, leaving two critical gaps: (i) parameter-memory backflow, where retrieval reactivates parametric remnants or memory artifacts reintroduce sensitive content, and (ii) the absence of a unified strategy that covers both parameter and memory pathways. We present Synchronized Backflow Unlearning (SBU), a framework that unlearns jointly across parameter and memory pathways. The memory pathway performs dependency closure-based unlearning that prunes isolated entities while logically invalidating shared artifacts. The parameter pathway employs stochastic reference alignment to guide model outputs toward a high-entropy prior. These pathways are integrated via a synchronized dual-update protocol, forming a closed-loop mechanism where memory unlearning and parametric suppression reinforce each other to prevent cross-pathway recontamination. Experiments on medical QA benchmarks show that SBU reduces traces of targeted private information across both pathways with limited degradation on retained data.

摘要（中文）: 本文介绍了一种**主动式卸学**方法，该方法可以从具有闭环交互的智能体的模型参数和持久化记忆中移除指定信息。现有的卸学方法仅针对参数，留下了两个关键缺口：（i）参数-记忆回流，其中检索会重新激活参数残留，或记忆伪影会重新引入敏感内容，以及（ii）缺乏覆盖参数和记忆路径的统一策略。我们提出了一种同步回流卸学(SBU)框架，该框架可以在参数和记忆路径上协同卸学。记忆路径执行基于依赖闭包的卸学，该卸学方法修剪孤立的实体，同时在逻辑上使共享伪影失效。参数路径采用随机参考对齐，以引导模型输出趋向于高熵先验。这些路径通过同步双更新协议集成，形成闭环机制，其中记忆卸学和参数抑制相互增强，以防止跨路径再污染。在医学问答基准上的实验表明，SBU可以减少目标私有信息在两个路径上的痕迹，同时对保留数据的退化限制在较小程度。

TLDR: This paper introduces "agentic unlearning" via Synchronized Backflow Unlearning (SBU), which jointly removes specified information from both model parameters and persistent memory in LLM agents with closed-loop interaction, addressing the limitations of existing parameter-alone unlearning methods.

简要说明: 本文介绍了“代理式卸载学习”(agentic unlearning)的概念，并通过同步回流卸载学习(SBU)在具有闭环交互的LLM代理中，联合移除模型参数和持久内存中特定的信息，解决了现有仅针对参数的卸载学习方法的局限性。

Authors: Bin Wang, Fan Wang, Pingping Wang, Jinyu Cong, Yang Yu, Yilong Yin, Zhongyi Han, Benzheng Wei

Do It for HER: First-Order Temporal Logic Reward Specification in Reinforcement Learning (Extended Version)

Abstract (English): In this work, we propose a novel framework for the logical specification of non-Markovian rewards in Markov Decision Processes (MDPs) with large state spaces. Our approach leverages Linear Temporal Logic Modulo Theories over finite traces (LTLfMT), a more expressive extension of classical temporal logic in which predicates are first-order formulas of arbitrary first-order theories rather than simple Boolean variables. This enhanced expressiveness enables the specification of complex tasks over unstructured and heterogeneous data domains, promoting a unified and reusable framework that eliminates the need for manual predicate encoding. However, the increased expressive power of LTLfMT introduces additional theoretical and computational challenges compared to standard LTLf specifications. We address these challenges from a theoretical standpoint, identifying a fragment of LTLfMT that is tractable but sufficiently expressive for reward specification in an infinite-state-space context. From a practical perspective, we introduce a method based on reward machines and Hindsight Experience Replay (HER) to translate first-order logic specifications and address reward sparsity. We evaluate this approach to a continuous-control setting using Non-Linear Arithmetic Theory, showing that it enables natural specification of complex tasks. Experimental results show how a tailored implementation of HER is fundamental in solving tasks with complex goals.

摘要（中文）: 在本文中，我们提出了一种新型框架，用于马尔可夫决策过程 (MDP) 中具有大状态空间的非马尔可夫奖励的逻辑规范。 我们的方法利用有限轨迹上的线性时序逻辑模理论 (LTLfMT)，这是经典时序逻辑的一种更具表现力的扩展，其中谓词是任意一阶理论的一阶公式，而不是简单的布尔变量。 这种增强的表现力能够在非结构化和异构数据域上指定复杂的任务，从而促进统一且可重用的框架，并消除了手动谓词编码的需要。 然而，与标准 LTLf 规范相比，LTLfMT 增强的表现力引入了额外的理论和计算挑战。 我们从理论角度解决了这些挑战，确定了 LTLfMT 的一个易处理但具有足够表现力的片段，用于在无限状态空间上下文中进行奖励规范。 从实践角度来看，我们引入了一种基于奖励机器和事后经验回放 (HER) 的方法来转换一阶逻辑规范并解决奖励稀疏性问题。 我们使用非线性算术理论，在连续控制环境中评估了这种方法，结果表明它可以自然地指定复杂的任务。 实验结果表明，量身定制的 HER 实现对于解决具有复杂目标的任务至关重要。

TLDR: This paper introduces a novel reinforcement learning framework using Linear Temporal Logic Modulo Theories over finite traces (LTLfMT) for specifying complex, non-Markovian rewards and addresses associated theoretical and practical challenges in continuous control with Hindsight Experience Replay.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种新的强化学习框架，使用有限迹上的线性时序逻辑模理论（LTLfMT）来指定复杂的非马尔可夫奖励，并使用后见之明经验回放解决了连续控制中相关的理论和实践挑战。

Authors: Pierriccardo Olivieri, Fausto Lasca, Alessandro Gianola, Matteo Papini

Diamond Maps: Efficient Reward Alignment via Stochastic Flow Maps

Abstract (English): Flow and diffusion models produce high-quality samples, but adapting them to user preferences or constraints post-training remains costly and brittle, a challenge commonly called reward alignment. We argue that efficient reward alignment should be a property of the generative model itself, not an afterthought, and redesign the model for adaptability. We propose "Diamond Maps", stochastic flow map models that enable efficient and accurate alignment to arbitrary rewards at inference time. Diamond Maps amortize many simulation steps into a single-step sampler, like flow maps, while preserving the stochasticity required for optimal reward alignment. This design makes search, sequential Monte Carlo, and guidance scalable by enabling efficient and consistent estimation of the value function. Our experiments show that Diamond Maps can be learned efficiently via distillation from GLASS Flows, achieve stronger reward alignment performance, and scale better than existing methods. Our results point toward a practical route to generative models that can be rapidly adapted to arbitrary preferences and constraints at inference time.

摘要（中文）: 流模型和扩散模型能够生成高质量的样本，但使它们在训练后适应用户偏好或约束仍然代价高昂且脆弱，这种挑战通常被称为奖励对齐。我们认为，高效的奖励对齐应该是生成模型本身的一个属性，而不是事后诸葛亮，因此我们重新设计了模型以提高适应性。我们提出了“钻石地图”（Diamond Maps），这是一种随机流图模型，能够在推理时高效且准确地对齐任意奖励。与流图类似，钻石地图将许多模拟步骤摊销到一个单步采样器中，同时保留了最佳奖励对齐所需的随机性。这种设计使得搜索、序列蒙特卡罗和引导变得可扩展，因为它能够高效且一致地估计价值函数。我们的实验表明，钻石地图可以通过从GLASS Flows进行蒸馏来高效学习，实现更强的奖励对齐性能，并且比现有方法更好地扩展。我们的结果指向了一种实用的途径，即生成模型能够在推理时快速适应任意偏好和约束。

TLDR: The paper introduces Diamond Maps, a stochastic flow map model for efficient and accurate reward alignment in generative models, enabling rapid adaptation to arbitrary preferences and constraints at inference time.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 Diamond Maps，一种随机流图模型，用于在生成模型中实现高效且准确的奖励对齐，从而能够在推理时快速适应任意偏好和约束。

Authors: Peter Holderrieth, Douglas Chen, Luca Eyring, Ishin Shah, Giri Anantharaman, Yutong He, Zeynep Akata, Tommi Jaakkola, Nicholas Matthew Boffi, Max Simchowitz

LSA: Localized Semantic Alignment for Enhancing Temporal Consistency in Traffic Video Generation

Abstract (English): Controllable video generation has emerged as a versatile tool for autonomous driving, enabling realistic synthesis of traffic scenarios. However, existing methods depend on control signals at inference time to guide the generative model towards temporally consistent generation of dynamic objects, limiting their utility as scalable and generalizable data engines. In this work, we propose Localized Semantic Alignment (LSA), a simple yet effective framework for fine-tuning pre-trained video generation models. LSA enhances temporal consistency by aligning semantic features between ground-truth and generated video clips. Specifically, we compare the output of an off-the-shelf feature extraction model between the ground-truth and generated video clips localized around dynamic objects inducing a semantic feature consistency loss. We fine-tune the base model by combining this loss with the standard diffusion loss. The model fine-tuned for a single epoch with our novel loss outperforms the baselines in common video generation evaluation metrics. To further test the temporal consistency in generated videos we adapt two additional metrics from object detection task, namely mAP and mIoU. Extensive experiments on nuScenes and KITTI datasets show the effectiveness of our approach in enhancing temporal consistency in video generation without the need for external control signals during inference and any computational overheads.

摘要（中文）: 可控视频生成已成为自动驾驶领域的多用途工具，能够逼真地合成交通场景。然而，现有方法依赖于推理时的控制信号来引导生成模型，从而实现对动态对象在时间上一致的生成，这限制了其作为可扩展和通用数据引擎的效用。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种局部语义对齐（LSA）方法，一个简单而有效的框架，用于微调预训练的视频生成模型。LSA通过对齐真实视频片段和生成视频片段之间的语义特征，来增强时间一致性。具体来说，我们比较了现成的特征提取模型在真实视频片段和生成视频片段中，围绕动态对象局部区域的输出，从而引入语义特征一致性损失。我们通过将此损失与标准扩散损失相结合来微调基础模型。仅用一个epoch通过我们的新颖损失进行微调的模型，在常见的视频生成评估指标上优于基线模型。为了进一步测试生成视频中的时间一致性，我们从目标检测任务中调整了两个额外的指标，即mAP和mIoU。在nuScenes和KITTI数据集上的大量实验表明，我们的方法在增强视频生成的时间一致性方面是有效的，同时无需在推理期间使用外部控制信号，也无需任何计算开销。

TLDR: The paper introduces Localized Semantic Alignment (LSA), a fine-tuning framework for pre-trained video generation models that enhances temporal consistency by aligning semantic features between ground-truth and generated videos around dynamic objects, improving performance without inference-time control signals.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为局部语义对齐（LSA）的微调框架，用于预训练的视频生成模型。它通过对齐真实视频和生成视频中动态对象周围的语义特征来增强时间一致性，从而在没有推理时控制信号的情况下提高性能。

Authors: Mirlan Karimov, Teodora Spasojevic, Markus Braun, Julian Wiederer, Vasileios Belagiannis, Marc Pollefeys

Learning to Share: Selective Memory for Efficient Parallel Agentic Systems

Abstract (English): Agentic systems solve complex tasks by coordinating multiple agents that iteratively reason, invoke tools, and exchange intermediate results. To improve robustness and solution quality, recent approaches deploy multiple agent teams running in parallel to explore diverse reasoning trajectories. However, parallel execution comes at a significant computational cost: when different teams independently reason about similar sub-problems or execute analogous steps, they repeatedly perform substantial overlapping computation. To address these limitations, in this paper, we propose Learning to Share (LTS), a learned shared-memory mechanism for parallel agentic frameworks that enables selective cross-team information reuse while controlling context growth. LTS introduces a global memory bank accessible to all teams and a lightweight controller that decides whether intermediate agent steps should be added to memory or not. The controller is trained using stepwise reinforcement learning with usage-aware credit assignment, allowing it to identify information that is globally useful across parallel executions. Experiments on the AssistantBench and GAIA benchmarks show that LTS significantly reduces overall runtime while matching or improving task performance compared to memory-free parallel baselines, demonstrating that learned memory admission is an effective strategy for improving the efficiency of parallel agentic systems. Project page: https://joefioresi718.github.io/LTS_webpage/

摘要（中文）: 自主系统通过协调多个智能体迭代推理、调用工具和交换中间结果来解决复杂任务。为了提高鲁棒性和解决方案质量，最近的方法部署多个并行运行的智能体团队，以探索不同的推理轨迹。然而，并行执行带来了巨大的计算成本：当不同的团队独立推理类似的子问题或执行相似的步骤时，它们会重复执行大量的重叠计算。为了解决这些限制，在本文中，我们提出了一种用于并行自主框架的学习共享（LTS）机制，该机制是一种学习型的共享内存机制，能够在控制上下文增长的同时，实现选择性的跨团队信息重用。LTS引入了一个所有团队都可以访问的全局内存库和一个轻量级的控制器，用于决定是否将中间智能体步骤添加到内存中。该控制器使用步进式强化学习进行训练，并进行使用感知的信用分配，使其能够识别在并行执行中全局有用的信息。在AssistantBench和GAIA基准测试上的实验表明，与无内存的并行基线相比，LTS显著减少了总体运行时间，同时匹配甚至提高了任务性能，这表明学习型内存准入是提高并行自主系统效率的有效策略。项目页面：https://joefioresi718.github.io/LTS_webpage/

TLDR: The paper introduces Learning to Share (LTS), a learned shared-memory mechanism for parallel agentic frameworks that significantly reduces runtime and improves task performance by selectively reusing information across agent teams.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 Learning to Share (LTS)，一个用于并行代理框架的学习型共享内存机制，通过选择性地重用跨代理团队的信息，显著减少运行时间并提高任务性能。

Authors: Joseph Fioresi, Parth Parag Kulkarni, Ashmal Vayani, Song Wang, Mubarak Shah

RFDM: Residual Flow Diffusion Model for Efficient Causal Video Editing

Abstract (English): Instructional video editing applies edits to an input video using only text prompts, enabling intuitive natural-language control. Despite rapid progress, most methods still require fixed-length inputs and substantial compute. Meanwhile, autoregressive video generation enables efficient variable-length synthesis, yet remains under-explored for video editing. We introduce a causal, efficient video editing model that edits variable-length videos frame by frame. For efficiency, we start from a 2D image-to-image (I2I) diffusion model and adapt it to video-to-video (V2V) editing by conditioning the edit at time step t on the model's prediction at t-1. To leverage videos' temporal redundancy, we propose a new I2I diffusion forward process formulation that encourages the model to predict the residual between the target output and the previous prediction. We call this Residual Flow Diffusion Model (RFDM), which focuses the denoising process on changes between consecutive frames. Moreover, we propose a new benchmark that better ranks state-of-the-art methods for editing tasks. Trained on paired video data for global/local style transfer and object removal, RFDM surpasses I2I-based methods and competes with fully spatiotemporal (3D) V2V models, while matching the compute of image models and scaling independently of input video length. More content can be found in: https://smsd75.github.io/RFDM_page/

摘要（中文）: 教学视频编辑仅使用文本提示对输入视频进行编辑，从而实现直观的自然语言控制。尽管进展迅速，但大多数方法仍然需要固定长度的输入和大量的计算。同时，自回归视频生成能够实现高效的可变长度合成，但在视频编辑方面仍未得到充分探索。我们提出了一种因果的、高效的视频编辑模型，该模型能够逐帧编辑可变长度的视频。为了提高效率，我们从2D图像到图像（I2I）的扩散模型出发，并通过在时间步t根据模型在t-1的预测来调节编辑，从而将其适配到视频到视频（V2V）的编辑。为了利用视频的时间冗余，我们提出了一种新的I2I扩散正向过程公式，该公式鼓励模型预测目标输出与先前预测之间的残差。我们称之为残差流扩散模型（RFDM），它将去噪过程集中在连续帧之间的变化上。此外，我们提出了一个新的基准测试，可以更好地对最先进的方法进行任务编辑排名。RFDM在配对视频数据上进行全局/局部风格迁移和物体移除的训练，超越了基于I2I的方法，并与完全时空（3D）的V2V模型相媲美，同时保持了图像模型的计算量，并且可以独立于输入视频长度进行缩放。更多内容请访问：https://smsd75.github.io/RFDM_page/

TLDR: This paper introduces a novel Residual Flow Diffusion Model (RFDM) for efficient, causal, and variable-length video editing using text prompts, achieving competitive performance with image model compute and outperforming I2I methods. The authors also propose a new benchmark for evaluating video editing methods.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为剩余流扩散模型（RFDM）的新模型，用于高效、因果地编辑变长视频，通过文本提示实现，以图像模型的计算成本取得了与最先进水平相当的性能，并优于 I2I 方法。作者还提出了一个新的用于评估视频编辑方法的基准。

Authors: Mohammadreza Salehi, Mehdi Noroozi, Luca Morreale, Ruchika Chavhan, Malcolm Chadwick, Alberto Gil Ramos, Abhinav Mehrotra

NECromancer: Breathing Life into Skeletons via BVH Animation

Abstract (English): Motion tokenization is a key component of generalizable motion models, yet most existing approaches are restricted to species-specific skeletons, limiting their applicability across diverse morphologies. We propose NECromancer (NEC), a universal motion tokenizer that operates directly on arbitrary BVH skeletons. NEC consists of three components: (1) an Ontology-aware Skeletal Graph Encoder (OwO) that encodes structural priors from BVH files, including joint semantics, rest-pose offsets, and skeletal topology, into skeletal embeddings; (2) a Topology-Agnostic Tokenizer (TAT) that compresses motion sequences into a universal, topology-invariant discrete representation; and (3) the Unified BVH Universe (UvU), a large-scale dataset aggregating BVH motions across heterogeneous skeletons. Experiments show that NEC achieves high-fidelity reconstruction under substantial compression and effectively disentangles motion from skeletal structure. The resulting token space supports cross-species motion transfer, composition, denoising, generation with token-based models, and text-motion retrieval, establishing a unified framework for motion analysis and synthesis across diverse morphologies. Demo page: https://animotionlab.github.io/NECromancer/

摘要（中文）: 运动标记化是可泛化运动模型的关键组成部分，然而，现有的大多数方法都局限于特定物种的骨骼，限制了其在不同形态上的应用。我们提出了NECromancer (NEC)，一种直接在任意BVH骨骼上操作的通用运动标记器。NEC由三个部分组成：（1）本体感知骨骼图编码器 (OwO)，它将来自BVH文件的结构先验，包括关节语义、静止姿势偏移和骨骼拓扑，编码成骨骼嵌入；（2）拓扑无关标记器 (TAT)，它将运动序列压缩成一个通用的、拓扑不变的离散表示；以及（3）统一的BVH宇宙 (UvU)，一个大规模数据集，聚合了来自异构骨骼的BVH运动。实验表明，NEC在显著压缩下实现了高保真度的重建，并有效地将运动与骨骼结构解耦。由此产生的标记空间支持跨物种的运动迁移、组合、去噪、基于标记模型的生成以及文本-运动检索，为不同形态的运动分析和合成建立了一个统一的框架。演示页面：https://animotionlab.github.io/NECromancer/

TLDR: The paper introduces NECromancer, a universal motion tokenizer for BVH skeletons that enables cross-species motion transfer, composition, and generation by encoding skeletal structures and motion sequences into a topology-invariant discrete representation.

Authors: Mingxi Xu, Qi Wang, Zhengyu Wen, Phong Dao Thien, Zhengyu Li, Ning Zhang, Xiaoyu He, Wei Zhao, Kehong Gong, Mingyuan Zhang

Learning Human Visual Attention on 3D Surfaces through Geometry-Queried Semantic Priors

Abstract (English): Human visual attention on three-dimensional objects emerges from the interplay between bottom-up geometric processing and top-down semantic recognition. Existing 3D saliency methods rely on hand-crafted geometric features or learning-based approaches that lack semantic awareness, failing to explain why humans fixate on semantically meaningful but geometrically unremarkable regions. We introduce SemGeo-AttentionNet, a dual-stream architecture that explicitly formalizes this dichotomy through asymmetric cross-modal fusion, leveraging diffusion-based semantic priors from geometry-conditioned multi-view rendering and point cloud transformers for geometric processing. Cross-attention ensures geometric features query semantic content, enabling bottom-up distinctiveness to guide top-down retrieval. We extend our framework to temporal scanpath generation through reinforcement learning, introducing the first formulation respecting 3D mesh topology with inhibition-of-return dynamics. Evaluation on SAL3D, NUS3D and 3DVA datasets demonstrates substantial improvements, validating how cognitively motivated architectures effectively model human visual attention on three-dimensional surfaces.

摘要（中文）: 人类对三维物体的视觉注意力源于自底向上的几何处理与自顶向下的语义识别之间的相互作用。现有的3D显著性方法依赖于手工设计的几何特征或缺乏语义感知的基于学习的方法，无法解释为什么人类会注视于语义上有意义但几何上不显著的区域。我们提出了SemGeo-AttentionNet，一个双流架构，通过非对称跨模态融合明确地形式化了这种二分法，利用基于扩散的语义先验，该先验来自几何条件下的多视角渲染和用于几何处理的点云Transformer。交叉注意力确保了几何特征查询语义内容，从而使自底向上的独特性可以引导自顶向下的检索。我们通过强化学习将我们的框架扩展到时间扫描路径生成，引入了第一个尊重3D网格拓扑并具有返回抑制动态的公式。在SAL3D、NUS3D和3DVA数据集上的评估表明，性能得到了显著提升，验证了认知驱动的架构如何有效地建模人类对三维表面的视觉注意力。

TLDR: This paper introduces SemGeo-AttentionNet, a novel architecture that combines geometric and semantic information to model human visual attention on 3D surfaces, outperforming existing methods on several datasets. It also extends to temporal scanpath generation via reinforcement learning.

Authors: Soham Pahari, Sandeep C. Kumain

SPDA-SAM: A Self-prompted Depth-Aware Segment Anything Model for Instance Segmentation

Abstract (English): Recently, Segment Anything Model (SAM) has demonstrated strong generalizability in various instance segmentation tasks. However, its performance is severely dependent on the quality of manual prompts. In addition, the RGB images that instance segmentation methods normally use inherently lack depth information. As a result, the ability of these methods to perceive spatial structures and delineate object boundaries is hindered. To address these challenges, we propose a Self-prompted Depth-Aware SAM (SPDA-SAM) for instance segmentation. Specifically, we design a Semantic-Spatial Self-prompt Module (SSSPM) which extracts the semantic and spatial prompts from the image encoder and the mask decoder of SAM, respectively. Furthermore, we introduce a Coarse-to-Fine RGB-D Fusion Module (C2FFM), in which the features extracted from a monocular RGB image and the depth map estimated from it are fused. In particular, the structural information in the depth map is used to provide coarse-grained guidance to feature fusion, while local variations in depth are encoded in order to fuse fine-grained feature representations. To our knowledge, SAM has not been explored in such self-prompted and depth-aware manners. Experimental results demonstrate that our SPDA-SAM outperforms its state-of-the-art counterparts across twelve different data sets. These promising results should be due to the guidance of the self-prompts and the compensation for the spatial information loss by the coarse-to-fine RGB-D fusion operation.

摘要（中文）: 近来，Segment Anything Model (SAM) 在各种实例分割任务中展现出强大的泛化能力。然而，其性能严重依赖于人工提示的质量。此外，实例分割方法通常使用的 RGB 图像本身缺乏深度信息。因此，这些方法感知空间结构和描绘物体边界的能力受到阻碍。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了一种自提示深度感知 SAM (SPDA-SAM) 用于实例分割。具体而言，我们设计了一个语义-空间自提示模块 (SSSPM)，其从 SAM 图像编码器和掩码解码器中分别提取语义和空间提示。此外，我们引入了一个粗到精 RGB-D 融合模块 (C2FFM)，其中融合了从单目 RGB 图像及其估计的深度图像中提取的特征。特别地，深度图中的结构信息用于为特征融合提供粗粒度指导，而深度中的局部变化被编码以融合细粒度的特征表示。据我们所知，SAM 尚未以这种自提示和深度感知的方式进行探索。实验结果表明，我们的 SPDA-SAM 在十二个不同的数据集上优于其最先进的同类方法。这些有希望的结果应归功于自提示的指导以及粗到精 RGB-D 融合操作对空间信息损失的补偿。

TLDR: The paper introduces SPDA-SAM, a self-prompted and depth-aware Segment Anything Model (SAM) for instance segmentation, which enhances SAM's performance by using semantic-spatial self-prompts and coarse-to-fine RGB-D fusion, demonstrating state-of-the-art results across twelve datasets.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了SPDA-SAM，一个自提示和深度感知的分割一切模型（SAM）用于实例分割。通过使用语义-空间自提示和粗到细的RGB-D融合，增强了SAM的性能，并在十二个数据集上展示了最先进的结果。

Authors: Yihan Shang, Wei Wang, Chao Huang, Xinghui Dong

Soft Forward-Backward Representations for Zero-shot Reinforcement Learning with General Utilities

Abstract (English): Recent advancements in zero-shot reinforcement learning (RL) have facilitated the extraction of diverse behaviors from unlabeled, offline data sources. In particular, forward-backward algorithms (FB) can retrieve a family of policies that can approximately solve any standard RL problem (with additive rewards, linear in the occupancy measure), given sufficient capacity. While retaining zero-shot properties, we tackle the greater problem class of RL with general utilities, in which the objective is an arbitrary differentiable function of the occupancy measure. This setting is strictly more expressive, capturing tasks such as distribution matching or pure exploration, which may not be reduced to additive rewards. We show that this additional complexity can be captured by a novel, maximum entropy (soft) variant of the forward-backward algorithm, which recovers a family of stochastic policies from offline data. When coupled with zero-order search over compact policy embeddings, this algorithm can sidestep iterative optimization schemes, and optimizes general utilities directly at test-time. Across both didactic and high-dimensional experiments, we demonstrate that our method retains favorable properties of FB algorithms, while also extending their range to more general RL problems.

摘要（中文）: 零样本强化学习（RL）的最新进展促进了从无标签离线数据源中提取多样化行为。 特别是，前向-后向算法（FB）可以在给定足够容量的情况下，检索出一系列策略，这些策略可以近似地解决任何标准的强化学习问题（具有可加奖励，且奖励在线性占用度量中）。 在保持零样本特性的同时，我们处理了具有更广义效用函数的强化学习问题类别，其中目标是占用度量的任意可微函数。 这种设置具有更强的表达能力，能够捕捉诸如分布匹配或纯粹探索等任务，这些任务可能无法简化为可加奖励。 我们证明了这种额外的复杂性可以被一种新颖的、最大熵（soft）变体的前向-后向算法所捕获，该算法从离线数据中恢复出一系列随机策略。 当与紧凑策略嵌入上的零阶搜索结合使用时，该算法可以绕过迭代优化方案，并在测试时直接优化广义效用函数。 在教学实验和高维实验中，我们证明了我们的方法保留了FB算法的有利特性，同时将其范围扩展到更广泛的强化学习问题。

TLDR: This paper introduces a soft forward-backward algorithm to extend zero-shot reinforcement learning to handle general utility functions in RL, enabling solutions for tasks beyond additive rewards, such as distribution matching and pure exploration, using offline data.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种软前向-后向算法，以扩展零样本强化学习，使其能够处理RL中的通用效用函数，从而可以使用离线数据解决超出加性奖励的任务，例如分布匹配和纯探索。

Authors: Marco Bagatella, Thomas Rupf, Georg Martius, Andreas Krause

Disentanglement by means of action-induced representations

Abstract (English): Learning interpretable representations with variational autoencoders (VAEs) is a major goal of representation learning. The main challenge lies in obtaining disentangled representations, where each latent dimension corresponds to a distinct generative factor. This difficulty is fundamentally tied to the inability to perform nonlinear independent component analysis. Here, we introduce the framework of action-induced representations (AIRs) which models representations of physical systems given experiments (or actions) that can be performed on them. We show that, in this framework, we can provably disentangle degrees of freedom w.r.t. their action dependence. We further introduce a variational AIR architecture (VAIR) that can extract AIRs and therefore achieve provable disentanglement where standard VAEs fail. Beyond state representation, VAIR also captures the action dependence of the underlying generative factors, directly linking experiments to the degrees of freedom they influence.

摘要（中文）: 使用变分自编码器（VAE）学习可解释的表示是表示学习的一个主要目标。主要的挑战在于获得解耦的表示，其中每个潜在维度对应一个不同的生成因子。这种困难从根本上与无法执行非线性独立成分分析有关。在此，我们引入了动作诱导表示（AIRs）的框架，该框架对给定可以对其执行的实验（或动作）的物理系统的表示进行建模。我们证明，在这个框架中，我们可以根据自由度对动作的依赖性进行可证明的解耦。我们进一步引入了一种变分AIR架构（VAIR），它可以提取AIRs，从而实现标准VAE无法实现的可证明的解耦。除了状态表示之外，VAIR还捕获了底层生成因子的动作依赖性，直接将实验与它们所影响的自由度联系起来。

TLDR: This paper introduces Action-Induced Representations (AIRs) which provably disentangle latent representations in VAEs based on the action dependence of generative factors, potentially improving interpretability and linking experiments to degrees of freedom.

简要说明: 本文介绍了动作诱导表示 (AIR)，它根据生成因子的动作依赖性，可证明地解开 VAE 中潜在表示的纠缠，从而可能提高可解释性并将实验与自由度关联起来。

Authors: Gorka Muñoz-Gil, Hendrik Poulsen Nautrup, Arunava Majumder, Paulin de Schoulepnikoff, Florian Fürrutter, Marius Krumm, Hans J. Briegel

Diffusion-State Policy Optimization for Masked Diffusion Language Models

Abstract (English): Masked diffusion language models generate by iteratively filling masked tokens over multiple denoising steps, so learning only from a terminal reward on the final completion yields coarse credit assignment over intermediate decisions. We propose DiSPO (Diffusion-State Policy Optimization), a plug-in credit-assignment layer that directly optimizes intermediate filling decisions. At selected intermediate masked states, DiSPO branches by resampling fillings for the currently masked positions from rollout-cached logits, scores the resulting completions, and updates only the newly filled tokens -- without additional multi-step diffusion rollouts. We formalize a fixed-state objective for branched completions and derive a policy-gradient estimator that can be combined with terminal-feedback policy optimization using the same rollouts. On LLaDA-8B-Instruct, DiSPO consistently improves over the terminal-feedback diffu-GRPO baseline on math and planning benchmarks under matched rollout compute and optimizer steps. Our code will be available at https://daioba.github.io/dispo .

摘要（中文）: 掩码扩散语言模型通过在多个去噪步骤中迭代填充掩码标记来生成文本，因此仅从最终完成时的终端奖励进行学习，会导致对中间决策的粗略信用分配。我们提出 DiSPO (Diffusion-State Policy Optimization，扩散状态策略优化)，这是一个插件式信用分配层，可以直接优化中间填充决策。在选定的中间掩码状态，DiSPO 通过从 rollout 缓存的 logits 重采样当前掩码位置的填充来生成分支，对生成的完成结果进行评分，并且仅更新新填充的标记——无需额外的多步扩散 rollout。我们正式确定了分支完成的固定状态目标，并推导出一个策略梯度估计器，该估计器可以与使用相同 rollout 的终端反馈策略优化相结合。在 LLaDA-8B-Instruct 上，在匹配的 rollout 计算和优化器步骤下，DiSPO 在数学和规划基准测试中始终优于终端反馈 diffu-GRPO 基线。我们的代码将在 https://daioba.github.io/dispo 上提供。

TLDR: The paper introduces DiSPO, a method for improving credit assignment in masked diffusion language models by optimizing intermediate filling decisions using a fixed-state objective and policy-gradient estimator. DiSPO improves performance on math and planning benchmarks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为DiSPO的方法，通过优化中间填充决策，改进了掩码扩散语言模型中的信用分配，使用固定状态目标和策略梯度估计器。DiSPO在数学和规划基准测试中提高了性能。

Authors: Daisuke Oba, Hiroki Furuta, Naoaki Okazaki

Online Adaptive Reinforcement Learning with Echo State Networks for Non-Stationary Dynamics

Abstract (English): Reinforcement learning (RL) policies trained in simulation often suffer from severe performance degradation when deployed in real-world environments due to non-stationary dynamics. While Domain Randomization (DR) and meta-RL have been proposed to address this issue, they typically rely on extensive pretraining, privileged information, or high computational cost, limiting their applicability to real-time and edge systems. In this paper, we propose a lightweight online adaptation framework for RL based on Reservoir Computing. Specifically, we integrate an Echo State Networks (ESNs) as an adaptation module that encodes recent observation histories into a latent context representation, and update its readout weights online using Recursive Least Squares (RLS). This design enables rapid adaptation without backpropagation, pretraining, or access to privileged information. We evaluate the proposed method on CartPole and HalfCheetah tasks with severe and abrupt environment changes, including periodic external disturbances and extreme friction variations. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed approach significantly outperforms DR and representative adaptive baselines under out-of-distribution dynamics, achieving stable adaptation within a few control steps. Notably, the method successfully handles intra-episode environment changes without resetting the policy. Due to its computational efficiency and stability, the proposed framework provides a practical solution for online adaptation in non-stationary environments and is well suited for real-world robotic control and edge deployment.

摘要（中文）: 在模拟环境中训练的强化学习（RL）策略在部署到真实世界环境时，由于非平稳动态特性，通常会遭受严重的性能下降。虽然领域随机化（DR）和元强化学习（meta-RL）已被提出用于解决这个问题，但它们通常依赖于大量的预训练、特权信息或高昂的计算成本，从而限制了它们在实时和边缘系统中的适用性。在本文中，我们提出了一种基于储层计算的轻量级强化学习在线自适应框架。具体来说，我们集成了一个回声状态网络（ESN）作为自适应模块，将最近的观测历史编码为潜在的上下文表示，并使用递归最小二乘法（RLS）在线更新其读出权重。这种设计无需反向传播、预训练或访问特权信息即可实现快速适应。我们通过CartPole和HalfCheetah任务评估了所提出的方法在剧烈和突发环境变化下的性能，包括周期性的外部干扰和极端的摩擦变化。实验结果表明，所提出的方法在分布外动态特性下明显优于领域随机化和具有代表性的自适应基线，在几个控制步骤内实现了稳定的适应。值得注意的是，该方法成功处理了情节内的环境变化，而无需重置策略。由于其计算效率和稳定性，所提出的框架为非平稳环境中的在线自适应提供了一种实用的解决方案，并且非常适合于现实世界的机器人控制和边缘部署。

TLDR: This paper introduces a lightweight online adaptive RL framework using Echo State Networks for faster adaptation to non-stationary environments, outperforming domain randomization without pretraining.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种轻量级的在线自适应强化学习框架，使用回声状态网络，可以更快地适应非平稳环境，优于领域随机化，且无需预训练。

Authors: Aoi Yoshimura, Gouhei Tanaka

Flow Matching for Offline Reinforcement Learning with Discrete Actions

Abstract (English): Generative policies based on diffusion models and flow matching have shown strong promise for offline reinforcement learning (RL), but their applicability remains largely confined to continuous action spaces. To address a broader range of offline RL settings, we extend flow matching to a general framework that supports discrete action spaces with multiple objectives. Specifically, we replace continuous flows with continuous-time Markov chains, trained using a Q-weighted flow matching objective. We then extend our design to multi-agent settings, mitigating the exponential growth of joint action spaces via a factorized conditional path. We theoretically show that, under idealized conditions, optimizing this objective recovers the optimal policy. Extensive experiments further demonstrate that our method performs robustly in practical scenarios, including high-dimensional control, multi-modal decision-making, and dynamically changing preferences over multiple objectives. Our discrete framework can also be applied to continuous-control problems through action quantization, providing a flexible trade-off between representational complexity and performance.

摘要（中文）: 基于扩散模型和流匹配的生成策略在离线强化学习（RL）中展现出强劲潜力，但其适用性仍然主要局限于连续动作空间。为了应对更广泛的离线强化学习环境，我们将流匹配扩展到一个支持离散动作空间和多目标的通用框架。具体而言，我们用连续时间马尔可夫链取代连续流，并使用Q值加权的流匹配目标进行训练。然后，我们将我们的设计扩展到多智能体环境，通过分解的条件路径来缓解联合动作空间的指数增长。我们在理论上证明，在理想条件下，优化该目标可以恢复最优策略。大量的实验进一步表明，我们的方法在实际场景中表现稳健，包括高维控制、多模态决策以及对多个目标动态变化的偏好。我们的离散框架也可以通过动作量化应用于连续控制问题，从而在表示复杂性和性能之间提供灵活的权衡。

TLDR: This paper extends flow matching for offline RL to discrete action spaces using continuous-time Markov chains and demonstrates its effectiveness in single and multi-agent settings, showcasing its applicability to various scenarios, including continuous control via action quantization.

简要说明: 本文将基于流匹配的离线强化学习扩展到离散动作空间，使用连续时间马尔可夫链，并在单智能体和多智能体环境中展示了其有效性，并证明了其在各种场景中的适用性，包括通过动作量化实现的连续控制。

Authors: Fairoz Nower Khan, Nabuat Zaman Nahim, Ruiquan Huang, Haibo Yang, Peizhong Ju

Pragmatic Curiosity: A Hybrid Learning-Optimization Paradigm via Active Inference

Abstract (English): Many engineering and scientific workflows depend on expensive black-box evaluations, requiring decision-making that simultaneously improves performance and reduces uncertainty. Bayesian optimization (BO) and Bayesian experimental design (BED) offer powerful yet largely separate treatments of goal-seeking and information-seeking, providing limited guidance for hybrid settings where learning and optimization are intrinsically coupled. We propose "pragmatic curiosity," a hybrid learning-optimization paradigm derived from active inference, in which actions are selected by minimizing the expected free energy--a single objective that couples pragmatic utility with epistemic information gain. We demonstrate the practical effectiveness and flexibility of pragmatic curiosity on various real-world hybrid tasks, including constrained system identification, targeted active search, and composite optimization with unknown preferences. Across these benchmarks, pragmatic curiosity consistently outperforms strong BO-type and BED-type baselines, delivering higher estimation accuracy, better critical-region coverage, and improved final solution quality.

摘要（中文）: 许多工程和科学工作流程依赖于昂贵的黑盒评估，因此需要进行兼顾性能提升和不确定性降低的决策。 贝叶斯优化（BO）和贝叶斯实验设计（BED）为目标导向和信息导向提供了强大的但很大程度上独立的处理方法，对于学习和优化固有耦合的混合设置，所提供的指导有限。我们提出了一种源自主动推断的混合学习-优化范式——“功利性好奇心”，其中行动的选择通过最小化期望自由能来完成，这是一个将实用效用与认知信息增益耦合在一起的单一目标。我们在一系列现实世界的混合任务中展示了功利性好奇心的实用有效性和灵活性，包括约束系统辨识、定向主动搜索以及具有未知偏好的复合优化。在这些基准测试中，功利性好奇心始终优于强大的BO型和BED型基线方法，实现了更高的估计精度、更好的临界区域覆盖和改进的最终解质量。

TLDR: This paper introduces "pragmatic curiosity," a hybrid learning-optimization paradigm based on active inference, outperforming Bayesian Optimization and Bayesian Experimental Design methods in real-world tasks that combine learning and optimization.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种基于主动推理的混合学习-优化范式“实用好奇心”，在结合学习和优化的真实世界任务中优于贝叶斯优化和贝叶斯实验设计方法。

Authors: Yingke Li, Anjali Parashar, Enlu Zhou, Chuchu Fan

Perception-Control Coupled Visual Servoing for Textureless Objects Using Keypoint-Based EKF

Abstract (English): Visual servoing is fundamental to robotic applications, enabling precise positioning and control. However, applying it to textureless objects remains a challenge due to the absence of reliable visual features. Moreover, adverse visual conditions, such as occlusions, often corrupt visual feedback, leading to reduced accuracy and instability in visual servoing. In this work, we build upon learning-based keypoint detection for textureless objects and propose a method that enhances robustness by tightly integrating perception and control in a closed loop. Specifically, we employ an Extended Kalman Filter (EKF) that integrates per-frame keypoint measurements to estimate 6D object pose, which drives pose-based visual servoing (PBVS) for control. The resulting camera motion, in turn, enhances the tracking of subsequent keypoints, effectively closing the perception-control loop. Additionally, unlike standard PBVS, we propose a probabilistic control law that computes both camera velocity and its associated uncertainty, enabling uncertainty-aware control for safe and reliable operation. We validate our approach on real-world robotic platforms using quantitative metrics and grasping experiments, demonstrating that our method outperforms traditional visual servoing techniques in both accuracy and practical application.

摘要（中文）: 视觉伺服是机器人应用的基础，能够实现精确定位和控制。然而，由于缺乏可靠的视觉特征，将其应用于无纹理物体仍然是一个挑战。此外，诸如遮挡等不利的视觉条件经常会破坏视觉反馈，导致视觉伺服的精度降低和不稳定。在这项工作中，我们基于用于无纹理物体的基于学习的关键点检测，并提出一种通过在闭环中紧密集成感知和控制来增强鲁棒性的方法。具体而言，我们采用扩展卡尔曼滤波器（EKF）来整合每帧关键点测量值，以估计6D物体姿态，从而驱动基于姿态的视觉伺服（PBVS）进行控制。由此产生的相机运动反过来又增强了后续关键点的跟踪，从而有效地闭合了感知-控制环路。此外，与标准PBVS不同，我们提出了一种概率控制律，该控制律计算相机速度及其相关的不确定性，从而实现不确定性感知控制，以实现安全可靠的操作。我们使用定量指标和抓取实验在真实世界的机器人平台上验证了我们的方法，证明了我们的方法在精度和实际应用方面都优于传统的视觉伺服技术。

TLDR: This paper proposes a perception-control coupled visual servoing method using an EKF and probabilistic control law to improve the accuracy and robustness of robotic manipulation for textureless objects, validated through real-world experiments.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种感知-控制耦合的视觉伺服方法，该方法使用扩展卡尔曼滤波器（EKF）和概率控制律，提高了机器人操作纹理缺失物体的精确性和鲁棒性，并通过真实世界的实验进行了验证。

Authors: Allen Tao, Jun Yang, Stanko Oparnica, Wenjie Xue

A 26-Gram Butterfly-Inspired Robot Achieving Autonomous Tailless Flight

Abstract (English): Flapping-wing micro air vehicles (FWMAVs) have demonstrated remarkable bio-inspired agility, yet tailless two-winged configurations remain largely unexplored due to their complex fluid-structure and wing-body coupling. Here we present \textit{AirPulse}, a 26-gram butterfly-inspired FWMAV that achieves fully onboard, closed-loop, untethered flight without auxiliary control surfaces. The AirPulse robot replicates key biomechanical traits of butterfly flight, including low wing aspect ratio, compliant carbon-fiber-reinforced wings, and low-frequency, high-amplitude flapping that induces cyclic variations in the center of gravity and moment of inertia, producing characteristic body undulation. We establish a quantitative mapping between flapping modulation parameters and force-torque generation, and introduce the Stroke Timing Asymmetry Rhythm (STAR) generator, enabling smooth, stable, and linearly parameterized wingstroke asymmetry for flapping control. Integrating these with an attitude controller, the AirPulse robot maintains pitch and yaw stability despite strong oscillatory dynamics. Free-flight experiments demonstrate stable climbing and turning maneuvers via either angle offset or stroke timing modulation, marking the first onboard controlled flight of the lightest two-winged, tailless butterfly-inspired FWMAV reported in peer-reviewed literature. This work corroborates a foundational platform for lightweight, collision-proof FWMAVs, bridging biological inspiration with practical aerial robotics. Their non-invasive maneuverability is ideally suited for real-world applications, such as confined-space inspection and ecological monitoring, inaccessible to traditional drones, while their biomechanical fidelity provides a physical model to decode the principles underlying the erratic yet efficient flight of real butterflies.

摘要（中文）: 扑翼微型飞行器（FWMAV）已展现出卓越的仿生灵活性，然而由于其复杂的流固耦合以及机翼-机身耦合，无尾双翼构型在很大程度上仍未被探索。本文介绍 \textit{AirPulse}，一款 26 克重的蝴蝶仿生 FWMAV，无需辅助控制面即可实现完全机载、闭环式、无系绳飞行。AirPulse 机器人复制了蝴蝶飞行的关键生物力学特征，包括低翼展比、柔性碳纤维增强机翼，以及低频、高振幅的扑动，从而引起重心和转动惯量的周期性变化，产生特征性的机身波动。我们建立了扑翼调制参数与力-力矩生成之间的定量映射关系，并引入了冲程时间不对称节奏（STAR）生成器，从而实现平滑、稳定且线性参数化的翼冲不对称性，以进行扑翼控制。通过将这些与姿态控制器集成，AirPulse 机器人能够在强烈的振荡动力学下保持俯仰和偏航稳定性。自由飞行实验表明，该机器人可以通过角度偏移或冲程时间调制来实现稳定的爬升和转弯机动，这标志着在同行评审文献中首次报道了最轻的采用机载控制的两翼、无尾蝴蝶仿生 FWMAV 的受控飞行。这项工作证实了轻质、防撞 FWMAV 的基础平台，将生物灵感与实际的空中机器人技术相结合。其非侵入式机动性非常适合现实应用，例如传统无人机无法进入的狭小空间检查和生态监测，而其生物力学保真度则提供了一个物理模型来解码真实蝴蝶不规则但高效飞行的背后的原理。

TLDR: This paper presents a 26-gram tailless butterfly-inspired robot, AirPulse, that achieves stable and autonomous flight using a novel control method based on wing stroke asymmetry, demonstrating its potential for applications in confined spaces.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一款26克的无尾蝴蝶仿生机器人AirPulse，它利用基于机翼冲程不对称的新型控制方法实现了稳定自主飞行，展示了其在狭小空间应用中的潜力。

Authors: Weibin Gu, Chenrui Feng, Lian Liu, Chen Yang, Xingchi Jiao, Yuhe Ding, Xiaofei Shi, Chao Gao, Alessandro Rizzo, Guyue Zhou

Efficient and Robust Modeling of Nonlinear Mechanical Systems

Abstract (English): The development of efficient and robust dynamic models is fundamental in the field of systems and control engineering. In this paper, a new formulation for the dynamic model of nonlinear mechanical systems, that can be applied to different automotive and robotic case studies, is proposed, together with a modeling procedure allowing to automatically obtain the model formulation. Compared with the Euler-Lagrange formulation, the proposed model is shown to give superior performances in terms of robustness against measurement noise for systems exhibiting dependence on some external variables, as well as in terms of execution time when computing the inverse dynamics of the system.

摘要（中文）: 高效且鲁棒的动态模型开发是系统与控制工程领域的基础。本文提出了一种新的非线性机械系统动态模型公式，可应用于不同的汽车和机器人案例研究，并提供了一种建模程序，可以自动获得模型公式。与 Euler-Lagrange 公式相比，对于依赖某些外部变量的系统，所提出的模型在抗测量噪声方面表现出更优越的性能，并且在计算系统逆动力学时，执行时间也更短。

TLDR: This paper presents a novel dynamic model formulation for nonlinear mechanical systems, claiming improved robustness against measurement noise and faster inverse dynamics computation compared to the Euler-Lagrange method, with automotive and robotic applications.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种用于非线性机械系统的新型动态模型公式，声称与欧拉-拉格朗日方法相比，在测量噪声方面具有更高的鲁棒性，并且逆动力学计算速度更快，适用于汽车和机器人领域。

Authors: Davide Tebaldi, Roberto Zanasi

TFusionOcc: Student's t-Distribution Based Object-Centric Multi-Sensor Fusion Framework for 3D Occupancy Prediction

Abstract (English): 3D semantic occupancy prediction enables autonomous vehicles (AVs) to perceive fine-grained geometric and semantic structure of their surroundings from onboard sensors, which is essential for safe decision-making and navigation. Recent models for 3D semantic occupancy prediction have successfully addressed the challenge of describing real-world objects with varied shapes and classes. However, the intermediate representations used by existing methods for 3D semantic occupancy prediction rely heavily on 3D voxel volumes or a set of 3D Gaussians, hindering the model's ability to efficiently and effectively capture fine-grained geometric details in the 3D driving environment. This paper introduces TFusionOcc, a novel object-centric multi-sensor fusion framework for predicting 3D semantic occupancy. By leveraging multi-stage multi-sensor fusion, Student's t-distribution, and the T-Mixture model (TMM), together with more geometrically flexible primitives, such as the deformable superquadric (superquadric with inverse warp), the proposed method achieved state-of-the-art (SOTA) performance on the nuScenes benchmark. In addition, extensive experiments were conducted on the nuScenes-C dataset to demonstrate the robustness of the proposed method in different camera and lidar corruption scenarios. The code will be available at: https://github.com/DanielMing123/TFusionOcc

摘要（中文）: 3D语义占据预测使自动驾驶车辆 (AVs) 能够利用车载传感器感知周围环境的精细几何和语义结构，这对于安全决策和导航至关重要。 近期用于3D语义占据预测的模型已经成功地解决了描述具有不同形状和类别的真实世界物体的挑战。 然而，现有3D语义占据预测方法使用的中间表示形式严重依赖于3D体素卷或一组3D高斯分布，从而阻碍了模型高效且有效地捕捉3D驾驶环境中精细几何细节的能力。 本文介绍了一种新颖的、以对象为中心的3D语义占据预测多传感器融合框架TFusionOcc。 通过利用多阶段多传感器融合、学生t分布和T-混合模型 (TMM)，以及更具几何灵活性的基元，例如可变形超二次曲面（具有逆向扭曲的超二次曲面），所提出的方法在nuScenes基准测试上实现了最先进 (SOTA) 的性能。 此外，在nuScenes-C数据集上进行了大量实验，以证明所提出的方法在不同的相机和激光雷达损坏场景中的鲁棒性。 代码将在以下地址开放获取：https://github.com/DanielMing123/TFusionOcc

TLDR: This paper introduces TFusionOcc, a novel multi-sensor fusion framework using Student's t-distribution and deformable superquadrics for 3D semantic occupancy prediction, achieving SOTA results on nuScenes and showing robustness to sensor corruption.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为TFusionOcc的新型多传感器融合框架，该框架使用Student's t分布和可变形超二次曲面进行3D语义占用预测，在nuScenes上实现了SOTA结果，并显示出对传感器损坏的鲁棒性。

Authors: Zhenxing Ming, Julie Stephany Berrio, Mao Shan, Stewart Worrall

A High-Fidelity Robotic Manipulator Teleoperation Framework for Human-Centered Augmented Reality Evaluation

Abstract (English): Validating Augmented Reality (AR) tracking and interaction models requires precise, repeatable ground-truth motion. However, human users cannot reliably perform consistent motion due to biomechanical variability. Robotic manipulators are promising to act as human motion proxies if they can mimic human movements. In this work, we design and implement ARBot, a real-time teleoperation platform that can effectively capture natural human motion and accurately replay the movements via robotic manipulators. ARBot includes two capture models: stable wrist motion capture via a custom CV and IMU pipeline, and natural 6-DOF control via a mobile application. We design a proactively-safe QP controller to ensure smooth, jitter-free execution of the robotic manipulator, enabling it to function as a high-fidelity record and replay physical proxy. We open-source ARBot and release a benchmark dataset of 132 human and synthetic trajectories captured using ARBot to support controllable and scalable AR evaluation.

摘要（中文）: 验证增强现实 (AR) 追踪和交互模型需要精确且可重复的真值运动。然而，由于生物力学变异性，人类用户无法可靠地执行一致的运动。如果机器人机械臂能够模仿人类运动，它们有望充当人类运动代理。在这项工作中，我们设计并实现了 ARBot，一个实时遥操作平台，可以有效地捕捉自然的人类运动，并通过机器人机械臂精确地重放这些运动。 ARBot 包含两种捕捉模型：通过定制的 CV 和 IMU 流水线实现的稳定腕部运动捕捉，以及通过移动应用程序实现的自然 6 自由度控制。我们设计了一个主动安全的 QP 控制器，以确保机器人机械臂平稳、无抖动地执行运动，使其能够作为高保真记录和重放物理代理发挥作用。我们开源了 ARBot，并发布了一个包含 132 条使用 ARBot 捕捉的人类和合成轨迹的基准数据集，以支持可控且可扩展的 AR 评估。

TLDR: The paper introduces ARBot, a teleoperation platform for robotic manipulators using AR-based human motion capture, and releases a benchmark dataset for AR evaluation.

Authors: Harsh Chhajed, Tian Guo

Active Localization of Unstable Systems with Coarse Information

Abstract (English): We study localization and control for unstable systems under coarse, single-bit sensing. Motivated by understanding the fundamental limitations imposed by such minimal feedback, we identify sufficient conditions under which the initial state can be recovered despite instability and extremely sparse measurements. Building on these conditions, we develop an active localization algorithm that integrates a set-based estimator with a control strategy derived from Voronoi partitions, which provably estimates the initial state while ensuring the agent remains in informative regions. Under the derived conditions, the proposed approach guarantees exponential contraction of the initial-state uncertainty, and the result is further supported by numerical experiments. These findings can offer theoretical insight into localization in robotics, where sensing is often limited to coarse abstractions such as keyframes, segmentations, or line-based features.

摘要（中文）: 我们研究了在粗糙的、单比特感知下不稳定系统的定位与控制问题。出于理解这种极简反馈所带来的根本性限制，我们确定了在不稳定性和极其稀疏的测量条件下，初始状态可以被恢复的充分条件。基于这些条件，我们开发了一种主动定位算法，该算法将基于集合的估计器与源于Voronoi划分的控制策略相结合，可证明地估计初始状态，同时确保智能体保持在信息丰富的区域。在推导出的条件下，所提出的方法保证了初始状态不确定性的指数收缩，并且该结果得到了数值实验的进一步支持。这些发现可以为机器人领域的定位提供理论见解，在该领域中，感知通常仅限于粗糙的抽象，例如关键帧、分割或基于线条的特征。

TLDR: This paper presents an active localization algorithm for unstable systems with coarse sensing, demonstrating provable exponential contraction of initial-state uncertainty.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种针对具有粗略感测的不稳定系统的主动定位算法，证明了初始状态不确定性的指数收缩。

Authors: Ege Yuceel, Daniel Liberzon, Sayan Mitra

The SLAM Confidence Trap

Abstract (English): The SLAM community has fallen into a "Confidence Trap" by prioritizing benchmark scores over principled uncertainty estimation. This yields systems that are geometrically accurate but probabilitistically inconsistent and brittle. We advocate for a paradigm shift where the consistent, real-time computation of uncertainty becomes a primary metric of success.

摘要（中文）: SLAM领域因过度追求基准测试高分而忽略了有原则性的不确定性估计，已陷入“置信陷阱”。 这导致系统在几何精度上表现良好，但在概率上不一致且脆弱。 我们提倡一种范式转变，将不确定性的持续、实时计算作为衡量成功的首要指标。

TLDR: This paper critiques the SLAM community's over-reliance on benchmark scores at the expense of robust uncertainty estimation, advocating for a paradigm shift towards prioritizing probabilistic consistency in real-time SLAM systems.

Authors: Sebastian Sansoni, Santiago Ramón Tosetti Sanz

Rebenchmarking Unsupervised Monocular 3D Occupancy Prediction

Abstract (English): Inferring the 3D structure from a single image, particularly in occluded regions, remains a fundamental yet unsolved challenge in vision-centric autonomous driving. Existing unsupervised approaches typically train a neural radiance field and treat the network outputs as occupancy probabilities during evaluation, overlooking the inconsistency between training and evaluation protocols. Moreover, the prevalent use of 2D ground truth fails to reveal the inherent ambiguity in occluded regions caused by insufficient geometric constraints. To address these issues, this paper presents a reformulated benchmark for unsupervised monocular 3D occupancy prediction. We first interpret the variables involved in the volume rendering process and identify the most physically consistent representation of the occupancy probability. Building on these analyses, we improve existing evaluation protocols by aligning the newly identified representation with voxel-wise 3D occupancy ground truth, thereby enabling unsupervised methods to be evaluated in a manner consistent with that of supervised approaches. Additionally, to impose explicit constraints in occluded regions, we introduce an occlusion-aware polarization mechanism that incorporates multi-view visual cues to enhance discrimination between occupied and free spaces in these regions. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our approach not only significantly outperforms existing unsupervised approaches but also matches the performance of supervised ones. Our source code and evaluation protocol will be made available upon publication.

摘要（中文）: 以下是一个单张图像中推断3D结构，尤其是在遮挡区域，仍然是基于视觉的自动驾驶中一个根本却未解决的挑战。现有的无监督方法通常训练一个神经辐射场，并在评估过程中将网络输出视为占用概率，忽略了训练和评估规程之间的不一致性。此外，2D真值的普遍使用未能揭示由几何约束不足引起的遮挡区域中固有的模糊性。为了解决这些问题，本文提出了一个改进的无监督单目3D占用预测基准。我们首先解释了体渲染过程中涉及的变量，并确定了占用概率的最物理一致的表示。基于这些分析，我们通过将新确定的表示与体素化的3D占用真值对齐，从而改进了现有的评估协议，使无监督方法能够以与监督方法一致的方式进行评估。此外，为了在遮挡区域施加显式约束，我们引入了一种遮挡感知极化机制，该机制结合了多视角的视觉线索，以增强这些区域中占用空间和自由空间之间的辨别能力。大量实验表明，我们的方法不仅显著优于现有的无监督方法，而且还达到了与监督方法相当的性能。我们的源代码和评估协议将在发布后公开。

TLDR: The paper re-benchmarks unsupervised monocular 3D occupancy prediction by identifying a more physically consistent occupancy representation, improving evaluation protocols with voxel-wise 3D ground truth, and introducing an occlusion-aware polarization mechanism, achieving performance comparable to supervised methods.

简要说明: 该论文重新评估了无监督单目3D占据预测，通过识别更符合物理的占据表示，改进了具有体素级3D真实数据的评估协议，并引入了一种考虑遮挡的极化机制，实现了与有监督方法相当的性能。

Authors: Zizhan Guo, Yi Feng, Mengtan Zhang, Haoran Zhang, Wei Ye, Rui Fan

Instance-Free Domain Adaptive Object Detection

Abstract (English): While Domain Adaptive Object Detection (DAOD) has made significant strides, most methods rely on unlabeled target data that is assumed to contain sufficient foreground instances. However, in many practical scenarios (e.g., wildlife monitoring, lesion detection), collecting target domain data with objects of interest is prohibitively costly, whereas background-only data is abundant. This common practical constraint introduces a significant technical challenge: the difficulty of achieving domain alignment when target instances are unavailable, forcing adaptation to rely solely on the target background information. We formulate this challenge as the novel problem of Instance-Free Domain Adaptive Object Detection. To tackle this, we propose the Relational and Structural Consistency Network (RSCN) which pioneers an alignment strategy based on background feature prototypes while simultaneously encouraging consistency in the relationship between the source foreground features and the background features within each domain, enabling robust adaptation even without target instances. To facilitate research, we further curate three specialized benchmarks, including simulative auto-driving detection, wildlife detection, and lung nodule detection. Extensive experiments show that RSCN significantly outperforms existing DAOD methods across all three benchmarks in the instance-free scenario. The code and benchmarks will be released soon.

摘要（中文）: 域自适应目标检测（DAOD）已经取得了显著进展，但大多数方法依赖于假定包含足够前景实例的未标注目标域数据。然而，在许多实际场景中（例如，野生动物监测、病灶检测），收集包含感兴趣对象的目标域数据成本高昂，而仅包含背景的数据则非常丰富。这种常见的实际约束带来了一个重大的技术挑战：当目标实例不可用时，域对齐的难度，迫使自适应完全依赖于目标背景信息。我们把这个挑战定义为实例无关域自适应目标检测这一新问题。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了关系和结构一致性网络（RSCN），它率先提出了一种基于背景特征原型对齐的策略，同时鼓励源域前景特征和每个域内的背景特征之间关系的一致性，从而即使没有目标实例也能实现稳健的自适应。为了方便研究，我们进一步策划了三个专门的基准测试，包括模拟自动驾驶检测、野生动物检测和肺结节检测。大量实验表明，在实例无关场景下，RSCN在所有三个基准测试中都显著优于现有的DAOD方法。代码和基准测试即将发布。

TLDR: The paper introduces Instance-Free Domain Adaptive Object Detection, a novel problem where target domain object detection must adapt without foreground instances, and proposes a Relational and Structural Consistency Network (RSCN) to address it.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种新的问题，即无实例领域自适应目标检测，其中目标域目标检测必须在没有前景实例的情况下进行自适应，并提出了一种关系和结构一致性网络 (RSCN) 来解决这个问题。

Authors: Hengfu Yu, Jinhong Deng, Lixin Duan, Wen Li

A neuromorphic model of the insect visual system for natural image processing

Abstract (English): Insect vision supports complex behaviors including associative learning, navigation, and object detection, and has long motivated computational models for understanding biological visual processing. However, many contemporary models prioritize task performance while neglecting biologically grounded processing pathways. Here, we introduce a bio-inspired vision model that captures principles of the insect visual system to transform dense visual input into sparse, discriminative codes. The model is trained using a fully self-supervised contrastive objective, enabling representation learning without labeled data and supporting reuse across tasks without reliance on domain-specific classifiers. We evaluated the resulting representations on flower recognition tasks and natural image benchmarks. The model consistently produced reliable sparse codes that distinguish visually similar inputs. To support different modelling and deployment uses, we have implemented the model as both an artificial neural network and a spiking neural network. In a simulated localization setting, our approach outperformed a simple image downsampling comparison baseline, highlighting the functional benefit of incorporating neuromorphic visual processing pathways. Collectively, these results advance insect computational modelling by providing a generalizable bio-inspired vision model capable of sparse computation across diverse tasks.

摘要（中文）: 昆虫视觉支持复杂的行为，包括联想学习、导航和物体检测，长期以来一直激励着用于理解生物视觉处理的计算模型。然而，许多当代模型优先考虑任务性能，而忽略了生物学基础的处理通路。在此，我们介绍了一种受生物启发的视觉模型，该模型捕捉了昆虫视觉系统的原理，将密集的视觉输入转化为稀疏且具有区分性的编码。该模型使用完全自监督的对比目标进行训练，无需标记数据即可实现表征学习，并支持跨任务的重用，而无需依赖于特定领域的分类器。我们评估了所得表征在花朵识别任务和自然图像基准上的表现。该模型始终如一地产生可靠的稀疏编码，从而区分视觉上相似的输入。为了支持不同的建模和部署用途，我们已将该模型实现为人工神经网络和脉冲神经网络。在模拟的定位环境中，我们的方法优于简单的图像下采样比较基线，突出了结合神经形态视觉处理通路的功能优势。总的来说，这些结果通过提供一种通用的、受生物启发的视觉模型，该模型能够在各种任务中进行稀疏计算，从而推进了昆虫计算建模。

TLDR: This paper introduces a biologically-inspired, self-supervised neuromorphic vision model based on insect visual systems, demonstrating sparse and discriminative representation learning for flower recognition and natural image tasks.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种受生物学启发的、基于昆虫视觉系统的自监督神经形态视觉模型，展示了用于花朵识别和自然图像任务的稀疏和区分性表示学习。

Authors: Adam D. Hines, Karin Nordström, Andrew B. Barron

ForeHOI: Feed-forward 3D Object Reconstruction from Daily Hand-Object Interaction Videos

Abstract (English): The ubiquity of monocular videos capturing daily hand-object interactions presents a valuable resource for embodied intelligence. While 3D hand reconstruction from in-the-wild videos has seen significant progress, reconstructing the involved objects remains challenging due to severe occlusions and the complex, coupled motion of the camera, hands, and object. In this paper, we introduce ForeHOI, a novel feed-forward model that directly reconstructs 3D object geometry from monocular hand-object interaction videos within one minute of inference time, eliminating the need for any pre-processing steps. Our key insight is that, the joint prediction of 2D mask inpainting and 3D shape completion in a feed-forward framework can effectively address the problem of severe occlusion in monocular hand-held object videos, thereby achieving results that outperform the performance of optimization-based methods. The information exchanges between the 2D and 3D shape completion boosts the overall reconstruction quality, enabling the framework to effectively handle severe hand-object occlusion. Furthermore, to support the training of our model, we contribute the first large-scale, high-fidelity synthetic dataset of hand-object interactions with comprehensive annotations. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ForeHOI achieves state-of-the-art performance in object reconstruction, significantly outperforming previous methods with around a 100x speedup. Code and data are available at: https://github.com/Tao-11-chen/ForeHOI.

摘要（中文）: 捕捉日常手部与物体交互的单目视频随处可见，为具身智能提供了宝贵的资源。虽然从真实场景的视频中进行3D手部重建已取得显著进展，但由于严重的遮挡以及相机、手部和物体复杂的耦合运动，重建涉及的物体仍然具有挑战性。在本文中，我们提出了一种新颖的前馈模型ForeHOI，该模型可以直接从单目手部-物体交互视频中重建3D物体几何形状，且推理时间在一分钟内，无需任何预处理步骤。我们的核心思想是，在前馈框架中联合预测2D掩模修复和3D形状补全可以有效地解决单目手持物体视频中严重的遮挡问题，从而实现优于基于优化方法的效果。2D和3D形状补全的信息交换提高了整体重建质量，使该框架能够有效地处理严重的手部-物体遮挡。此外，为了支持我们模型的训练，我们贡献了第一个大规模、高保真的手部-物体交互合成数据集，其中包含全面的标注。大量实验表明，ForeHOI在物体重建方面实现了最先进的性能，相比以往的方法，速度提升了约100倍。代码和数据可在以下网址获取：https://github.com/Tao-11-chen/ForeHOI。

TLDR: The paper introduces ForeHOI, a feed-forward model for fast 3D object reconstruction from monocular hand-object interaction videos, achieving state-of-the-art performance and a significant speedup compared to existing methods, along with a new synthetic dataset.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了ForeHOI，一种用于从单目手-物体交互视频中快速进行3D物体重建的前馈模型，与现有方法相比实现了最先进的性能和显著的加速，并提供了一个新的合成数据集。

Authors: Yuantao Chen, Jiahao Chang, Chongjie Ye, Chaoran Zhang, Zhaojie Fang, Chenghong Li, Xiaoguang Han

DroneKey++: A Size Prior-free Method and New Benchmark for Drone 3D Pose Estimation from Sequential Images

Abstract (English): Accurate 3D pose estimation of drones is essential for security and surveillance systems. However, existing methods often rely on prior drone information such as physical sizes or 3D meshes. At the same time, current datasets are small-scale, limited to single models, and collected under constrained environments, which makes reliable validation of generalization difficult. We present DroneKey++, a prior-free framework that jointly performs keypoint detection, drone classification, and 3D pose estimation. The framework employs a keypoint encoder for simultaneous keypoint detection and classification, and a pose decoder that estimates 3D pose using ray-based geometric reasoning and class embeddings. To address dataset limitations, we construct 6DroneSyn, a large-scale synthetic benchmark with over 50K images covering 7 drone models and 88 outdoor backgrounds, generated using 360-degree panoramic synthesis. Experiments show that DroneKey++ achieves MAE 17.34 deg and MedAE 17.1 deg for rotation, MAE 0.135 m and MedAE 0.242 m for translation, with inference speeds of 19.25 FPS (CPU) and 414.07 FPS (GPU), demonstrating both strong generalization across drone models and suitability for real-time applications. The dataset is publicly available.

摘要（中文）: 无人机的精确3D姿态估计对于安全和监控系统至关重要。然而，现有方法通常依赖于无人机的先验信息，例如物理尺寸或3D网格模型。同时，目前的数据集规模较小，仅限于单一模型，并且是在受限环境下收集的，这使得可靠的泛化验证变得困难。我们提出了DroneKey++，一个无需先验信息的框架，可联合执行关键点检测、无人机分类和3D姿态估计。该框架采用关键点编码器，用于同步进行关键点检测和分类，以及一个姿态解码器，该解码器利用基于射线几何推理和类别嵌入来估计3D姿态。为了解决数据集的局限性，我们构建了6DroneSyn，一个大规模合成基准，包含超过5万张图像，涵盖7种无人机模型和88种室外背景，该基准是使用360度全景合成生成的。实验表明，DroneKey++在旋转上的平均绝对误差(MAE)为17.34度，中值绝对误差(MedAE)为17.1度，在平移上的平均绝对误差(MAE)为0.135米，中值绝对误差(MedAE)为0.242米，推理速度为19.25 FPS (CPU)和414.07 FPS (GPU)，这证明了其在不同无人机模型上的强大泛化能力以及适用于实时应用的能力。该数据集已公开。

TLDR: The paper introduces DroneKey++, a prior-free framework for 3D drone pose estimation from sequential images, along with a large-scale synthetic dataset (6DroneSyn) to address generalization limitations of existing methods. The method shows good performance and real-time capabilities.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了DroneKey++，一个无需先验信息的无人机三维姿态估计框架，以及一个大型合成数据集（6DroneSyn），旨在解决现有方法的泛化局限性。该方法表现出良好的性能和实时性。
