Authors: Seo-Bin Hwang, Yeong-Jun Cho

A first realization of reinforcement learning-based closed-loop EEG-TMS

Abstract (English): Background: Transcranial magnetic stimulation (TMS) is a powerful tool to investigate neurophysiology of the human brain and treat brain disorders. Traditionally, therapeutic TMS has been applied in a one-size-fits-all approach, disregarding inter- and intra-individual differences. Brain state-dependent EEG-TMS, such as coupling TMS with a pre-specified phase of the sensorimotor mu-rhythm, enables the induction of differential neuroplastic effects depending on the targeted phase. But this approach is still user-dependent as it requires defining an a-priori target phase. Objectives: To present a first realization of a machine-learning-based, closed-loop real-time EEG-TMS setup to identify user-independently the individual mu-rhythm phase associated with high- vs. low-corticospinal excitability states. Methods: We applied EEG-TMS to 25 participants targeting the supplementary motor area-primary motor cortex network and used a reinforcement learning algorithm to identify the mu-rhythm phase associated with high- vs. low corticospinal excitability. We employed linear mixed effects models and Bayesian analysis to determine effects of reinforced learning on corticospinal excitability indexed by motor evoked potential amplitude, and functional connectivity indexed by the imaginary part of resting-state EEG coherence. Results: Reinforcement learning effectively identified the mu-rhythm phase associated with high- vs. low-excitability states, and their repetitive stimulation resulted in long-term increases vs. decreases in functional connectivity in the stimulated sensorimotor network. Conclusions: We demonstrated for the first time the feasibility of closed-loop EEG-TMS in humans, a critical step towards individualized treatment of brain disorders.

摘要（中文）: 背景：经颅磁刺激（TMS）是一种研究人脑神经生理学和治疗脑部疾病的强大工具。传统上，治疗性TMS采用一刀切的方法，忽略了个体间和个体内的差异。脑状态依赖性EEG-TMS，例如将TMS与感觉运动μ节律的预定相位耦合，能够根据靶向相位诱导不同的神经可塑性效应。但这种方法仍然依赖于用户，因为它需要预先定义目标相位。目的：展示一种基于机器学习的闭环实时EEG-TMS设置的首次实现，以用户独立的方式识别与高皮质脊髓兴奋性状态与低皮质脊髓兴奋性状态相关的个体μ节律相位。方法：我们对25名参与者应用EEG-TMS，靶向辅助运动区-初级运动皮层网络，并使用强化学习算法来识别与高/低皮质脊髓兴奋性相关的μ节律相位。我们采用线性混合效应模型和贝叶斯分析来确定强化学习对皮质脊髓兴奋性的影响，通过运动诱发电位幅度进行评估，以及对静息态脑电相干性的虚部进行评估的功能连接。结果：强化学习有效地识别了与高/低兴奋性状态相关的μ节律相位，并且它们的重复刺激导致刺激的感觉运动网络中功能连接的长期增加与减少。结论：我们首次证明了闭环EEG-TMS在人类中的可行性，这是实现脑部疾病个性化治疗的关键一步。

TLDR: This paper presents a closed-loop EEG-TMS system using reinforcement learning to personalize brain stimulation, achieving long-term modulation of functional connectivity in the sensorimotor network.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种基于强化学习的闭环脑电-TMS系统，用于个性化脑刺激，实现了感觉运动网络功能连接的长期调节。

Authors: Dania Humaidan, Jiahua Xu, Jing Chen, Christoph Zrenner, David Emanuel Vetter, Laura Marzetti, Paolo Belardinelli, Timo Roine, Risto J. Ilmoniemi, Gian Luca Romani, Ulf Zieman

The hidden risks of temporal resampling in clinical reinforcement learning

Abstract (English): Offline reinforcement learning (ORL) has shown potential for improving decision-making in healthcare. However, contemporary research typically aggregates patient data into fixed time intervals, simplifying their mapping to standard ORL frameworks. The impact of these temporal manipulations on model safety and efficacy remains poorly understood. In this work, using both a gridworld navigation task and the UVA/Padova clinical diabetes simulator, we demonstrate that temporal resampling significantly degrades the performance of offline reinforcement learning algorithms during live deployment. We propose three mechanisms that drive this failure: (i) the generation of counterfactual trajectories, (ii) the distortion of temporal expectations, and (iii) the compounding of generalisation errors. Crucially, we find that standard off-policy evaluation metrics can fail to detect these drops in performance. Our findings reveal a fundamental risk in current healthcare ORL pipelines and emphasise the need for methods that explicitly handle the irregular timing of clinical decision-making.

摘要（中文）: 离线强化学习(ORL)已显示出在提升医疗保健决策方面的潜力。然而，当前的研究通常将患者数据聚合到固定的时间间隔内，从而简化了其到标准ORL框架的映射。这些时间操纵对模型安全性和有效性的影响仍然知之甚少。 在这项工作中，我们使用网格世界导航任务和UVA/Padova临床糖尿病模拟器，证明了时间重采样会显著降低离线强化学习算法在实时部署期间的性能。我们提出了导致这种失败的三个机制：（i）反事实轨迹的生成，（ii）时间期望的扭曲，以及（iii）泛化误差的累积。 关键是，我们发现标准的离策略评估指标可能无法检测到这些性能下降。我们的研究结果揭示了当前医疗保健ORL流程中的一个根本风险，并强调了对明确处理临床决策不规则时间问题的方法的需求。

TLDR: This paper identifies and analyzes the risks of temporal resampling in offline reinforcement learning within healthcare, showing performance degradation and evaluation metric failures, highlighting the need for handling irregular clinical data timing.

简要说明: 该论文识别并分析了医疗保健领域离线强化学习中时间重采样的风险，展示了性能下降和评估指标失效的问题，强调了处理不规则临床数据时间的需求。

Authors: Thomas Frost, Hrisheekesh Vaidya, Steve Harris

Curiosity is Knowledge: Self-Consistent Learning and No-Regret Optimization with Active Inference

Abstract (English): Active inference (AIF) unifies exploration and exploitation by minimizing the Expected Free Energy (EFE), balancing epistemic value (information gain) and pragmatic value (task performance) through a curiosity coefficient. Yet it has been unclear when this balance yields both coherent learning and efficient decision-making: insufficient curiosity can drive myopic exploitation and prevent uncertainty resolution, while excessive curiosity can induce unnecessary exploration and regret. We establish the first theoretical guarantee for EFE-minimizing agents, showing that a single requirement--sufficient curiosity--simultaneously ensures self-consistent learning (Bayesian posterior consistency) and no-regret optimization (bounded cumulative regret). Our analysis characterizes how this mechanism depends on initial uncertainty, identifiability, and objective alignment, thereby connecting AIF to classical Bayesian experimental design and Bayesian optimization within one theoretical framework. We further translate these theories into practical design guidelines for tuning the epistemic-pragmatic trade-off in hybrid learning-optimization problems, validated through real-world experiments.

摘要（中文）: 主动推理 (AIF) 通过最小化期望自由能 (EFE) 来统一探索和利用，并通过好奇心系数来平衡认知价值（信息增益）和实用价值（任务表现）。然而，这种平衡何时能够产生连贯的学习和高效的决策，一直不清楚：不足的好奇心会导致短视的利用并阻止不确定性的解决，而过度的好奇心会导致不必要的探索和后悔。 我们为最小化期望自由能的智能体建立了第一个理论保证，表明一个单一的要求 —— 足够的好奇心 —— 同时确保了自洽的学习（贝叶斯后验一致性）和无悔优化（有界累积后悔）。 我们的分析刻画了这种机制如何依赖于初始不确定性、可识别性和目标对齐，从而将 AIF 连接到经典贝叶斯实验设计和贝叶斯优化，并将其置于一个理论框架中。 我们进一步将这些理论转化为实际的设计指南，以调整混合学习-优化问题中的认知-实用权衡，并通过真实世界的实验进行验证。

TLDR: This paper provides theoretical guarantees for Active Inference (AIF) agents, showing that sufficient curiosity ensures both self-consistent learning and no-regret optimization, and validates these findings with real-world experiments.

简要说明: 该论文为主动推理 (AIF) 智能体提供了理论保证，证明了足够的求知欲可以确保自我一致的学习和无悔优化，并通过真实世界的实验验证这些发现。

Authors: Yingke Li, Anjali Parashar, Enlu Zhou, Chuchu Fan

Airspace-aware Contingency Landing Planning

Abstract (English): This paper develops a real-time, search-based aircraft contingency landing planner that minimizes traffic disruptions while accounting for ground risk. The airspace model captures dense air traffic departure and arrival flows, helicopter corridors, and prohibited zones and is demonstrated with a Washington, D.C., area case study. Historical Automatic Dependent Surveillance-Broadcast (ADS-B) data are processed to estimate air traffic density. A low-latency computational geometry algorithm generates proximity-based heatmaps around high-risk corridors and restricted regions. Airspace risk is quantified as the cumulative exposure time of a landing trajectory within congested regions, while ground risk is assessed from overflown population density to jointly guide trajectory selection. A landing site selection module further mitigates disruption to nominal air traffic operations. Benchmarking against minimum-risk Dubins solutions demonstrates that the proposed planner achieves lower joint risk and reduced airspace disruption while maintaining real-time performance. Under airspace-risk-only conditions, the planner generates trajectories within an average of 2.9 seconds on a laptop computer. Future work will incorporate dynamic air traffic updates to enable spatiotemporal contingency landing planning that minimizes the need for real-time traffic rerouting.

摘要（中文）: 本文开发了一种基于搜索的飞机应急着陆实时规划器，该规划器在考虑地面风险的同时，最大限度地减少交通中断。空域模型捕获了密集的空中交通起降流量、直升机走廊和禁飞区，并以华盛顿特区区域案例研究为例进行了演示。历史自动相关监视广播（ADS-B）数据经过处理，用于估计空中交通密度。一种低延迟的计算几何算法生成基于邻近度的高风险走廊和限制区域热图。空域风险被量化为着陆轨迹在拥堵区域内的累积暴露时间，而地面风险则根据飞越的人口密度进行评估，从而共同指导轨迹选择。着陆点选择模块进一步减轻了对正常空中交通运营的干扰。与最小风险杜宾斯解的基准测试表明，所提出的规划器实现了更低的联合风险和减少的空域中断，同时保持了实时性能。在仅考虑空域风险的条件下，该规划器在一台笔记本电脑上平均用时2.9秒生成轨迹。未来的工作将结合动态空中交通更新，以实现时空应急着陆规划，从而最大限度地减少实时交通重新规划的需求。

TLDR: This paper presents a real-time contingency landing planner that minimizes traffic disruptions and ground risk using historical ADS-B data and computational geometry to model airspace risk. It could provide a useful environment or test-bed for robotics applications.

Authors: H. Emre Tekaslan, Ella M. Atkins

ASMa: Asymmetric Spatio-temporal Masking for Skeleton Action Representation Learning

Abstract (English): Self-supervised learning (SSL) has shown remarkable success in skeleton-based action recognition by leveraging data augmentations to learn meaningful representations. However, existing SSL methods rely on data augmentations that predominantly focus on masking high-motion frames and high-degree joints such as joints with degree 3 or 4. This results in biased and incomplete feature representations that struggle to generalize across varied motion patterns. To address this, we propose Asymmetric Spatio-temporal Masking (ASMa) for Skeleton Action Representation Learning, a novel combination of masking to learn a full spectrum of spatio-temporal dynamics inherent in human actions. ASMa employs two complementary masking strategies: one that selectively masks high-degree joints and low-motion, and another that masks low-degree joints and high-motion frames. These masking strategies ensure a more balanced and comprehensive skeleton representation learning. Furthermore, we introduce a learnable feature alignment module to effectively align the representations learned from both masked views. To facilitate deployment in resource-constrained settings and on low-resource devices, we compress the learned and aligned representation into a lightweight model using knowledge distillation. Extensive experiments on NTU RGB+D 60, NTU RGB+D 120, and PKU-MMD datasets demonstrate that our approach outperforms existing SSL methods with an average improvement of 2.7-4.4% in fine-tuning and up to 5.9% in transfer learning to noisy datasets and achieves competitive performance compared to fully supervised baselines. Our distilled model achieves 91.4% parameter reduction and 3x faster inference on edge devices while maintaining competitive accuracy, enabling practical deployment in resource-constrained scenarios.

摘要（中文）: 自监督学习(SSL)通过利用数据增强来学习有意义的表征，在基于骨骼的动作识别中表现出了显著的成功。然而，现有的SSL方法依赖于主要集中于掩蔽高运动帧和高阶关节（例如度数为3或4的关节）的数据增强。这导致了有偏且不完整的特征表征，难以泛化到各种运动模式中。为了解决这个问题，我们提出用于骨骼动作表征学习的非对称时空掩蔽(ASMa)，这是一种新颖的掩蔽组合方法，用于学习人类动作中固有的完整时空动力学。ASMa采用两种互补的掩蔽策略：一种选择性地掩蔽高阶关节和低运动，另一种掩蔽低阶关节和高运动帧。这些掩蔽策略确保了更平衡和全面的骨骼表征学习。此外，我们引入了一个可学习的特征对齐模块，以有效地对齐从两个掩蔽视图学习到的表征。为了便于在资源受限的环境和低资源设备上的部署，我们使用知识蒸馏将学习和对齐后的表征压缩成一个轻量级模型。在NTU RGB+D 60, NTU RGB+D 120和PKU-MMD数据集上的大量实验表明，我们的方法优于现有的SSL方法，在微调中平均提高了2.7-4.4%，在迁移学习到噪声数据集时最高提高了5.9%，并且与完全监督的基线相比取得了有竞争力的性能。我们蒸馏后的模型实现了91.4%的参数缩减和在边缘设备上3倍的推理速度提升，同时保持了有竞争力的准确率，从而能够在资源受限的场景中进行实际部署。

TLDR: The paper introduces ASMa, a self-supervised learning method for skeleton-based action recognition that uses asymmetric spatio-temporal masking to learn more robust representations, and demonstrates strong performance and efficient deployment capabilities.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了ASMa，一种用于基于骨骼的动作识别的自监督学习方法，该方法采用非对称时空掩蔽来学习更鲁棒的表示，并展示了强大的性能和高效的部署能力。

Authors: Aman Anand, Amir Eskandari, Elyas Rahsno, Farhana Zulkernine

Urban Spatio-Temporal Foundation Models for Climate-Resilient Housing: Scaling Diffusion Transformers for Disaster Risk Prediction

Abstract (English): Climate hazards increasingly disrupt urban transportation and emergency-response operations by damaging housing stock, degrading infrastructure, and reducing network accessibility. This paper presents Skjold-DiT, a diffusion-transformer framework that integrates heterogeneous spatio-temporal urban data to forecast building-level climate-risk indicators while explicitly incorporating transportation-network structure and accessibility signals relevant to intelligent vehicles (e.g., emergency reachability and evacuation-route constraints). Concretely, Skjold-DiT enables hazard-conditioned routing constraints by producing calibrated, uncertainty-aware accessibility layers (reachability, travel-time inflation, and route redundancy) that can be consumed by intelligent-vehicle routing and emergency dispatch systems. Skjold-DiT combines: (1) Fjell-Prompt, a prompt-based conditioning interface designed to support cross-city transfer; (2) Norrland-Fusion, a cross-modal attention mechanism unifying hazard maps/imagery, building attributes, demographics, and transportation infrastructure into a shared latent representation; and (3) Valkyrie-Forecast, a counterfactual simulator for generating probabilistic risk trajectories under intervention prompts. We introduce the Baltic-Caspian Urban Resilience (BCUR) dataset with 847,392 building-level observations across six cities, including multi-hazard annotations (e.g., flood and heat indicators) and transportation accessibility features. Experiments evaluate prediction quality, cross-city generalization, calibration, and downstream transportation-relevant outcomes, including reachability and hazard-conditioned travel times under counterfactual interventions.

摘要（中文）: 气候灾害日益扰乱城市交通和应急响应行动，具体表现为破坏房屋存量、降低基础设施质量以及降低网络可达性。本文提出 Skjold-DiT，一种扩散-Transformer框架，该框架整合了异构时空城市数据以预测建筑层面的气候风险指标，同时显式地纳入了与智能车辆相关的交通网络结构和可达性信号（例如，应急可达性和疏散路线约束）。具体而言，Skjold-DiT通过生成校准的、具有不确定性意识的可达性层（可达性、旅行时间膨胀和路线冗余）来实现灾害条件下的路径约束，这些可达性层可供智能车辆路径规划和紧急调度系统使用。Skjold-DiT结合了：（1）Fjell-Prompt，一种基于提示的条件接口，旨在支持跨城市迁移；（2）Norrland-Fusion，一种跨模态注意力机制，将灾害地图/图像、建筑属性、人口统计数据和交通基础设施统一到一个共享的潜在表示中；以及（3）Valkyrie-Forecast，一种反事实模拟器，用于生成干预提示下的概率风险轨迹。我们引入了波罗的海-里海城市韧性（BCUR）数据集，该数据集包含六个城市的 847,392 个建筑层面的观测数据，包括多灾害注释（例如，洪水和高温指标）以及交通可达性特征。实验评估了预测质量、跨城市泛化能力、校准以及下游与交通相关的结果，包括可达性和反事实干预下的灾害条件旅行时间。

Authors: Olaf Yunus Laitinen Imanov, Derya Umut Kulali, Taner Yilmaz

POPL-KF: A Pose-Only Geometric Representation-Based Kalman Filter for Point-Line-Based Visual-Inertial Odometry

Abstract (English): Mainstream Visual-inertial odometry (VIO) systems rely on point features for motion estimation and localization. However, their performance degrades in challenging scenarios. Moreover, the localization accuracy of multi-state constraint Kalman filter (MSCKF)-based VIO systems suffers from linearization errors associated with feature 3D coordinates and delayed measurement updates. To improve the performance of VIO in challenging scenes, we first propose a pose-only geometric representation for line features. Building on this, we develop POPL-KF, a Kalman filter-based VIO system that employs a pose-only geometric representation for both point and line features. POPL-KF mitigates linearization errors by explicitly eliminating both point and line feature coordinates from the measurement equations, while enabling immediate update of visual measurements. We also design a unified base-frames selection algorithm for both point and line features to ensure optimal constraints on camera poses within the pose-only measurement model. To further improve line feature quality, a line feature filter based on image grid segmentation and bidirectional optical flow consistency is proposed. Our system is evaluated on public datasets and real-world experiments, demonstrating that POPL-KF outperforms the state-of-the-art (SOTA) filter-based methods (OpenVINS, PO-KF) and optimization-based methods (PL-VINS, EPLF-VINS), while maintaining real-time performance.

摘要（中文）: 主流的视觉惯性里程计(VIO)系统依赖于点特征进行运动估计和定位。然而，它们在具有挑战性的场景中性能会下降。此外，基于多状态约束卡尔曼滤波器(MSCKF)的VIO系统的定位精度会受到与特征3D坐标和延迟测量更新相关的线性化误差的影响。为了提高VIO在具有挑战性场景中的性能，我们首先提出了一种仅姿态的几何表示用于线特征。在此基础上，我们开发了POPL-KF，一个基于卡尔曼滤波器的VIO系统，它采用仅姿态的几何表示用于点和线特征。POPL-KF通过显式消除测量方程中的点和线特征坐标来减轻线性化误差，同时能够立即更新视觉测量。我们还为点和线特征设计了一种统一的基帧选择算法，以确保仅姿态测量模型中相机姿态的最佳约束。为了进一步提高线特征质量，提出了一种基于图像网格分割和双向光流一致性的线特征滤波器。我们的系统在公共数据集和真实世界实验中进行了评估，结果表明POPL-KF优于最先进的（SOTA）基于滤波的方法（OpenVINS、PO-KF）和基于优化的方法（PL-VINS、EPLF-VINS），同时保持了实时性能。

TLDR: The paper presents POPL-KF, a novel Kalman filter-based VIO system that uses a pose-only geometric representation for both point and line features, improving accuracy and robustness in challenging environments compared to SOTA methods.

Authors: Aiping Wang, Zhaolong Yang, Shuwen Chen, Hai Zhang

MetaSSP: Enhancing Semi-supervised Implicit 3D Reconstruction through Meta-adaptive EMA and SDF-aware Pseudo-label Evaluation

Abstract (English): Implicit SDF-based methods for single-view 3D reconstruction achieve high-quality surfaces but require large labeled datasets, limiting their scalability. We propose MetaSSP, a novel semi-supervised framework that exploits abundant unlabeled images. Our approach introduces gradient-based parameter importance estimation to regularize adaptive EMA updates and an SDF-aware pseudo-label weighting mechanism combining augmentation consistency with SDF variance. Beginning with a 10% supervised warm-up, the unified pipeline jointly refines labeled and unlabeled data. On the Pix3D benchmark, our method reduces Chamfer Distance by approximately 20.61% and increases IoU by around 24.09% compared to existing semi-supervised baselines, setting a new state of the art.

TLDR: MetaSSP introduces a semi-supervised method for 3D reconstruction using implicit SDFs, achieving state-of-the-art results on Pix3D by leveraging unlabeled data with meta-adaptive EMA and SDF-aware pseudo-labeling.

Authors: Luoxi Zhang, Chun Xie, Itaru Kitahara

MambaVF: State Space Model for Efficient Video Fusion

Abstract (English): Video fusion is a fundamental technique in various video processing tasks. However, existing video fusion methods heavily rely on optical flow estimation and feature warping, resulting in severe computational overhead and limited scalability. This paper presents MambaVF, an efficient video fusion framework based on state space models (SSMs) that performs temporal modeling without explicit motion estimation. First, by reformulating video fusion as a sequential state update process, MambaVF captures long-range temporal dependencies with linear complexity while significantly reducing computation and memory costs. Second, MambaVF proposes a lightweight SSM-based fusion module that replaces conventional flow-guided alignment via a spatio-temporal bidirectional scanning mechanism. This module enables efficient information aggregation across frames. Extensive experiments across multiple benchmarks demonstrate that our MambaVF achieves state-of-the-art performance in multi-exposure, multi-focus, infrared-visible, and medical video fusion tasks. We highlight that MambaVF enjoys high efficiency, reducing up to 92.25% of parameters and 88.79% of computational FLOPs and a 2.1x speedup compared to existing methods. Project page: https://mambavf.github.io

摘要（中文）: 视频融合是各种视频处理任务中的一项基础技术。然而，现有的视频融合方法严重依赖光流估计和特征扭曲，导致严重的计算开销和有限的可扩展性。本文提出了一种高效的视频融合框架MambaVF，该框架基于状态空间模型(SSM)，可在没有显式运动估计的情况下执行时间建模。首先，通过将视频融合重新表述为一个连续的状态更新过程，MambaVF能够以线性复杂度捕获长距离时间依赖关系，同时显著降低计算和内存成本。其次，MambaVF提出了一种轻量级的基于SSM的融合模块，该模块通过时空双向扫描机制取代了传统的流引导对齐，从而能够高效地聚合跨帧信息。在多个基准测试上的大量实验表明，我们的MambaVF在多曝光、多焦点、红外-可见光和医学视频融合任务中均取得了最先进的性能。我们重点强调MambaVF具有很高的效率，与现有方法相比，参数量减少高达92.25%，计算量减少高达88.79%，速度提升2.1倍。项目主页：https://mambavf.github.io

Authors: Zixiang Zhao, Yukun Cui, Lilun Deng, Haowen Bai, Haotong Qin, Tao Feng, Konrad Schindler

Reinforcement Learning-Based Dynamic Management of Structured Parallel Farm Skeletons on Serverless Platforms

Abstract (English): We present a framework for dynamic management of structured parallel processing skeletons on serverless platforms. Our goal is to bring HPC-like performance and resilience to serverless and continuum environments while preserving the programmability benefits of skeletons. As a first step, we focus on the well known Farm pattern and its implementation on the open-source OpenFaaS platform, treating autoscaling of the worker pool as a QoS-aware resource management problem. The framework couples a reusable farm template with a Gymnasium-based monitoring and control layer that exposes queue, timing, and QoS metrics to both reactive and learning-based controllers. We investigate the effectiveness of AI-driven dynamic scaling for managing the farm's degree of parallelism via the scalability of serverless functions on OpenFaaS. In particular, we discuss the autoscaling model and its training, and evaluate two reinforcement learning (RL) policies against a baseline of reactive management derived from a simple farm performance model. Our results show that AI-based management can better accommodate platform-specific limitations than purely model-based performance steering, improving QoS while maintaining efficient resource usage and stable scaling behaviour.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了一种在Serverless平台上动态管理结构化并行处理骨架的框架。我们的目标是在Serverless和连续统环境中实现类HPC的性能和弹性，同时保留骨架的可编程性优势。作为第一步，我们专注于著名的Farm模式及其在开源OpenFaaS平台上的实现，将工作池的自动扩展视为一个具有服务质量感知（QoS-aware）的资源管理问题。该框架将一个可重用的Farm模板与一个基于Gymnasium的监控和控制层相结合，该层向反应式和基于学习的控制器暴露队列、时间和QoS指标。我们通过OpenFaaS上Serverless函数的可扩展性，研究了AI驱动的动态扩展在管理Farm并行度方面的有效性。特别地，我们讨论了自动扩展模型及其训练，并针对一个源自简单Farm性能模型的反应式管理基线，评估了两种强化学习（RL）策略。我们的结果表明，与纯粹基于模型的性能调优相比，基于AI的管理能够更好地适应平台特定的限制，在保持高效资源利用率和稳定扩展行为的同时，提高服务质量。

TLDR: This paper presents a reinforcement learning framework for dynamically managing parallel 'Farm' skeletons on serverless platforms like OpenFaaS to improve performance, resilience, and resource usage compared to reactive methods.

Authors: Lanpei Li, Massimo Coppola, Malio Li, Valerio Besozzi, Jack Bell, Vincenzo Lomonaco

Constraint Manifold Exploration for Efficient Continuous Coverage Estimation

Abstract (English): Many automated manufacturing processes rely on industrial robot arms to move process-specific tools along workpiece surfaces. In applications like grinding, sanding, spray painting, or inspection, they need to cover a workpiece fully while keeping their tools perpendicular to its surface. While there are approaches to generate trajectories for these applications, there are no sufficient methods for analyzing the feasibility of full surface coverage. This work proposes a sampling-based approach for continuous coverage estimation that explores reachable surface regions in the configuration space. We define an extended ambient configuration space that allows for the representation of tool position and orientation constraints. A continuation-based approach is used to explore it using two different sampling strategies. A thorough evaluation across different kinematics and environments analyzes their runtime and efficiency. This validates our ability to accurately and efficiently calculate surface coverage for complex surfaces in complicated environments.

摘要（中文）: 许多自动化制造过程依赖于工业机器人手臂，将特定工艺的工具沿着工件表面移动。在诸如研磨、打磨、喷漆或检测等应用中，它们需要完全覆盖工件表面，同时保持工具与其表面垂直。虽然存在生成这些应用轨迹的方法，但尚无充分的手段来分析表面完全覆盖的可行性。本文提出了一种基于采样的连续覆盖估计方法，该方法探索构型空间中可达的表面区域。我们定义了一个扩展的环境构型空间，允许表示工具的位置和姿态约束。采用基于连续化的方法，使用两种不同的采样策略来探索该空间。通过对不同运动学和环境的全面评估，分析了它们的运行时间和效率。这验证了我们能够准确高效地计算复杂环境中复杂表面的表面覆盖率。

TLDR: This paper introduces a sampling-based method to estimate continuous surface coverage for industrial robots, addressing the problem of feasibility analysis for full surface coverage in automated manufacturing.

Authors: Robert Wilbrandt, Rüdiger Dillmann

Feasible Static Workspace Optimization of Tendon Driven Continuum Robot based on Euclidean norm

Abstract (English): This paper focuses on the optimal design of a tendon-driven continuum robot (TDCR) based on its feasible static workspace (FSW). The TDCR under consideration is a two-segment robot driven by eight tendons, with four tendon actuators per segment. Tendon forces are treated as design variables, while the feasible static workspace (FSW) serves as the optimization objective. To determine the robot's feasible static workspace, a genetic algorithm optimization approach is employed to maximize a Euclidian norm of the TDCR's tip position over the workspace. During the simulations, the robot is subjected to external loads, including torques and forces. The results demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed method in identifying optimal tendon forces to maximize the feasible static workspace, even under the influence of external forces and torques.

摘要（中文）: 本文着重研究基于可行静态工作空间(FSW)的腱驱动连续体机器人(TDCR)的优化设计。所考虑的TDCR是一个由八根腱驱动的两段式机器人，每段由四个腱驱动器控制。腱力被视为设计变量，而可行静态工作空间(FSW)则作为优化目标。为了确定机器人的可行静态工作空间，采用遗传算法优化方法，以最大化TDCR末端位置在工作空间内的欧几里得范数。在仿真过程中，机器人受到包括扭矩和力在内的外部载荷作用。结果表明，即使在外部力和扭矩的作用下，所提出的方法也能有效地识别出最佳腱力，从而最大限度地扩大可行静态工作空间。

TLDR: This paper presents a method for optimizing the tendon forces of a tendon-driven continuum robot (TDCR) to maximize its feasible static workspace (FSW) using a genetic algorithm while considering external loads.

Authors: Mohammad Jabari, Carmen Visconte, Giuseppe Quaglia, Med Amine Laribi

A Consistency-Improved LiDAR-Inertial Bundle Adjustment

Abstract (English): Simultaneous Localization and Mapping (SLAM) using 3D LiDAR has emerged as a cornerstone for autonomous navigation in robotics. While feature-based SLAM systems have achieved impressive results by leveraging edge and planar structures, they often suffer from the inconsistent estimator associated with feature parameterization and estimated covariance. In this work, we present a consistency-improved LiDAR-inertial bundle adjustment (BA) with tailored parameterization and estimator. First, we propose a stereographic-projection representation parameterizing the planar and edge features, and conduct a comprehensive observability analysis to support its integrability with consistent estimator. Second, we implement a LiDAR-inertial BA with Maximum a Posteriori (MAP) formulation and First-Estimate Jacobians (FEJ) to preserve the accurate estimated covariance and observability properties of the system. Last, we apply our proposed BA method to a LiDAR-inertial odometry.

摘要（中文）: 使用3D激光雷达的同步定位与地图构建（SLAM）已成为机器人自主导航的基石。尽管基于特征的SLAM系统通过利用边缘和平面结构取得了令人瞩目的成果，但它们通常受到与特征参数化和估计协方差相关的不一致估计器的影响。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种一致性改进的激光雷达惯性捆绑调整（BA），采用了定制的参数化和估计器。首先，我们提出了一种用立体投影表示参数化平面和边缘特征的方法，并进行了全面的可观测性分析，以支持其与一致性估计器的可集成性。其次，我们采用最大后验（MAP）公式和首次估计雅可比矩阵（FEJ）来实现激光雷达惯性BA，以保留系统精确的估计协方差和可观测性属性。最后，我们将提出的BA方法应用于激光雷达惯性里程计。

TLDR: This paper introduces a consistency-improved LiDAR-inertial bundle adjustment method using stereographic-projection representation and First-Estimate Jacobians to address the inconsistent estimator problem in feature-based LiDAR SLAM.

Authors: Xinran Li, Shuaikang Zheng, Pengcheng Zheng, Xinyang Wang, Jiacheng Li, Zhitian Li, Xudong Zou

Bioinspired Kirigami Capsule Robot for Minimally Invasive Gastrointestinal Biopsy

Abstract (English): Wireless capsule endoscopy (WCE) has transformed gastrointestinal (GI) diagnostics by enabling noninvasive visualization of the digestive tract, yet its diagnostic yield remains constrained by the absence of biopsy capability, as histological analysis is still the gold standard for confirming disease. Conventional biopsy using forceps, needles, or rotating blades is invasive, limited in reach, and carries risks of perforation or mucosal trauma, while fluid- or microbiota-sampling capsules cannot provide structured tissue for pathology, leaving a critical gap in swallowable biopsy solutions. Here we present the Kiri-Capsule, a kirigami-inspired capsule robot that integrates deployable PI-film flaps actuated by a compact dual-cam mechanism to achieve minimally invasive and repeatable tissue collection. The kirigami surface remains flat during locomotion but transforms into sharp protrusions upon cam-driven stretching, enabling controlled penetration followed by rotary scraping, with specimens retained in internal fan-shaped cavities. Bench tests confirmed that PI films exhibit a Young's modulus of approximately 20 MPa and stable deployment angles (about 34$^\circ$ at 15% strain), while ex vivo porcine studies demonstrated shallow penetration depths (median $\sim$0.61 mm, range 0.46--0.66 mm) and biopsy yields comparable to standard forceps (mean $\sim$10.9 mg for stomach and $\sim$18.9 mg for intestine), with forces within safe ranges reported for GI biopsy. These findings demonstrate that the Kiri-Capsule bridges passive imaging and functional biopsy, providing a swallowable, depth-controlled, and histology-ready solution that advances capsule-based diagnostics toward safe and effective clinical application.

摘要（中文）: 无线胶囊内窥镜(WCE)通过实现消化道的无创可视化，革新了胃肠道(GI)诊断技术，但由于缺乏活检能力，其诊断率仍然受到限制，组织学分析仍然是确认疾病的金标准。 传统的利用钳子、针头或旋转刀片的活检方法具有侵入性，到达范围有限，并存在穿孔或黏膜损伤的风险，而液体或微生物群采样胶囊无法提供用于病理学的结构化组织，这在可吞咽活检解决方案中留下了一个关键空白。 在此，我们介绍了 Kiri-Capsule，一种受剪纸启发设计的胶囊机器人，它集成了可展开的 PI 薄膜翼片，由紧凑型双凸轮机构驱动，以实现微创且可重复的组织采集。 剪纸表面在运动过程中保持平坦，但在凸轮驱动的拉伸下转变为锋利的突起，从而实现可控的穿透，随后进行旋转刮取，并将样本保留在内部扇形腔体内。 台架试验证实，PI 薄膜的杨氏模量约为 20 MPa，且具有稳定的展开角度（在 15% 应变下约为 34$^\circ$），而离体猪研究表明其穿透深度较浅（中位数$\sim$0.61 mm，范围 0.46--0.66 mm），活检产量与标准活检钳相当（胃的平均值$\sim$10.9 mg，肠的平均值$\sim$18.9 mg），且作用力在胃肠道活检报告的安全范围内。 这些发现表明，Kiri-Capsule 连接了被动成像和功能性活检，提供了一种可吞咽、深度可控且可用于组织学分析的解决方案，从而推动了基于胶囊的诊断技术朝着安全有效的临床应用方向发展。

TLDR: The paper introduces a novel kirigami-inspired capsule robot (Kiri-Capsule) for minimally invasive gastrointestinal biopsy, offering a swallowable solution for tissue collection comparable to standard forceps but with depth control.

Authors: Ruizhou Zhao, Yichen Chu, Shuwei Zhao, Wenchao Yue, Raymond Shing-Yan Tang, Hongliang Ren

Orientation-Robust Latent Motion Trajectory Learning for Annotation-free Cardiac Phase Detection in Fetal Echocardiography

Abstract (English): Fetal echocardiography is essential for detecting congenital heart disease (CHD), facilitating pregnancy management, optimized delivery planning, and timely postnatal interventions. Among standard imaging planes, the four-chamber (4CH) view provides comprehensive information for CHD diagnosis, where clinicians carefully inspect the end-diastolic (ED) and end-systolic (ES) phases to evaluate cardiac structure and motion. Automated detection of these cardiac phases is thus a critical component toward fully automated CHD analysis. Yet, in the absence of fetal electrocardiography (ECG), manual identification of ED and ES frames remains a labor-intensive bottleneck. We present ORBIT (Orientation-Robust Beat Inference from Trajectories), a self-supervised framework that identifies cardiac phases without manual annotations under various fetal heart orientation. ORBIT employs registration as self-supervision task and learns a latent motion trajectory of cardiac deformation, whose turning points capture transitions between cardiac relaxation and contraction, enabling accurate and orientation-robust localization of ED and ES frames across diverse fetal positions. Trained exclusively on normal fetal echocardiography videos, ORBIT achieves consistent performance on both normal (MAE = 1.9 frames for ED and 1.6 for ES) and CHD cases (MAE = 2.4 frames for ED and 2.1 for ES), outperforming existing annotation-free approaches constrained by fixed orientation assumptions. These results highlight the potential of ORBIT to facilitate robust cardiac phase detection directly from 4CH fetal echocardiography.

摘要（中文）: 胎儿超声心动图对于检测先天性心脏病（CHD）至关重要，有助于妊娠管理、优化分娩计划以及及时进行产后干预。在标准成像切面中，四腔心（4CH）切面为CHD诊断提供全面的信息，临床医生会仔细检查舒张末期（ED）和收缩末期（ES）阶段，以评估心脏结构和运动。因此，自动检测这些心脏相位是实现全自动CHD分析的关键组成部分。然而，在缺乏胎儿心电图（ECG）的情况下，手动识别ED和ES帧仍然是一项劳动密集型的瓶颈。我们提出ORBIT（基于轨迹的方向鲁棒搏动推断），这是一个自监督框架，可在各种胎儿心脏方向下识别心脏相位，而无需手动标注。ORBIT采用配准作为自监督任务，并学习心脏变形的潜在运动轨迹，其转折点捕捉心脏松弛和收缩之间的过渡，从而能够在不同的胎儿位置实现ED和ES帧的精确且方向鲁棒的定位。ORBIT仅在正常的胎儿超声心动图视频上进行训练，在正常（ED的MAE = 1.9帧，ES的MAE = 1.6帧）和CHD病例（ED的MAE = 2.4帧，ES的MAE = 2.1帧）上均实现了稳定性能，优于现有受固定方向假设限制的无标注方法。这些结果突显了ORBIT直接从4CH胎儿超声心动图促进稳健的心脏相位检测的潜力。

TLDR: This paper introduces ORBIT, a self-supervised framework for annotation-free cardiac phase detection in fetal echocardiography, achieving orientation-robust and accurate localization of end-diastolic and end-systolic frames for both normal and CHD cases.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为ORBIT的自监督框架，用于在胎儿超声心动图中进行免注释的心脏相位检测。该框架实现了对心脏舒张末期和收缩末期帧的 Orientierungs-Robust 及精确定位，适用于正常和先天性心脏病 (CHD) 病例。

Authors: Yingyu Yang, Qianye Yang, Can Peng, Elena D'Alberti, Olga Patey, Aris T. Papageorghiou, J. Alison Noble

Clinical-Prior Guided Multi-Modal Learning with Latent Attention Pooling for Gait-Based Scoliosis Screening

Abstract (English): Adolescent Idiopathic Scoliosis (AIS) is a prevalent spinal deformity whose progression can be mitigated through early detection. Conventional screening methods are often subjective, difficult to scale, and reliant on specialized clinical expertise. Video-based gait analysis offers a promising alternative, but current datasets and methods frequently suffer from data leakage, where performance is inflated by repeated clips from the same individual, or employ oversimplified models that lack clinical interpretability. To address these limitations, we introduce ScoliGait, a new benchmark dataset comprising 1,572 gait video clips for training and 300 fully independent clips for testing. Each clip is annotated with radiographic Cobb angles and descriptive text based on clinical kinematic priors. We propose a multi-modal framework that integrates a clinical-prior-guided kinematic knowledge map for interpretable feature representation, alongside a latent attention pooling mechanism to fuse video, text, and knowledge map modalities. Our method establishes a new state-of-the-art, demonstrating a significant performance gap on a realistic, non-repeating subject benchmark. Our approach establishes a new state of the art, showing a significant performance gain on a realistic, subject-independent benchmark. This work provides a robust, interpretable, and clinically grounded foundation for scalable, non-invasive AIS assessment.

摘要（中文）: 青少年特发性脊柱侧弯 (AIS) 是一种常见的脊柱畸形，通过早期检测可以减轻其进展。传统的筛查方法通常具有主观性、难以规模化，且依赖于专业的临床知识。基于视频的步态分析提供了一种有前景的替代方案，但当前的数据集和方法通常存在数据泄露问题，同一受试者的重复片段会虚增性能，或者采用过于简化的模型，缺乏临床可解释性。为了解决这些局限性，我们引入 ScoliGait，这是一个新的benchmark数据集，包含 1,572 个用于训练的步态视频片段和 300 个完全独立的用于测试的片段。每个片段都标注了放射科 Cobb 角和基于临床运动学先验的描述性文本。我们提出了一种多模态框架，该框架集成了临床先验指导的运动学知识图谱以实现可解释的特征表示，以及一个潜在注意力池化机制来融合视频、文本和知识图谱模态。我们的方法建立了一个新的最先进水平，在真实的、非重复受试者的基准测试中表现出显著的性能提升。这项工作为可扩展的、非侵入性的 AIS 评估提供了稳健、可解释且具有临床基础的基础。

TLDR: The paper introduces ScoliGait, a new benchmark dataset and multi-modal framework for gait-based scoliosis screening, addressing data leakage issues and improving clinical interpretability with a clinical-prior-guided knowledge map.

Authors: Dong Chen, Zizhuang Wei, Jialei Xu, Xinyang Sun, Zonglin He, Meiru An, Huili Peng, Yong Hu, Kenneth MC Cheung

A Fast and Generalizable Fourier Neural Operator-Based Surrogate for Melt-Pool Prediction in Laser Processing

Abstract (English): High-fidelity simulations of laser welding capture complex thermo-fluid phenomena, including phase change, free-surface deformation, and keyhole dynamics, however their computational cost limits large-scale process exploration and real-time use. In this work we present the Laser Processing Fourier Neural Operator (LP-FNO), a Fourier Neural Operator (FNO) based surrogate model that learns the parametric solution operator of various laser processes from multiphysics simulations generated with FLOW-3D WELD (registered trademark). Through a novel approach of reformulating the transient problem in the moving laser frame and applying temporal averaging, the system results in a quasi-steady state setting suitable for operator learning, even in the keyhole welding regime. The proposed LP-FNO maps process parameters to three-dimensional temperature fields and melt-pool boundaries across a broad process window spanning conduction and keyhole regimes using the non-dimensional normalized enthalpy formulation. The model achieves temperature prediction errors on the order of 1% and intersection-over-union scores for melt-pool segmentation over 0.9. We demonstrate that a LP-FNO model trained on coarse-resolution data can be evaluated on finer grids, yielding accurate super-resolved predictions in mesh-converged conduction regimes, whereas discrepancies in keyhole regimes reflect unresolved dynamics in the coarse-mesh training data. These results indicate that the LP-FNO provides an efficient surrogate modeling framework for laser welding, enabling prediction of full three-dimensional fields and phase interfaces over wide parameter ranges in just tens of milliseconds, up to a hundred thousand times faster than traditional Finite Volume multi-physics software.

摘要（中文）: 激光焊接的高保真模拟能够捕捉复杂的热流体现象，包括相变、自由表面变形和匙孔动力学，但其计算成本限制了大规模工艺探索和实时应用。本文提出了一种激光加工傅里叶神经算子（LP-FNO），这是一种基于傅里叶神经算子（FNO）的替代模型，它从用FLOW-3D WELD（注册商标）生成的多物理场模拟中学习各种激光工艺的参数化解算子。通过一种新颖的方法，在移动激光坐标系中重新表述瞬态问题并应用时间平均，该系统产生了一种适用于算子学习的准稳态设置，即使在匙孔焊接状态下也是如此。所提出的LP-FNO使用无量纲归一化焓公式，将工艺参数映射到跨越传导和匙孔状态的广泛工艺窗口中的三维温度场和熔池边界。该模型实现的温度预测误差约为1%，熔池分割的交并比得分超过0.9。我们证明了在粗分辨率数据上训练的LP-FNO模型可以在更精细的网格上进行评估，从而在网格收敛的传导状态下产生准确的超分辨率预测，而在匙孔状态下的差异反映了粗网格训练数据中未解析的动力学。这些结果表明，LP-FNO为激光焊接提供了一个高效的替代建模框架，能够在短短几十毫秒内预测宽参数范围内的完整三维场和相界面，比传统的有限体积多物理场软件快达十万倍。

TLDR: This paper introduces a Fourier Neural Operator (LP-FNO) based surrogate model for fast and accurate melt-pool prediction in laser welding, achieving significant speedups compared to traditional simulations.

Authors: Alix Benoit, Toni Ivas, Mateusz Papierz, Asel Sagingalieva, Alexey Melnikov, Elia Iseli

A Hybrid Data-Driven Algorithm for Real-Time Friction Force Estimation in Hydraulic Cylinders

Abstract (English): Hydraulic systems are widely utilized in industrial applications due to their high force generation, precise control, and ability to function in harsh environments. Hydraulic cylinders, as actuators in these systems, apply force and position through the displacement of hydraulic fluid, but their operation is significantly influenced by friction force. Achieving precision in hydraulic cylinders requires an accurate friction model under various operating conditions. Existing analytical models, often derived from experimental tests, necessitate the identification or estimation of influencing factors but are limited in adaptability and computational efficiency. This research introduces a data-driven, hybrid algorithm based on Long Short-Term Memory (LSTM) networks and Random Forests for nonlinear friction force estimation. The algorithm effectively combines feature detection and estimation processes using training data acquired from an experimental hydraulic test setup. It achieves a consistent and stable model error of less than 10% across diverse operating conditions and external load variations, ensuring robust performance in complex situations. The computational cost of the algorithm is 1.51 milliseconds per estimation, making it suitable for real-time applications. The proposed method addresses the limitations of analytical models by delivering high precision and computational efficiency. The algorithm's performance is validated through detailed analysis and experimental results, including direct comparisons with the LuGre model. The comparison highlights that while the LuGre model offers a theoretical foundation for friction modeling, its performance is limited by its inability to dynamically adjust to varying operational conditions of the hydraulic cylinder, further emphasizing the advantages of the proposed hybrid approach in real-time applications.

摘要（中文）: 液压系统因其高力生成、精确控制以及在恶劣环境中工作的能力而被广泛应用于工业领域。液压缸作为这些系统中的执行器，通过液压流体的位移来施加力和定位，但其运行受摩擦力的显著影响。在液压缸中实现精度需要一种在各种工况下准确的摩擦模型。现有的分析模型通常从实验测试中推导出，需要识别或估计影响因素，但在适应性和计算效率方面受到限制。本研究引入了一种基于长短期记忆（LSTM）网络和随机森林的用于非线性摩擦力估计的数据驱动混合算法。该算法有效地结合了特征检测和估计过程，利用从实验性液压测试装置获取的训练数据。它在各种工况和外部载荷变化下实现了低于10%的一致且稳定的模型误差，确保了在复杂情况下的鲁棒性能。该算法的计算成本为每次估计1.51毫秒，使其适用于实时应用。所提出的方法通过提供高精度和计算效率，解决了分析模型的局限性。该算法的性能通过详细分析和实验结果进行验证，包括与LuGre模型的直接比较。比较结果表明，虽然LuGre模型为摩擦建模提供了理论基础，但其性能受到无法动态调整液压缸各种工况的限制，进一步强调了所提出的混合方法在实时应用中的优势。

TLDR: This paper introduces a hybrid LSTM and Random Forest data-driven algorithm for real-time friction force estimation in hydraulic cylinders, demonstrating improved accuracy and computational efficiency compared to the LuGre model.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种混合LSTM和随机森林的数据驱动算法，用于液压缸中的实时摩擦力估计，与LuGre模型相比，该算法具有更高的精度和计算效率。

Authors: Mohamad Amin Jamshidi, Mehrbod Zarifi, Zolfa Anvari, Hamed Ghafarirad, Mohammad Zareinejad

Optimization of an Augmented R-CUBE mechanism for Cervical Surgery

Abstract (English): In some surgical operations targeting the spine, it is required to drill cavities in the vertebrae for the insertion of pedicle screws. A new mechanical architecture is proposed for this application. It is based on an augmented version of the full translational R-CUBE mechanism, with improved linkages to implement additional rotational motion. Using this concept, a mechanism presented with a 3T2R motion that is required for the manipulation of the surgical drill. It is mainly composed three stages: one translational, one transmitting and one rotational. Their respective kinematic and velocity models are separately derived, then combined. Based on the drilling trajectories obtained from a real patient case, the mechanism is optimized for generating the highest kinematic performances.

摘要（中文）: 在一些针对脊柱的外科手术中，需要在椎骨上钻孔以便植入椎弓根螺钉。针对此应用，本文提出了一种新的机械结构。该结构基于完整的平移R-CUBE机构的增强版本，并改进了连杆机构以实现额外的旋转运动。基于此概念，提出了一种具有3T2R运动机构，该运动对于外科手术钻的操作至关重要。该机构主要由三个阶段组成：一个是平移阶段，一个是传递阶段，一个是旋转阶段。分别推导了它们各自的运动学和速度模型，然后将其组合。基于从真实患者病例中获得的钻孔轨迹，对该机构进行了优化，以产生最高的运动学性能。

TLDR: The paper proposes an augmented R-CUBE mechanism for cervical surgery, specifically for drilling cavities in vertebrae. It focuses on kinematic modeling and optimization for real patient case trajectories.

Authors: Terence Essomba, Yu-Wen Wu, Abdelbadia Chaker, Med Amine Laribi

A novel Integrated Motion Tracking Device (IMTD) for Objective Laparoscopic Training Assessment: Development and Validation

Abstract (English): This paper presents a novel, compact four-degree-of-freedom motion-tracking device (IMTD) designed for training and evaluation in laparoscopic surgery. The device's kinematics, mechanical design, instrumentation, and prototypes are developed and presented to meet the specific requirements of laparoscopic training context, including movement around a fixed center of motion and seamless integration into standard box trainers. The system IMTD's tracking accuracy and reliability are compared to a motion capture system (MoCap), assessing its ability to capture both angular and translational motions of surgical instruments. The study then focuses on key performance parameters including precision, fluidity, speed, and overall motion efficiency. The results highlight the system's effectiveness in tracking surgical gestures, providing valuable insights into its potential as a tool for training and performance evaluation in minimally invasive surgery. Additionally, IMTD's low cost and integrated design allow for easy integration and implementation in training rooms, offering a practical and accessible solution for general use. By offering objective, real-time feedback, the system can significantly contribute to improving surgical skills and shortening the learning curve for novice students, while also providing a foundation for future development of gesture scoring algorithms and standardized training protocols.

摘要（中文）: 本文提出了一种新型紧凑型四自由度运动跟踪装置（IMTD），专为腹腔镜手术的训练和评估而设计。针对腹腔镜训练环境的特殊要求，包括围绕固定运动中心的运动以及与标准箱式训练器的无缝集成，本文对该装置的运动学、机械设计、仪器仪表和原型进行了开发和展示。将该IMTD系统的跟踪精度和可靠性与运动捕捉系统（MoCap）进行比较，评估其捕捉手术器械角度和线性运动的能力。随后，研究重点关注关键性能参数，包括精度、流畅性、速度和整体运动效率。结果表明，该系统能有效跟踪手术动作，为将其作为微创手术训练和性能评估工具提供了有价值的见解。此外，IMTD的低成本和集成设计使其易于集成和部署在训练室中，为通用提供了一种实用且易于使用的解决方案。通过提供客观的实时反馈，该系统可以显著提高手术技能，缩短新手学生的学习曲线，同时为未来手势评分算法和标准化培训协议的开发奠定基础。

TLDR: The paper presents a novel integrated motion tracking device (IMTD) for objective assessment in laparoscopic surgical training, demonstrating its accuracy and potential for improving surgical skills through real-time feedback.

Authors: Siwar Bouzid, Abdelbadia Chaker, Marc Arsicault, Sami Bennour, Med Amine Laribi

Primary Experimental Feedback on a Co-manipulated Robotic System for Assisted Cervical Surgery

Abstract (English): Robotic-assisted surgery has emerged as a promising approach to improve surgical ergonomics, precision, and workflow efficiency, particularly in complex procedures such as cervical spine surgery. In this study, we evaluate the performance of a collaborative robotic system designed to assist surgeons in drilling tasks by assessing its accuracy in executing predefined trajectories. A total of 14 drillings were performed by eight experienced cervical surgeons, utilizing a robotic-assisted setup aimed at ensuring stability and alignment. The primary objective of this study is to quantify the deviations in the position and orientation of the drilling tool relative to the planned trajectory, providing insights into the system's reliability and potential impact on clinical outcomes. While the primary function of robotic assistance in surgery is to enhance surgeon comfort and procedural guidance rather than solely optimizing precision, understanding the system's accuracy remains crucial for its effective integration into surgical practices part of this primary experimental feedback, the study offers an in-depth analysis of the co-manipulated robotic system's performance, focusing on the experimental setup and error evaluation methods. The findings of this study will contribute to the ongoing development of robotic-assisted cervical surgery, highlighting both its advantages and areas for improvement in achieving safer and more efficient surgical workflows

摘要（中文）: 机器人辅助手术已成为一种有前景的方法，可以提高手术的人体工程学、精确度和工作流程效率，尤其是在颈椎手术等复杂手术中。在本研究中，我们评估了一种协作机器人系统的性能，该系统旨在通过评估其执行预定义轨迹的准确性来辅助外科医生进行钻孔任务。共有八位经验丰富的颈椎外科医生进行了14次钻孔，他们使用了一种机器人辅助装置，旨在确保稳定性和对齐。本研究的主要目标是量化钻孔工具相对于计划轨迹的位置和方向的偏差，从而深入了解系统的可靠性以及对临床结果的潜在影响。虽然机器人辅助手术的主要功能是增强外科医生的舒适度和程序指导，而不是仅仅优化精度，但了解系统的准确性对于其有效整合到外科实践中仍然至关重要。作为主要实验反馈的一部分，该研究提供了对共操控机器人系统性能的深入分析，重点关注实验设置和误差评估方法。本研究的结果将有助于机器人辅助颈椎手术的持续发展，突出其优势以及在实现更安全、更高效的手术工作流程方面需要改进的领域。

Authors: Seifeddine Sellemi, Abdelbadia Chaker, Tanguy Vendeuvre, Terence Essomba, Med Amine Laribi

Location-Aware Dispersion on Anonymous Graphs

Abstract (English): The well-studied DISPERSION problem is a fundamental coordination problem in distributed robotics, where a set of mobile robots must relocate so that each occupies a distinct node of a network. DISPERSION assumes that a robot can settle at any node as long as no other robot settles on that node. In this work, we introduce LOCATION-AWARE DISPERSION, a novel generalization of DISPERSION that incorporates location awareness: Let $G = (V, E)$ be an anonymous, connected, undirected graph with $n = |V|$ nodes, each labeled with a color $\sf{col}(v) \in C = \{c_1, \dots, c_t\}, t\leq n$. A set $R = \{r_1, \dots, r_k\}$ of $k \leq n$ mobile robots is given, where each robot $r_i$ has an associated color $\mathsf{col}(r_i) \in C$. Initially placed arbitrarily on the graph, the goal is to relocate the robots so that each occupies a distinct node of the same color. When $|C|=1$, LOCATION-AWARE DISPERSION reduces to DISPERSION. There is a solution to DISPERSION in graphs with any $k\leq n$ without knowing $k,n$. Like DISPERSION, the goal is to solve LOCATION-AWARE DISPERSION minimizing both time and memory requirement at each agent. We develop several deterministic algorithms with guaranteed bounds on both time and memory requirement. We also give an impossibility and a lower bound for any deterministic algorithm for LOCATION-AWARE DISPERSION. To the best of our knowledge, the presented results collectively establish the algorithmic feasibility of LOCATION-AWARE DISPERSION in anonymous networks and also highlight the challenges on getting an efficient solution compared to the solutions for DISPERSION.

摘要（中文）: 分散问题（DISPERSION）是分布式机器人领域中一个被广泛研究的基础协调问题，其中一组移动机器人必须重新定位，使得每个机器人占据网络中一个不同的节点。分散问题假设机器人可以停留在任何节点上，只要没有其他机器人停留在该节点上。 在本工作中，我们引入了位置感知分散问题（LOCATION-AWARE DISPERSION），这是分散问题的一种新颖推广，它结合了位置感知能力：设 $G = (V, E)$ 是一个匿名、连通、无向图，其中 $n = |V|$ 个节点，每个节点被标记为一种颜色 $\sf{col}(v) \in C = \{c_1, \dots, c_t\}, t\leq n$。给定一组 $R = \{r_1, \dots, r_k\}$ 共 $k \leq n$ 个移动机器人，其中每个机器人 $r_i$ 具有相关联的颜色 $\mathsf{col}(r_i) \in C$。初始时，机器人任意放置在图上，目标是重新定位这些机器人，使得每个机器人占据一个相同颜色的不同节点。当 $|C|=1$ 时，位置感知分散问题退化为分散问题。在任何 $k\leq n$ 的图上，分散问题都存在解，且无需知道 $k,n$。 与分散问题类似，位置感知分散问题的目标是在最小化每个代理所需的时间和存储需求的前提下求解。我们开发了几种具有时间和存储需求保证界限的确定性算法。 我们还给出了位置感知分散问题的任何确定性算法的不可能性和下界。据我们所知，目前的结果共同证明了在匿名网络中位置感知分散问题的算法可行性，并且突出了相对于分散问题的现有解决方案而言，获得有效解决方案所面临的挑战。

TLDR: The paper introduces a novel generalization of the DISPERSION problem called LOCATION-AWARE DISPERSION, where robots with distinct colors must relocate to distinct nodes of the same color on an anonymous graph, and provides algorithms, impossibility results, and lower bounds.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种新的DISPERSION问题泛化，称为LOCATION-AWARE DISPERSION，其中具有不同颜色的机器人必须重新定位到匿名图上相同颜色的不同节点，并提供了算法、否定性结果和下界。

Authors: Himani, Supantha Pandit, Gokarna Sharma

Unsupervised MR-US Multimodal Image Registration with Multilevel Correlation Pyramidal Optimization

Abstract (English): Surgical navigation based on multimodal image registration has played a significant role in providing intraoperative guidance to surgeons by showing the relative position of the target area to critical anatomical structures during surgery. However, due to the differences between multimodal images and intraoperative image deformation caused by tissue displacement and removal during the surgery, effective registration of preoperative and intraoperative multimodal images faces significant challenges. To address the multimodal image registration challenges in Learn2Reg 2025, an unsupervised multimodal medical image registration method based on Multilevel Correlation Pyramidal Optimization (MCPO) is designed to solve these problems. First, the features of each modality are extracted based on the modality independent neighborhood descriptor, and the multimodal images is mapped to the feature space. Second, a multilevel pyramidal fusion optimization mechanism is designed to achieve global optimization and local detail complementation of the displacement field through dense correlation analysis and weight-balanced coupled convex optimization for input features at different scales. Our method focuses on the ReMIND2Reg task in Learn2Reg 2025. Based on the results, our method achieved the first place in the validation phase and test phase of ReMIND2Reg. The MCPO is also validated on the Resect dataset, achieving an average TRE of 1.798 mm. This demonstrates the broad applicability of our method in preoperative-to-intraoperative image registration. The code is available at https://github.com/wjiazheng/MCPO.

摘要（中文）: 基于多模态图像配准的手术导航在术中为外科医生提供指导方面发挥了重要作用，它能够显示目标区域与关键解剖结构在手术中的相对位置。然而，由于多模态图像之间的差异以及手术过程中组织移位和切除造成的术中图像形变，术前和术中多模态图像的有效配准面临着重大挑战。 为解决Learn2Reg 2025中多模态图像配准的挑战，我们设计了一种基于多层相关金字塔优化的（MCPO）的无监督多模态医学图像配准方法来解决这些问题。首先，基于模态独立的邻域描述符提取每种模态的特征，并将多模态图像映射到特征空间。其次，设计了一种多层金字塔融合优化机制，通过对不同尺度输入特征进行密集相关性分析和权重平衡的耦合凸优化，实现位移场的全局优化和局部细节补充。我们的方法主要关注Learn2Reg 2025中的ReMIND2Reg任务。根据结果显示，我们的方法在ReMIND2Reg的验证阶段和测试阶段均取得了第一名。MCPO还在Resect数据集上进行了验证，实现了1.798毫米的平均目标配准误差（TRE）。这证明了我们的方法在术前到术中图像配准中的广泛适用性。代码可在https://github.com/wjiazheng/MCPO获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces an unsupervised multimodal medical image registration method called Multilevel Correlation Pyramidal Optimization (MCPO) that placed first in the Learn2Reg 2025 ReMIND2Reg challenge, demonstrating strong performance in preoperative-to-intraoperative image registration.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为多级相关金字塔优化（MCPO）的无监督多模态医学图像配准方法，该方法在Learn2Reg 2025 ReMIND2Reg挑战赛中名列第一，展示了术前到术中图像配准的强大性能。

Authors: Jiazheng Wang, Zeyu Liu, Min Liu, Xiang Chen, Xinyao Yu, Yaonan Wang, Hang Zhang

Topography scanning as a part of process monitoring in power cable insulation process

Abstract (English): We present a novel topography scanning system developed to XLPE cable core monitoring. Modern measurement technology is utilized together with embedded high-performance computing to build a complete and detailed 3D surface map of the insulated core. Cross sectional and lengthwise geometry errors are studied, and melt homogeneity is identified as one major factor for these errors. A surface defect detection system has been developed utilizing deep learning methods. Our results show that convolutional neural networks are well suited for real time analysis of surface measurement data enabling reliable detection of surface defects.

摘要（中文）: 我们提出了一种新型地形扫描系统，用于XLPE电缆芯线监测。该系统利用现代测量技术与嵌入式高性能计算相结合，构建绝缘芯线的完整而详细的3D表面图。我们研究了横截面和长度方向上的几何误差，并将熔体均质性确定为这些误差的主要因素之一。同时，开发了一种利用深度学习方法的表面缺陷检测系统。我们的结果表明，卷积神经网络非常适合表面测量数据的实时分析，从而能够可靠地检测表面缺陷。

TLDR: This paper introduces a topography scanning system for real-time defect detection in XLPE cable core insulation using deep learning, specifically convolutional neural networks. The system aims to build detailed 3D surface maps and identify geometry errors and surface defects.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种地形扫描系统，该系统使用深度学习（特别是卷积神经网络）实时检测XLPE电缆芯绝缘层中的缺陷。该系统旨在构建详细的3D表面图，并识别几何误差和表面缺陷。
